</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>You see? It was a name I was already using at Hogwarts, to my most intimate friends only, of course. You think I was going to use my filthy Muggle father’s name forever? I, in whose veins runs the blood of Salazar Slytherin himself, through my mother’s side? I, keep the name of a foul, common Muggle, who abandoned me even before I was born, just because he found out his wife was a witch? No, Harry. I fashioned myself a new name, a name I knew wizards everywhere would one day fear to speak, when I had become the greatest sorcerer in the world!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Tom Riddle's transformation into Lord Voldemort<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p><b>Tom Marvolo Riddle</b> (<a href="/wiki/31_December" title="31 December">31 December</a> <a href="/wiki/1926" title="1926">1926</a><sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> – <a href="/wiki/2_May" title="2 May">2 May</a> <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>), later known as <b>Lord Voldemort</b> or, alternatively as <b>You-Know-Who</b>, <b>He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named</b>, or the <b>Dark Lord</b>, was an <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a> <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a><sup id="cite_ref-blood_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-blood-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> considered to have been the most powerful and dangerous <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizard</a> of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-dangerous_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dangerous-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> He was amongst the greatest wizards to have ever lived, often considered to be the second most powerful wizard in history, his only superior being <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>. The only child and son of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle_Senior" title="Tom Riddle Senior">Tom</a> and <a href="/wiki/Merope_Riddle" title="Merope Riddle">Merope Riddle</a> <span class="template-c">(née <a href="/wiki/House_of_Gaunt" title="House of Gaunt">Gaunt</a>)</span>, Riddle was raised in the Muggle-run <a href="/wiki/Wool%27s_Orphanage" title="Wool&#39;s Orphanage">Wool's Orphanage</a> after his father abandoned his new family on the streets of <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> when the potion's influence was lifted, and his mother died moments after giving birth to and naming him after his father and maternal grandfather, <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt" title="Marvolo Gaunt">Marvolo Gaunt</a>.  
</p><p>Riddle began attending <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> in <a href="/wiki/1938" title="1938">1938</a> and was sorted into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> house. Some of his early activities included the opening of <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> and the use of its <a href="/wiki/Serpent_of_Slytherin" title="Serpent of Slytherin">monster</a> to attack <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> students; several months' service as a purchasing agent for the Dark artefacts shop <a href="/wiki/Borgin_and_Burkes" title="Borgin and Burkes">Borgin and Burkes</a>; use of the ability to speak <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parseltongue</a>; and the attainment of <a href="/wiki/Immortality" title="Immortality">immortality</a> between the years of <a href="/wiki/1943" title="1943">1943</a> and <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, a process begun upon the creation of his first <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> at the age of sixteen.  
</p><p>Splitting his own spirit into a total of eight fragments, Riddle created seven Horcruxes, one unintentionally and without his knowledge — <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. Abandoning his 'Muggle' name, he became the self-proclaimed Lord Voldemort, which was an anagram of his birth name. He commanded <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">a veritable army of wizards and Dark creatures</a>, committed countless murders and atrocities personally and through his followers, and on one occasion nearly succeeded and on a later occasion did succeed in taking over the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>, installing a puppet Minister, <a href="/wiki/Pius_Thicknesse" title="Pius Thicknesse">Pius Thicknesse</a>, who was controlled with the <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a>. 
</p><p>Voldemort was ripped from his body in <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a> after attempting to kill Harry and, though unable to die, was not able to regain a permanent and physical body until 1995, thus spending the intervening fourteen years "<i>a shell, less than the meanest ghost</i>", but alive. He was finally killed by his own backfiring curse after Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter, following Dumbledore's death, succeeded in destroying all of his Horcruxes.  
</p><p>Unknown to most, however, Voldemort's legacy and bloodline would live on through his daughter <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a>, whom he conceived with his loyal follower <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>; sometime after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a> and before Voldemort's death at the hands of Harry in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>. 
</p><p>Riddle's broken and mutilated soul was then trapped in <a href="/wiki/Limbo" title="Limbo">Limbo</a> for eternity, unable to move on to the afterlife or even return as a <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">disembodied spirit</a>. 
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=1" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Biography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Biography"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family_lineage">Family lineage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=2" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Family lineage">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Family lineage"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>The Gaunts, a very ancient wizarding family noted for a vein of instability and violence that flourished through the generations due to their habit of marrying their own cousins.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Description of the House of Gaunt<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 172px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/86/Salazar_Slytherin_WWHP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140615154545" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="170" height="278" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Salazar Slytherin WWHP.jpg" data-image-key="Salazar_Slytherin_WWHP.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/86/Salazar_Slytherin_WWHP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20140615154545" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/86/Salazar_Slytherin_WWHP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140615154545" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/86/Salazar_Slytherin_WWHP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20140615154545" decoding="async" width="170" height="278" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Salazar Slytherin WWHP.jpg" data-image-key="Salazar_Slytherin_WWHP.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/86/Salazar_Slytherin_WWHP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20140615154545" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Salazar_Slytherin_WWHP.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a>, Voldemort's maternal ancestor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>By <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>'s time, Tom's family on his mother <a href="/wiki/Merope_Riddle" title="Merope Riddle">Merope</a>'s side were the last known members of the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Gaunt" title="House of Gaunt">House of Gaunt</a>. The Gaunts were an ancient, and formerly wealthy, wizarding family, noted for producing individuals with violent and unstable personalities due to generations of <a href="/wiki/Inbreeding" title="Inbreeding">inbreeding</a>.
</p><p>Previous, named members of the Gaunt family — Tom's distant relatives — included <a href="/wiki/Corvinus_Gaunt" title="Corvinus Gaunt">Corvinus Gaunt</a>, Tom's maternal ancestor, and a <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parselmouth</a> who hid the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> entrance in a girls' restroom at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>; <a href="/wiki/Rionach_Sayre" title="Rionach Sayre">Rionach Gaunt</a>, the mother of <a href="/wiki/Ilvermorny_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Ilvermorny School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Ilvermorny</a> founder <a href="/wiki/Isolt_Sayre" title="Isolt Sayre">Isolt Sayre</a>; and <a href="/wiki/Gormlaith_Gaunt" title="Gormlaith Gaunt">Gormlaith Gaunt</a>, the sister of Rionach; maternal aunt of Sayre; maternal great-aunt of <a href="/wiki/Rionach_Steward" title="Rionach Steward">Rionach Steward</a> and <a href="/wiki/Martha_Steward" title="Martha Steward">Martha Steward</a>; and, it is believed, the "last of the Irish branch of the Gaunt family".
</p><p>Because of the Gaunt family's liking for grandeur, along with little sensibility at their indulgences, the family gold was gambled away and gone long before the last known heirs of the lineage were born. Likewise, a tendency to "marry their own cousins" to "keep their bloodline pure", following the beliefs of their ancestor <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a>, caused the heirs to the Gaunt name to suffer the ill-effects of generations of inbreeding and incest.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/North_America" title="North America">North America</a>, in what would later become the state of <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts" title="Massachusetts">Massachusetts</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_of_America" title="United States of America">United States</a>, the descendants of the Irish branch of the Gaunt family, through the Sayre's line, were thought to have died out sometime in the 17th or 18th century. Rionach Steward, Sayre's <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">Half-blood</a> daughter and the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher at Ilvermony, was also rumoured to have inherited the ability to speak Parseltongue from her mother. Unwilling to further Slytherin's bloodline, since she viewed him as a <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizard</a>, Rionach never married or had children, and she later died without heirs.
</p><p>However, Rionach was unaware that another branch of the Gaunt family was still present, alive and well, across the ocean in <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>. It was from this line of Gaunts from which, centuries later, another Half-blood descendant, Tom Marvolo Riddle, would be born.
</p><p>Rionach's sister Martha, unlike her sibling, married a <a href="/wiki/Muggle" class="mw-redirect" title="Muggle">No-maj</a> (Muggle) friend of the nearby <a href="/wiki/Native_Americans" title="Native Americans">Pocumtuc Native American tribe</a>. Born a <a href="/wiki/Squib" title="Squib">Squib</a>, without any magical powers, Martha felt ostracised within the growing American wizarding community, despite being the child of an important family. In the end, due to the emotional pain caused by being unable to perform magic, and the stigma of being the the only Squib to grow up at Ilvermorny, Martha decided to live her life henceforth as a Muggle.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Tom's maternal grandfather, <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt" title="Marvolo Gaunt">Marvolo Gaunt</a>, and his maternal uncle, <a href="/wiki/Morfin_Gaunt" title="Morfin Gaunt">Morfin Gaunt</a>, claimed to be the last known male, <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> descendants of Slytherin by the early 20th century. As such, they regarded themselves as "royalty" for their ancestry, despite their poverty; squalor; lack of education; and mental and physical disorders from centuries of familial inbreeding.
</p><p>Tom's father, <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle_Senior" title="Tom Riddle Senior">Tom Riddle Senior</a>, was a wealthy Muggle living in the village of <a href="/wiki/Little_Hangleton" title="Little Hangleton">Little Hangleton</a>, near the Gaunt shack, who was forced into a relationship with <a href="/wiki/Merope_Riddle" title="Merope Riddle">Merope Gaunt</a> through the suspected use of the <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a> or a <a href="/wiki/Love_potion" title="Love potion">love potion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> After some time, it is speculated by <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> that Merope discontinued her bewitchment of Tom, in the hopes that he had really fallen in love with her, or would at least stay for their child's sake. To Merope's great sorrow, Tom Snr fled from her after he came to his senses and regained his free will and never wanted to see her again.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Early_life_(1926-1938)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_.281926-1938.29">Early life <span class="template-c">(1926-1938)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=3" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early life (1926-1938)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Early life (1926-1938)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I can make things move without touching them. I can make animals do what I want without training them. I can make bad things happen to people who are mean to me. I can make them hurt if I want to... I can <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">speak to snakes</a> too. They find me, they whisper to me.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Tom Riddle regarding the things he can do<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Tom_Orphanage.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20081031194143" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tom Orphanage.JPG" data-image-key="Tom_Orphanage.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Tom_Orphanage.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20081031194143" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Tom_Orphanage.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20081031194143" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Tom_Orphanage.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20081031194143" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tom Orphanage.JPG" data-image-key="Tom_Orphanage.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Tom_Orphanage.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20081031194143" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tom_Orphanage.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Tom in his room at <a href="/wiki/Wool%27s_orphanage" class="mw-redirect" title="Wool&#39;s orphanage">Wool's orphanage</a>, where he spent the majority of his childhood</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Tom Marvolo Riddle was born on <a href="/wiki/31_December" title="31 December">31 December</a>, <a href="/wiki/1926" title="1926">1926</a> at <a href="/wiki/Wool%27s_Orphanage" title="Wool&#39;s Orphanage">Wool's Orphanage</a> in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>. His mother Merope staggered to the door of the orphanage, gave birth to Tom there, and died shortly after. Riddle grew up in the dingy orphanage, completely unaware of his wizarding heritage. Since the Muggle orphanage staff did not know anything about his mother, they did not know about his magical background. Instead, they believed that Merope was a circus worker, as <a href="/wiki/Cole" title="Cole">Mrs Cole</a> told Dumbledore shortly before his first meeting with Riddle. It is unknown whether or not the staff relayed this to Riddle before his first encounter with Dumbledore.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite his ignorance of his mother's true background, Riddle did have some grasp on his abilities beyond that of normal magical children of his same age, and an unusually high degree of control over them. He could move objects with his mind and cause them to float wherever he wished, manipulate animals and creatures as he wished, speak Parseltongue, and use his power to inflict harm on other orphans. After getting into a fight with fellow orphan <a href="/wiki/Billy_Stubbs" title="Billy Stubbs">Billy Stubbs</a>, he used his powers to hang the boy's rabbit from the rafters. On one occasion, he took two other orphans, <a href="/wiki/Dennis_Bishop" title="Dennis Bishop">Dennis Bishop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Amy_Benson" title="Amy Benson">Amy Benson</a>, into a cave, where he performed an act so horrifying that the two orphans were traumatised into silence. Afterwards, he may have told them, in some means, not to tell anyone what happened in the cave. Riddle also stole from other orphans and hid their things in his cupboard like trophies.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Discovery_of_being_a_wizard">Discovery of being a wizard</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=4" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Discovery of being a wizard">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Discovery of being a wizard"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Did you know, sir? Then...?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Did I know that I had just met the most dangerous Dark wizard of all-time? No.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; A memory of Dumbledore meeting Tom Riddle for the first time<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c7/Child_Tom.png/revision/latest?cb=20181021171804" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Child Tom.png" data-image-key="Child_Tom.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c7/Child_Tom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181021171804" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c7/Child_Tom.png/revision/latest?cb=20181021171804" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c7/Child_Tom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181021171804" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Child Tom.png" data-image-key="Child_Tom.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c7/Child_Tom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181021171804" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Child_Tom.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> visiting 11-year-old Tom Riddle at Wool's Orphanage</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Riddle was eleven, Dumbledore, who at the time was the <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> teacher at Hogwarts, talked to Mrs Cole, who informed him of how unusual the boy was, sharing tales of his extraordinary influence over the other children. When Dumbledore was at last introduced to the boy, Riddle at first believed him to be a doctor or psychiatrist of some sort, come to take him to an asylum because of what the staff had seen. He was convinced after Dumbledore demonstrated his power by using a <a href="/wiki/Flame-Freezing_Charm" title="Flame-Freezing Charm">Flame-Freezing Charm</a> on Riddle's cupboard and revealed that Hogwarts was a school for people with <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a>, whereupon Riddle realised that was what his abilities were. Tom also mentioned his proficiency for <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parseltongue</a> in this same meeting, asking if it was a common gift amongst wizards, to which Dumbledore gave no reply. Dumbledore also admonished Riddle for stealing from others and made him return the items with his apologies. He also warned Riddle to stop his misbehaviour, as Hogwarts had an honour code whereupon lying, cheating and stealing were not tolerated.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At a very early age, it was clear that Riddle displayed a desire to be different and set apart from others (as it was hinted when he mentioned his dislike of his own name, because it was such a common name).<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Young_riddle_orphanage.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161002193849" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Young riddle orphanage.gif" data-image-key="Young_riddle_orphanage.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Young_riddle_orphanage.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161002193849" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Young_riddle_orphanage.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161002193849" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Young_riddle_orphanage.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161002193849" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Young riddle orphanage.gif" data-image-key="Young_riddle_orphanage.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Young_riddle_orphanage.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161002193849" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Young_riddle_orphanage.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> proving to Riddle that he is a wizard</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Riddle was not surprised upon being informed by Dumbledore that he was a wizard — he was, in fact, eager to believe that he had special gifts that no one else had. Riddle also showed an eminent fear of death, considering it a human weakness. He claimed that his mother could not have been a witch, because if she was magical, then she would have been able to avoid dying, and thought his father was a wizard. He asked if his father was an alumnus of Hogwarts, to which Dumbledore said he did not know offhand.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Riddle's abuse of his wizarding powers alarmed Albus. He resolved to keep a close eye on him, something he should have done in any case, seeing as he was "alone and friendless". Dumbledore also warned Riddle that at Hogwarts he would be introduced to the laws that controlled the usage of magic in the <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizarding world</a>, and that law-breakers were punished with severity not by Hogwarts but the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>. Riddle's demeanour changed after Dumbledore reprimanded him; he became more guarded and shielded his reactions. Dumbledore provided Riddle with enough information to find <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters" title="Platform Nine and Three-Quarters">Platform Nine and Three-Quarters</a>. He also provided Riddle with a stipend from school funds so that he could purchase his books and equipment. Travelling on his own to Diagon Alley, Riddle bought some second-hand robes and spell books for himself, along with his wand — thirteen-and-a-half inches, yew, phoenix feather core — at Ollivander's. <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a> later said that the wand was very powerful; Voldemort was very pleased with it until the wand failed him during his confrontation with Harry Potter in the Little Hangleton <a href="/wiki/Little_Hangleton_graveyard" title="Little Hangleton graveyard">graveyard</a>.
</p>
<h3><span id="Hogwarts_years_(1938-1945)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_years_.281938-1945.29">Hogwarts years <span class="template-c">(1938-1945)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=5" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1938-1945)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1938-1945)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half Blood Prince"><b>Tom Riddle</b>: "<i>Sir, I wondered what you know about…about Horcruxes?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Horace Slughorn</b>: "<i>Project for Defence Against the Dark Arts, is it?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Tom Riddle</b>: "<i>Not exactly, sir, I came across the term while reading and I didn’t fully understand it.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Tom Riddle inquiring about Horcruxes<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half_Blood_Prince" class="mw-redirect" title="Harry Potter and the Half Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Riddle was educated at Hogwarts from <a href="/wiki/1938" title="1938">1938</a> to <a href="/wiki/1945" title="1945">1945</a>, and was <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">sorted</a> into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Houses" title="Hogwarts Houses">House</a>, a nod to his ancestor Salazar Slytherin. During summer breaks, he was forced to return to the Muggle orphanage, which he despised and dreaded more than any other place on earth.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/Young_Death_Eaters.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720142700" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Young Death Eaters.jpg" data-image-key="Young_Death_Eaters.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/Young_Death_Eaters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720142700" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/Young_Death_Eaters.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720142700" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/Young_Death_Eaters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720142700" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Young Death Eaters.jpg" data-image-key="Young_Death_Eaters.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/Young_Death_Eaters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720142700" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Young_Death_Eaters.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club" title="Slug Club">Slug Club</a>, of which Tom was a member of during his education</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Riddle described the way he was seen as "<i>poor, but brilliant, parent-less, but so brave, a school <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a>, a model student.</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-COS_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Due to his exceptional acting abilities, he was able to convince virtually all of the Hogwarts staff and instructors that this facade was his true personality. The sole exception to this was Dumbledore, who, though not necessarily suspicious of Riddle, never forgot about his misdeeds at the orphanage, nor his unsettling behaviour during their first meeting. In turn, Riddle realised that he had been careless in showing Dumbledore his true character upon their first meeting, and never attempted to win him over as he had with his other instructors. In time, he came to fear and despise Dumbledore.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Over time, Riddle gathered to himself a <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_gang" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s gang">gang of Slytherin thugs</a>, a motley composition of "<i>the weak seeking protection, the ambitious seeking some shared glory, and the thuggish gravitating toward a leader who could show them more refined forms of cruelty,</i>" most of which would become the first <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. Riddle claimed they were his friends, and made it appear so in public, but in truth, they amounted to little more than servants, and he cared almost nothing for them. He often manipulated them into committing petty crimes and other misdeeds, but none of these incidents were reliably traced back to the group.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Opening_the_Chamber_of_Secrets">Opening the Chamber of Secrets</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=6" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Opening the Chamber of Secrets">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Opening the Chamber of Secrets"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Plot_to_open_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Plot to open the Chamber of Secrets">Plot to open the Chamber of Secrets</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>The last time the chamber was opened, a <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">Mudblood</a> died.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, regarding the first opening of the Chamber of Secrets<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Tom_in_the_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160525185959" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="109" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tom in the Chamber.jpg" data-image-key="Tom_in_the_Chamber.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Tom_in_the_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160525185959" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Tom_in_the_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160525185959" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Tom_in_the_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160525185959" decoding="async" width="250" height="109" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tom in the Chamber.jpg" data-image-key="Tom_in_the_Chamber.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Tom_in_the_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160525185959" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tom_in_the_Chamber.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Tom standing in the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Upon arriving at Hogwarts, Riddle became obsessed with his heritage and began researching it with an insatiable hunger. He focused solely on the identity of his father, thinking him to be the magical parent, as he felt his mother could not have been a witch if she had died. He searched for his father's name in the school trophy room, in the records of Hogwarts prefects and in records of wizarding history, but found nothing to suggest his father had even attended Hogwarts. He was eventually forced to accept that his father was the Muggle parent, and that his mother was the magical one. It was around this time that Riddle gave himself the alias "Lord Voldemort", to spare himself of the reminder of his "<i>filthy Muggle father</i>."<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Using his middle name, Marvolo, which was taken from his maternal grandfather, Riddle discovered his mother's heritage and the Gaunts' bloodline connection with Salazar Slytherin. Once Riddle learned of his ancestry, it was not long before he discovered the existence of the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> under Hogwarts, during his fifth year, and tamed the <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">Basilisk</a> which dwelt within. As the Heir of Slytherin through his mother's family, Tom was able to open the Chamber Slytherin had left behind in order to "<i>purge the school of all those who [were] unworthy to study magic</i>" — in Riddle's and Slytherin's eyes, <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180122221747" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="114" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tom Riddle framing Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180122221747" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180122221747" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180122221747" decoding="async" width="250" height="114" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tom Riddle framing Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180122221747" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tom_Riddle_framing_Hagrid.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A 16-year-old Riddle during the 1943 opening of the Chamber of Secrets threatening <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Around <a href="/wiki/13_June" title="13 June">13 June</a>, <a href="/wiki/1943" title="1943">1943</a>, the Basilisk injured many at Hogwarts, with its last victim being a student named <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">Myrtle Warren</a>, who was killed in the girls' bathroom when she saw the Basilisk's yellow eyes. In light of this incident, the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Board_of_Governors" title="Hogwarts Board of Governors">Hogwarts Board of Governors</a> decided that Hogwarts was to be closed. During that year, Riddle made a special request that Headmaster <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a> would allow him to stay at school over the summer break. However, Dippet informed him of the governors' decision, and denied his request. Realising that the Chamber would need to be closed and the culprit caught in order to keep the school open (and not have to return permanently to the orphanage), Riddle framed fellow student <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> and his pet <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>. He convinced Dippet that Aragog was the monster that had terrorised the school. Hagrid was expelled, and Riddle received an engraved trophy for <a href="/wiki/Special_Award_for_Services_to_the_School" title="Special Award for Services to the School">Special Services to the School</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180122221958" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore watching Tom Riddle.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180122221958" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180122221958" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180122221958" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore watching Tom Riddle.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180122221958" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_watching_Tom_Riddle.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore "<i>keeping an annoyingly close watch</i>" on Tom</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore, who did not believe that Hagrid was responsible for the killing, managed to arrange for him to be kept on as Hogwarts's groundskeeper. Distrusting Riddle, Dumbledore kept an "annoyingly close" watch on him after that. Due to this, Riddle realised that he would not be able to risk opening the Chamber while still a student. As such, he would use this murder to eventually preserve a part of his soul within <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s Diary">his own school diary</a>, the very first of his seven <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, hoping it would one day lead someone to finish Salazar Slytherin's "noble work".
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Murder_of_the_Riddle_family">Murder of the Riddle family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=7" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Murder of the Riddle family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Murder of the Riddle family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_the_Riddle_family" title="Murder of the Riddle family">Murder of the Riddle family</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Morfin Gaunt</b>: "<i>I thought you was that <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle_Senior" title="Tom Riddle Senior">Muggle</a>, you look mighty like that Muggle.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Riddle</b>: "<i>What Muggle?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Morfin Gaunt</b>: "<i>That Muggle what my sister took a fancy to, that Muggle what lives in the big house over the way, you look right like him. Riddle. But he's older now, in 'e? He's older 'n you, now I think on it... he come back, see.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Riddle confronts his maternal uncle<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/HBP_chapter_17_BW.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190125020314" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="245" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="HBP chapter 17 BW.jpg" data-image-key="HBP_chapter_17_BW.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/HBP_chapter_17_BW.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20190125020314" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/HBP_chapter_17_BW.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190125020314" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/HBP_chapter_17_BW.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20190125020314" decoding="async" width="245" height="245" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="HBP chapter 17 BW.jpg" data-image-key="HBP_chapter_17_BW.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/HBP_chapter_17_BW.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20190125020314" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:HBP_chapter_17_BW.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Morfin_Gaunt" title="Morfin Gaunt">Morfin Gaunt</a> telling his nephew about the latter's heritage</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Around <a href="/wiki/August" title="August">August</a> <a href="/wiki/1943" title="1943">1943</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Riddle went to Little Hangleton to learn about his mother's family. While at the <a href="/wiki/Gaunt_Shack" title="Gaunt Shack">Gaunt Shack</a>, he met his uncle Morfin Gaunt, with whom he was far from impressed. Morfin mentioned offhandedly at one point during this meeting that he thought that Tom looked "<i>mighty like that Muggle</i>," Merope's husband, Tom Riddle Snr. Riddle immediately demanded the identity of the Muggle in question, and Morfin told Riddle the story of his Muggle father, which infuriated Tom to the point of seeking revenge. Riddle stunned Morfin and took his wand, went over to the <a href="/wiki/Riddle_House" title="Riddle House">Riddle House</a> and, using his uncle's wand, murdered his father, <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Riddle" title="Thomas Riddle">grandfather</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Mary_Riddle" title="Mary Riddle">grandmother</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a>.
</p><p>Riddle covered up his crimes by altering Morfin's memory, causing him to believe that he was the killer. When the Ministry of Magic investigated the crime, Morfin, who had previously served three years in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> for using magic in front of and against Muggles, freely admitted to the deed and was sentenced to life imprisonment in Azkaban. Tom took the <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring" title="Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s Ring">Gaunt family's signet ring</a> from Morfin and later on would preserve another part of his soul within it to make his second Horcrux, wearing it like a trophy at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Learning_about_Horcruxes">Learning about Horcruxes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=8" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Learning about Horcruxes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Learning about Horcruxes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Riddle</b>: "<i>How do you split your soul?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Horace Slughorn</b>: "<i>Well, you must understand that the soul is supposed to remain intact and whole. Splitting it is an act of violation, it is against nature.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Riddle</b>: "<i>But how do you do it?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Horace Slughorn</b>: "<i>By an act of evil — the supreme act of evil. By commiting murder. Killing rips the soul apart. The wizard intent upon creating a Horcrux would use the damage to his advantage: He would encase the torn portion —</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Discussion of how Horcruxes are made<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2e/Slughorn_and_Riddle.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20180720151739" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Slughorn and Riddle.jpeg" data-image-key="Slughorn_and_Riddle.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2e/Slughorn_and_Riddle.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720151739" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2e/Slughorn_and_Riddle.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20180720151739" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2e/Slughorn_and_Riddle.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720151739" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Slughorn and Riddle.jpeg" data-image-key="Slughorn_and_Riddle.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2e/Slughorn_and_Riddle.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720151739" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Slughorn_and_Riddle.jpeg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Young Riddle asking <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Professor Slughorn</a> about <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During his sixth year, Riddle questioned <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Professor Slughorn</a>, who was taken in by Riddle's charisma, about the possibility of creating more than one Horcrux, something Slughorn felt deeply ashamed of in later years. In his mid-teen years, Riddle already sought to make himself <a href="/wiki/Immortality" title="Immortality">immortal</a>; being unable to find any recorded information on creating multiple Horcruxes. He wanted to split his soul into seven, as this is the most powerful magical number, and asked the experienced and knowledgeable Slughorn for an opinion before attempting this unknown feat. Slughorn answered all of Riddle's questions under the belief it was merely academic curiosity but was deeply horrified at the thought of creating multiple Horcruxes.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/First_time.gif/revision/latest?cb=20180904181155" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="159" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="First time.gif" data-image-key="First_time.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/First_time.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20180904181155" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/First_time.gif/revision/latest?cb=20180904181155" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/First_time.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20180904181155" decoding="async" width="245" height="159" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="First time.gif" data-image-key="First_time.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/First_time.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20180904181155" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:First_time.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Riddle <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">splitting his soul</a> for the first time</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Riddle succeeded in doing so at some point during this year, creating his first Horcrux in the form of the aforementioned diary and his second in the form of the inherited ring. During Riddle's seventh year at Hogwarts, he was made <a href="/wiki/Head_Boy_or_Girl" title="Head Boy or Girl">Head Boy</a>, earned outstanding marks in every examination he took, and received a <a href="/wiki/Medal_for_Magical_Merit" title="Medal for Magical Merit">Medal for Magical Merit</a>. Riddle was regarded as one of the most brilliant students ever to attend Hogwarts, a fact admitted by Dumbledore himself.
</p>
<div style="clear:left; margin:0; padding:0;"></div>
<h3><span id="After_Hogwarts_(1945-1949)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="After_Hogwarts_.281945-1949.29">After Hogwarts <span class="template-c">(1945-1949)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=9" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: After Hogwarts (1945-1949)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: After Hogwarts (1945-1949)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Rumours of your doings have reached your old school, Tom. I should be sorry to believe half of them.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Riddle</b>: "<i>Greatness inspires envy, envy engenders spite, spite spawns lies. You must know this, Dumbledore.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; A business intercourse between a headmaster and his old student<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7d/B2C4M2_Borgin_and_Burkes.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180417010225" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B2C4M2 Borgin and Burkes.jpg" data-image-key="B2C4M2_Borgin_and_Burkes.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7d/B2C4M2_Borgin_and_Burkes.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180417010225" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7d/B2C4M2_Borgin_and_Burkes.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180417010225" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7d/B2C4M2_Borgin_and_Burkes.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180417010225" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B2C4M2 Borgin and Burkes.jpg" data-image-key="B2C4M2_Borgin_and_Burkes.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7d/B2C4M2_Borgin_and_Burkes.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180417010225" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B2C4M2_Borgin_and_Burkes.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Borgin_and_Burkes" title="Borgin and Burkes">Borgin and Burkes</a>, Voldemort's former place of employment</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After graduating, Riddle immediately approached Dippet and asked him for a chance to teach <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, and to remain at Hogwarts, for reasons that he did not confide with the then-headmaster — Hogwarts being his true home at heart, using the influential position as a teacher to recruit students into his future army, and to continue to learn the castle's magical secrets. Dippet rejected this offer, deeming the boy too young, but invited Riddle to reapply in a few years, if he was still interested in the post, something that Dumbledore heavily advised against.
</p><p>Shortly before leaving Hogwarts, however, Riddle charmed <a href="/wiki/Helena_Ravenclaw" title="Helena Ravenclaw">Helena Ravenclaw</a>, the daughter of <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw" title="Rowena Ravenclaw">Rowena Ravenclaw</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">ghost</a> of <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw House</a>, into telling him the location of <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw%27s_Diadem" class="mw-redirect" title="Rowena Ravenclaw&#39;s Diadem">her mother's diadem</a>, which she revealed as a hollow tree deep within a far-flung forest in <a href="/wiki/Albania" title="Albania">Albania</a>. He presumably travelled there at her instruction, murdering an <a href="/wiki/Albanian_peasant" title="Albanian peasant">Albanian peasant</a> along the way before retrieving the diadem, which he later preserved a third part of his soul within to make his third Horcrux.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Upon his return to Britain, Riddle was offered several positions in the Ministry of Magic, but ended up working at <a href="/wiki/Borgin_and_Burkes" title="Borgin and Burkes">Borgin and Burkes</a>, to the disappointment and surprise of many. Riddle set to persuading witches and wizards to part with their valuable magical heirlooms — a job at which he was very good.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="The_rise_of_the_Dark_Lord_(1950-1970)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="The_rise_of_the_Dark_Lord_.281950-1970.29">The rise of the Dark Lord <span class="template-c">(1950-1970)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=10" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The rise of the Dark Lord (1950-1970)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: The rise of the Dark Lord (1950-1970)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Murdering_Hepzibah_Smith">Murdering Hepzibah Smith</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=11" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Murdering Hepzibah Smith">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Murdering Hepzibah Smith"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>But before they were sure beyond doubt that the cup and the locket were both gone, the assistant who had worked at <a href="/wiki/Borgin_and_Burkes" title="Borgin and Burkes">Borgin and Burkes</a>, the young man who had visited Hepzibah so regularly and charmed her so well, had resigned his post and vanished. His superiors had no idea where he had gone; they were as surprised as anyone at his disappearance. And that was the last that was seen or heard of Tom Riddle for a very long time. </i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Tom disappears after murdering Hepzibah Smith<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Riddle_Hepzibah.png/revision/latest?cb=20141222162612" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="161" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Riddle Hepzibah.png" data-image-key="Riddle_Hepzibah.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Riddle_Hepzibah.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141222162612" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Riddle_Hepzibah.png/revision/latest?cb=20141222162612" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Riddle_Hepzibah.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141222162612" decoding="async" width="250" height="161" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Riddle Hepzibah.png" data-image-key="Riddle_Hepzibah.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Riddle_Hepzibah.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141222162612" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Riddle_Hepzibah.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hepzibah_Smith" title="Hepzibah Smith">Hepzibah Smith</a> shows Riddle Slytherin's Locket</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While working at Borgin and Burkes, Riddle befriended <a href="/wiki/Hepzibah_Smith" title="Hepzibah Smith">Hepzibah Smith</a>, a wealthy but elderly descendant of <a href="/wiki/Helga_Hufflepuff" title="Helga Hufflepuff">Helga Hufflepuff</a>. Between <a href="/wiki/1955" title="1955">1955</a> and <a href="/wiki/1961" title="1961">1961</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Hepzibah showed Riddle her two most valuable treasures: <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">his ancestor's locket</a> and <a href="/wiki/Helga_Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Helga Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup">her ancestor's cup</a>. Tom's eyes flashed red with greed and avarice upon seeing these objects, seeing the locket to be rightfully his as Slytherin's heir and the cup as a reminder of Hogwarts, as well as a priceless artefact. 
</p><p>Riddle murdered Hepzibah, by using a "<a href="/wiki/Little_known_poison" title="Little known poison">Little known poison</a>", to steal these coveted objects and vanished without a trace. He again covered his tracks well by implanting another false memory into an innocent bystander — <a href="/wiki/Hokey" title="Hokey">Hokey</a>, Hepzibah's <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elf</a>. Hokey admitted to accidentally putting <a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">poison</a> into Hepzibah's cocoa, which was believed, as Hokey was elderly herself. Meanwhile, Riddle immediately resigned his post at Borgin and Burkes and fled with the cup and locket, subsequently turning them into two more Horcruxes using the murders of Hepzibah and an unidentified <a href="/wiki/Muggle_tramp" title="Muggle tramp">Muggle tramp</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Lord_Voldemort's_request"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Lord_Voldemort.27s_request">Lord Voldemort's request</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=12" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort&#039;s request">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort&#039;s request"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I have experimented; I have pushed the boundaries of magic further, perhaps, than they have ever been pushed —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Tom regarding the magical experimentation he did while abroad<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Riddle disappeared for ten long years. He slipped deeper into the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>, travelled extensively, consorted with disreputable people, began to become distorted in appearance and lose his handsomeness due to splitting his soul so many times, and began to use the alias "Lord Voldemort" openly. He also severed contact with Slughorn, who became upset for not living up to the Potions Master's employment offers.
</p><p>Ten years after Hepzibah Smith's murder, Riddle appealed once more to the Headmaster of Hogwarts, now Albus Dumbledore, for the position of Professor of Defence Against the Dark Arts. After a short, superficially amiable chat, Dumbledore directly confronted Riddle regarding why he had requested the position, as he knew full well that Riddle had no desire whatsoever to teach. Riddle, unable to make an open request of Dumbledore due to the malicious nature of his true intentions, simply left after a final, gentle rebuke from his former teacher. From that day on, Hogwarts was never able to keep a Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher for more than a year, which was attributed by Dumbledore to a <a href="/wiki/Jinx_on_the_post_of_Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts_teacher" title="Jinx on the post of Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher">curse</a> by Riddle. The visit to Hogwarts was not fruitless, however, for Riddle used the opportunity to hide the diadem in the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>, where he believed it would never be found.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Voldemort, as Riddle was now exclusively called, spent the next few years before the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a> gathering followers in witches and wizards who called themselves, collectively, Death Eaters.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Some were supportive of his cause to dominate Muggles and Muggle-borns; while others were greedy for domination, wealth and fame; and yet others joined the Dark Lord out of fear. Voldemort considered them more like servants than friends or family. According to <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, Voldemort also used tricks, jinxes, and blackmail to get people to willingly join him. 
</p><p>At some point around this time, Voldemort greatly enhanced his skills in <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a>, to the point that he quickly earned a reputation as the greatest Legilimens alive. Voldemort could read, control and unhinge the minds of others, and could almost always tell when he was being lied to. According to <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, Voldemort often enjoyed telepathically invading the minds of others, creating visions designed to torture them into madness. Only after extracting the last exquisite ounce of agony, only when he had them literally begging for death, would he finally kill them.
</p>
<h3><span id="First_Wizarding_War_(1970-1981)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="First_Wizarding_War_.281970-1981.29">First Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1970-1981)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=13" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: First Wizarding War (1970-1981)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: First Wizarding War (1970-1981)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>He was takin' over. 'Course, some stood up to him — an' he killed 'em.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort's actions during the First Wizarding War<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Harry-potter1-voldemort.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170508224423" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-voldemort.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-voldemort.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Harry-potter1-voldemort.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170508224423" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Harry-potter1-voldemort.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170508224423" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Harry-potter1-voldemort.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170508224423" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-voldemort.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-voldemort.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Harry-potter1-voldemort.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170508224423" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter1-voldemort.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort wearing a hooded cloak during the First War, as a possible means to invoke fear</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In 1970, Voldemort started the First Wizarding War by taking advantage of one of the wizarding world's greatest weaknesses: the beings and creatures that they had outcast. The Dark Lord recruited the <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giants</a>, who had long ago been driven by <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">Wizardkind</a> into the mountains, and <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolves</a>, who were persecuted by most witches and wizards. Many feared the <a href="/wiki/Goblin" title="Goblin">goblins</a> would also join him, as they were restricted from wand use, but it never happened. In fact, Voldemort murdered a family of goblins near Nottingham at some point during the War, for an unknown reason (possibly anger at the neutrality of the goblins, or no reason at all). Voldemort's army caused widespread destruction and mayhem during the war.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Senior" title="Bartemius Crouch Senior">Bartemius Crouch Snr</a>, who was the head of the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Department of Magical Law Enforcement</a> at the time and was known for his fanatical hatred of the Dark Arts, issued an edict that gave <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> authorisation to use Unforgivable Curses on Death Eaters without warning, and suspects were sometimes handed over to the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> without a <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a> trial. Many innocent people were locked away. Due to the atrocities committed by the Death Eaters and Voldemort, and his terrifying persona, people were even afraid to speak his name, and he was referred to as <i>"You-Know-Who"</i> or <i>"He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named."</i>
</p><p>Under the staunch protection of Dumbledore, the only person Voldemort truly feared, Hogwarts remained a safe place of learning throughout the entire war. The <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> was created by Dumbledore at this time to fight against Voldemort. The war itself lasted for eleven long years.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Visiting_the_Lee_family">Visiting the Lee family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=14" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Visiting the Lee family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Visiting the Lee family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Eventually, Lord Voldemort visited the home of the <a href="/wiki/Barnaby_Lee%27s_father" title="Barnaby Lee&#39;s father">father</a> of <a href="/wiki/Barnaby_Lee" title="Barnaby Lee">Barnaby Lee</a>. Mr Lee told his son he was capable of anything if he could become as strong as the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Lord" title="Dark Lord">Dark Lord</a>, showing faith in his master. He later drowned Barnaby's pet <a href="/wiki/Kneazle" title="Kneazle">Kneazle</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Testing_his_Horcrux's_defences"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Testing_his_Horcrux.27s_defences">Testing his Horcrux's defences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=15" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Testing his Horcrux&#039;s defences">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Testing his Horcrux&#039;s defences"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>To the Dark Lord - I know I will be dead long before you read this, but I want you to know it was I who discovered your secret, I have stolen the real <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> and intend to destroy it as soon as I can, I can face death in the hope, that when you meet your match, you will be mortal once again. -R.A.B.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Regulus Black's letter to Voldermort before his untimely death.<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
