<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Inferi-0.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150128024629" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="149" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Inferi-0.jpg" data-image-key="Inferi-0.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Inferi-0.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20150128024629" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Inferi-0.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150128024629" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Inferi-0.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20150128024629" decoding="async" width="220" height="149" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Inferi-0.jpg" data-image-key="Inferi-0.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Inferi-0.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20150128024629" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Inferi-0.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Inferi in the crystal cave</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1979" title="1979">1979</a>, Voldemort decided to test the defences around his Horcruxes. He placed Slytherin's locket in the crystal cave, and asked <a href="/wiki/Regulus_Black" title="Regulus Black">Regulus Black</a>, a loyal 18-year-old Death Eater to lend him his house-elf, <a href="/wiki/Kreacher" title="Kreacher">Kreacher</a>. Voldemort took the elf with him to the cave, forced him to drink the <a href="/wiki/Emerald_Potion" title="Emerald Potion">Emerald Potion</a>, and left him to die on the Crystal Cave Island. Kreacher was able to escape using house-elf magic, and told Regulus of what had happened. Over the years, Voldemort created an army of Inferi from the people he had killed to further strengthen his defences. Upon hearing Kreacher's story, Regulus, who had already been somewhat uncomfortable with the reality of being a Death Eater, decided to defect. From clues left behind by Voldemort, he deduced that his master had created a Horcrux in order to become immortal. He took a duplicate locket and placed a note inside for Voldemort to find, then ordered Kreacher to take him to where the real locket was hidden. Kreacher guided Regulus past the cave's defences. At the island, with the basin of potion containing the locket, Regulus ordered Kreacher to take it once the potion was gone and replace it with the fake one, then escape without him and find a way to destroy the Horcrux. Regulus drank the potion himself, and when he tried to get water from the lake to quench his thirst, he was dragged to his death by the <a href="/wiki/Inferius" title="Inferius">Inferi</a>. Kreacher obeyed his master's orders and switched the lockets before escaping. However, despite his best efforts, he was unable to destroy the Horcrux.
</p><p>During this time, Voldemort gave his old diary to <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>, his loyal Death Eater, and ordered him to hide it. Malfoy kept it safe in <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">his manor</a>, but the Dark Lord never told him that the diary contained a fragment of his soul. Voldemort informed him only that the diary was cleverly charmed and smuggling it into Hogwarts will cause the reopening of the legendary Chamber of Secrets and send the Basilisk living inside the chamber to finish Slytherin's idea of cleansing the school of all Muggle-borns, thus proving that Voldemort was Slytherin's true heir.
</p><p>Voldemort also left the Hufflepuff's cup in the care of <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, another one of his loyal Death Eaters. Bellatrix, much like her brother-in-law Lucius, was ordered to hide it, so she stored it in <a href="/wiki/Lestrange_Vault" title="Lestrange Vault">her family vault</a> at <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts Wizarding Bank</a>, which was considered to be impossible to plunder. She treated the object with extreme priority, although Voldermort hadn't informed her that the cup was a Horcrux. The cup was protected by the bank's extensive security measures, but Lestrange casted some protective curses on it, like a spell which would cause any object to multiply exponentially if touched by anyone other than the vault's owners or to cause the object itself to glow hot as fire and burn the flesh of anyone trying to remove it without authorization.
</p><p>Probably during this time he returned Gaunt's ring to the Gaunt shack. He placed the ring inside a golden box and hid it beneath the shack's rotting floorboard, setting up many protective enchantments to deter outsiders from entering the shack and finding the ring. He also placed a powerful curse on the ring as well, one that would quickly lead to the death of the ring's wearer if not stemmed.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Prophecy">The Prophecy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=16" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Prophecy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: The Prophecy"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>The one with the power to vanquish the Dark Lord approaches... Born to those who have thrice defied him, born as the seventh month dies... And the Dark Lord will mark him as equal, but he will have power the Dark Lord knows not... And either must die at the hand of the other for neither can live while the other survives... The one with the power to vanquish the Dark Lord will be born as the seventh month dies...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">Sybill Trelawney's first prophecy</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><p>Ten years into the war, when Voldemort was at the height of his dominion, a prophecy was given by <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a> to Albus Dumbledore which predicted the fall of the Dark Lord. This prophecy was given in the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head Inn</a> during an interview for the position of Professor of <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> This prophecy was overheard by Death Eater and informant <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> According to Dumbledore, Snape only heard half of the prophecy and was then thrown out by the barman, <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth Dumbledore</a>, Albus' brother. He relayed to Voldemort what he had heard, not realising that he had missed an important part of the message.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Trelawney's description of the night's events was a bit different however, as she stated that after feeling "ill," Aberforth burst into the room with Snape in tow, whom he had caught eavesdropping at the door. This is in contrast with Dumbledore's description of events. However, this may be due to the fact that Dumbledore had wished to conceal the identity of the spy from Harry, and told him a simplified version of the events. In any case, Voldemort received only the first part of the prophecy. Feeling threatened, he sprang into action to prevent the fulfilment of the prophecy.
</p><p>There were, at the time, two babies to whom the prophecy could have referred — <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, the half-blood son of <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a>; and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, the pure-blood son of <a href="/wiki/Frank_Longbottom" title="Frank Longbottom">Frank</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alice_Longbottom" title="Alice Longbottom">Alice Longbottom</a>. Both families had sought to thwart Voldemort three times, and both families were members of the Order of the Phoenix. Both children in question were born at the end of the seventh month, July. Voldemort chose to target Harry instead of Neville; Dumbledore suspected this was because Harry shared a similar family heritage with Voldemort, both of them being half-bloods.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="First_fall_from_grace">First fall from grace</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=17" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: First fall from grace">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: First fall from grace"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Lily, take Harry and go! It's him! Go! Run! I'll hold him off!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;James Potter moments before his death<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Potter_family_murder.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007230659" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Potter family murder.gif" data-image-key="Potter_family_murder.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Potter_family_murder.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161007230659" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Potter_family_murder.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007230659" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Potter_family_murder.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161007230659" decoding="async" width="250" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Potter family murder.gif" data-image-key="Potter_family_murder.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Potter_family_murder.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161007230659" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Potter_family_murder.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort killing Lily Potter with the <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p> Some time after Harry's birth, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, member of the Order of the Phoenix and the Potter's <a href="/wiki/Secret_Keeper" title="Secret Keeper">Secret Keeper</a> began working as a Death Eater for Voldemort. On 31 October 1981 he told Voldemort of their location. The Dark Lord travelled to the <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a> and with the Potter's <a href="/wiki/Fidelius_Charm" title="Fidelius Charm">Fidelius Charm</a> broken, he simply walked into <a href="/wiki/Potters%27_Cottage" class="mw-redirect" title="Potters&#39; Cottage">their home</a>. Once inside he proceeded to murder James and Lily, who did not have their wands. However, when he used the Killing Curse on Harry, it rebounded and seemingly obliterated his body. This happened because Lily lovingly sacrificed her life to protect her son, creating a powerful defence of ancient magic around Harry which protected him for many years.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> After eleven years of domination and warfare, Voldemort was defeated for the first time.</p><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Harry_Voldemort_1981.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180606142545" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Voldemort 1981.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Voldemort_1981.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Harry_Voldemort_1981.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180606142545" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Harry_Voldemort_1981.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180606142545" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Harry_Voldemort_1981.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180606142545" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Voldemort 1981.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Voldemort_1981.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b7/Harry_Voldemort_1981.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180606142545" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Voldemort_1981.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Infant Harry Potter faces death for the first time</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>It was at this point that Voldemort's next Horcrux was unknowingly created. Years of experimentation, murder, and deliberately ripping apart his soul into so many Horcruxes had rendered the remainder of his soul so unstable that, when his body was destroyed, a small shard of his soul broke apart from the rest and latched unto the only other living being in what remained of the room: Harry Potter himself. The soul shard latched unto Harry's own soul, granting him some of the Dark Lord's own powers and providing him with a latent connection to Voldemort's own mind. Ironically, Harry became the Dark Lord's sixth Horcrux, the desired number Voldemort wanted in order to split his soul into seven pieces. What remained of Voldemort's mangled soul swiftly escaped from the ruins of the house that same night.
</p>
<h3><span id="Missing_years_(1981-1994)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Missing_years_.281981-1994.29">Missing years <span class="template-c">(1981-1994)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=18" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Missing years (1981-1994)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Missing years (1981-1994)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>I was ripped from my body, less than spirit, less than the meanest ghost, but still, I was alive.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lord Voldemort regarding his fall from power<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/B4C30M1_Wizengamot_trial_Pensieve_memory.png/revision/latest?cb=20190313000102" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="88" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B4C30M1 Wizengamot trial Pensieve memory.png" data-image-key="B4C30M1_Wizengamot_trial_Pensieve_memory.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/B4C30M1_Wizengamot_trial_Pensieve_memory.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190313000102" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/B4C30M1_Wizengamot_trial_Pensieve_memory.png/revision/latest?cb=20190313000102" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/B4C30M1_Wizengamot_trial_Pensieve_memory.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190313000102" decoding="async" width="220" height="88" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B4C30M1 Wizengamot trial Pensieve memory.png" data-image-key="B4C30M1_Wizengamot_trial_Pensieve_memory.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/B4C30M1_Wizengamot_trial_Pensieve_memory.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190313000102" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C30M1_Wizengamot_trial_Pensieve_memory.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Death Eaters' trial</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>
After Voldemort's first fall from domination, the Death Eaters dispersed and attempted to return to normal life. Many claimed they had been under the <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a>, while others stayed true to their master and continued his work, most notably the <a href="/wiki/Lestrange_family" title="Lestrange family">Lestrange family</a>, who were eventually taken into custody, convicted at trial, and imprisoned in Azkaban. Most of them however, managed ultimately to remain free and to re-integrate into society.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup></p><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Voldemort_Spirit.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20180811003923" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort Spirit.JPG" data-image-key="Voldemort_Spirit.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Voldemort_Spirit.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180811003923" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Voldemort_Spirit.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20180811003923" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Voldemort_Spirit.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180811003923" decoding="async" width="220" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort Spirit.JPG" data-image-key="Voldemort_Spirit.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Voldemort_Spirit.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180811003923" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_Spirit.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort's disembodied soul</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort lost his physical form and magical powers, but he remained alive in ghostly form. The Horcruxes he had created kept his spirit bound to the physical world. He retreated to the forests of Albania, where he had previously found his fifth Horcrux, and waited for his faithful Death Eaters to find him, but many of them now believed him dead, and those still faithful to him were either dead or in Azkaban. His one remaining power was possession. He gained physical form by inhabiting animals, mainly snakes, though he disliked doing so because the bodies of such animals were ill-equipped to perform magic, and because his possession significantly reduced their lifespans; none of his hosts survived for too long. Additionally, any help that he could have potentially rendered himself required the use of a wand, and animals, obviously, could not be used for this purpose. Voldemort did not dare enter the communities to possess humans, as he knew that Aurors were still abroad, looking for any signs of him.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Search_for_the_Philosopher's_Stone"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Search_for_the_Philosopher.27s_Stone">Search for the Philosopher's Stone</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=19" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Search for the Philosopher&#039;s Stone">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Search for the Philosopher&#039;s Stone"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Harry Potter... we meet again.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort speaking through Quirrell<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 306px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/QuirinusQuirrell_WB_F1_QuirrellInClassroomHoldingLizard_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170912184629" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="304" height="132" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="QuirinusQuirrell WB F1 QuirrellInClassroomHoldingLizard Still 080615 Land.jpg" data-image-key="QuirinusQuirrell_WB_F1_QuirrellInClassroomHoldingLizard_Still_080615_Land.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/QuirinusQuirrell_WB_F1_QuirrellInClassroomHoldingLizard_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/304?cb=20170912184629" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/QuirinusQuirrell_WB_F1_QuirrellInClassroomHoldingLizard_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170912184629" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/QuirinusQuirrell_WB_F1_QuirrellInClassroomHoldingLizard_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/304?cb=20170912184629" decoding="async" width="304" height="132" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="QuirinusQuirrell WB F1 QuirrellInClassroomHoldingLizard Still 080615 Land.jpg" data-image-key="QuirinusQuirrell_WB_F1_QuirrellInClassroomHoldingLizard_Still_080615_Land.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/QuirinusQuirrell_WB_F1_QuirrellInClassroomHoldingLizard_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/304?cb=20170912184629" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:QuirinusQuirrell_WB_F1_QuirrellInClassroomHoldingLizard_Still_080615_Land.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Quirinus Quirrell, Voldemort's temporary host</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>In <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>, Voldemort formed a plan to regain his physical body. Hogwarts Professor <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a> had made a voyage to Albania, where his foolish and gullible mind was vulnerable to Voldemort. He latched onto Quirrell's body and came back to England with him.
</p><p>Somehow, Voldemort learned of the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a>, and how it could somehow return him to his physical form. He ordered Quirrell to steal the stone from a <a href="/wiki/Vault_713" title="Vault 713">Vault 713</a> in <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts Wizarding Bank</a> so he could make the <a href="/wiki/Elixir_of_Life" title="Elixir of Life">Elixir of Life</a>. Voldemort discovered the Stone had been removed earlier that same day, and through Quirrell's connections at Hogwarts, learned it was hidden at the school.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_27-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The same year that Voldemort set to the task of stealing the Stone, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> began his first year at Hogwarts. There were many barriers protecting the Stone. <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, who had switched sides near the end of the war and become a professor of <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a>, was suspicious of Quirrell and hounded him relentlessly. On 31 October, Quirrell released a <a href="/wiki/Troll" title="Troll">troll</a> in the Hogwarts dungeons as a distraction and sneaked to the Third Floor Corridor, where the Stone was being hidden. Snape followed him and blocked him off, but he has been bitten on the leg by the three-headed dog <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a> in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_27-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Voldemort was not to be stopped.
</p><p>Later in the year, during a <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_vs_Slytherin_Quidditch_match_(1991)" title="Gryffindor vs Slytherin Quidditch match (1991)">Quidditch match between Gryffindor and Slytherin</a>, Voldemort ordered Quirrell to kill Harry Potter. Quirrell jinxed <a href="/wiki/Nimbus_2000" title="Nimbus 2000">Harry's broomstick</a> to throw him off, but Snape tried to save Harry with a counter-curse. <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, observing the crowd through binoculars to figure out who was jinxing the broom, saw Snape discreetly uttering the counter-curse incantation but erroneously assumed he was performing the actual curse. Running to Snape's stand and setting fire to his robes to distract him and make him stop, she accidentally knocked Quirrell over. This meant that Quirrell broke the necessary eye contact for performing his spell correctly.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>The hooded figure raised its head and looked right at Harry -- unicorn blood was dribbling down its front. It got to its feet and came swiftly toward Harry -- he couldn't move for fear</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort feasting on Unicorn blood<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Voldemort_drinking_unicorn_blood.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151211143338" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort drinking unicorn blood.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort_drinking_unicorn_blood.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Voldemort_drinking_unicorn_blood.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151211143338" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Voldemort_drinking_unicorn_blood.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151211143338" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Voldemort_drinking_unicorn_blood.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151211143338" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort drinking unicorn blood.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort_drinking_unicorn_blood.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Voldemort_drinking_unicorn_blood.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151211143338" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_drinking_unicorn_blood.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hooded Quirrell drinking unicorn blood in place of his master</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>
Throughout the year, hosting Voldemort's soul drastically weakened Quirrell's body. Voldemort ordered Quirrell to prey on <a href="/wiki/Unicorn" title="Unicorn">unicorns</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> and drink <a href="/wiki/Unicorn_blood" title="Unicorn blood">their blood</a> so he could gain strength from the unicorn's healing abilities and keep Quirrell alive. Quirrell met Harry, <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Fang" title="Fang">Fang</a> there, and was about to attack Harry until the centaur <a href="/wiki/Firenze" title="Firenze">Firenze</a> rescued him. About a week before Harry's exams, Harry overheard a conversation between Voldemort and Quirrell, in which the Dark Lord ordered the Defence teacher to try to get the stone again. Potter mistook the conversation for an argument between Snape and Quirrell, because after the match with Slytherin he saw the Potions Master trying to intimidate Quirrell. </p><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/Harry-potter1-voldemort_forest.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170730190007" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-voldemort forest.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-voldemort_forest.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/Harry-potter1-voldemort_forest.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170730190007" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/Harry-potter1-voldemort_forest.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170730190007" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/Harry-potter1-voldemort_forest.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170730190007" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-voldemort forest.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-voldemort_forest.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/Harry-potter1-voldemort_forest.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170730190007" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter1-voldemort_forest.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Quirrell preparing to attack Harry in the Forbidden Forest</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>Voldemort, perfectly aware of Hagrid's love for <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magical</a> <a href="/wiki/Creature" title="Creature">creatures</a> from their school days and well knowing that Fluffy belonged to the half-giant, forced Quirrell to trick the Hogwarts groundskeeper into telling him how to get past the three-headed dog. One day at the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a>, a hooded Quirrell met Hagrid and enticed him into a card game with the wager of a <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">dragon</a> <a href="/wiki/Dragon_egg" title="Dragon egg">egg</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_27-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Hagrid assumed that the mysterious man was a dragon dealer and fellow dangerous creature enthusiast. Under the influence of a fair amount of mead, Hagrid divulged Quirrell that playing music for the Fluffy would put him to sleep.
</p><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Voldemort_and_Quirrell.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190331110253" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort and Quirrell.gif" data-image-key="Voldemort_and_Quirrell.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Voldemort_and_Quirrell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190331110253" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Voldemort_and_Quirrell.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190331110253" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Voldemort_and_Quirrell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190331110253" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort and Quirrell.gif" data-image-key="Voldemort_and_Quirrell.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Voldemort_and_Quirrell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190331110253" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_and_Quirrell.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Quirrell and Voldemort in confrontation, while in the underground chambers</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/4_June" title="4 June">4 June</a> <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, Voldemort ordered Quirrell to send a fake letter to Albus Dumbledore, asking him to go to the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic_Headquarters" title="British Ministry of Magic Headquarters">Ministry of Magic</a>. Voldemort moved forward with his goal, moving through the security barriers to the <a href="/wiki/Mirror_of_Erised" title="Mirror of Erised">Mirror of Erised</a>. Quirrell saw himself presenting the stone to his master, but could not figure out how to get it.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>See what I have become? Mere shadow and vapour ... I have form only when I can share another's body... but there have always been those willing to let me into their hearts and minds.... <a href="/wiki/Unicorn_blood" title="Unicorn blood">Unicorn blood</a> has strengthened me, these past weeks... you saw faithful Quirrell drinking it for me in the forest... and once I have the <a href="/wiki/Elixir_of_Life" title="Elixir of Life">Elixir of Life</a>, I will be able to create a body of my own.... Now... why don't you give me that Stone in your pocket?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort explaining to Harry his non-corporeal and parasitic state of existence<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Harry_Potter_touches_Quirrel_face.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140705040703" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="108" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter touches Quirrel face.gif" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_touches_Quirrel_face.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Harry_Potter_touches_Quirrel_face.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20140705040703" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Harry_Potter_touches_Quirrel_face.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140705040703" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Harry_Potter_touches_Quirrel_face.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20140705040703" decoding="async" width="220" height="108" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter touches Quirrel face.gif" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_touches_Quirrel_face.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Harry_Potter_touches_Quirrel_face.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20140705040703" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_touches_Quirrel_face.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Quirrell's death and Voldemort fled away</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>It was only when Harry arrived, believing he was protecting the Stone from Snape, that Voldemort saw a way to get it. Dumbledore would later say, <i>"Only those who wanted to find the stone, but not use it, could get it from the mirror."</i> Voldemort figured this out, and Quirrell attacked Harry. When he touched Harry, however, his hands blistered and burned. Harry placed his hands on Quirrell's face, severely injuring him. However, before Quirrell could harm Harry, Dumbledore appeared, and Voldemort's soul fled, killing Quirrell in the process. Voldemort returned to the Albanian forest, weaker than ever. He had to wait yet again for someone to help him.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Reopening_the_Chamber_of_Secrets">Reopening the Chamber of Secrets</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=20" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Reopening the Chamber of Secrets">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Reopening the Chamber of Secrets"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Voldemort</b>: "<i>Well, how is it that you — a skinny boy with no extraordinary magical talent — managed to defeat the greatest wizard of all time? How did you escape with nothing but a scar, while Lord Voldemort’s powers were destroyed?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry</b>: "<i>Why do you care how I escaped? Voldemort was after your time. . . .</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Voldemort</b>: "<i>Voldemort, is my past, present, and future, Harry Potter. . . .</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Voldemort revealing his true identity to Harry Potter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-12239.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151211144355" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="119" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-12239.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-12239.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-12239.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151211144355" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-12239.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151211144355" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-12239.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151211144355" decoding="async" width="250" height="119" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-12239.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-12239.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-12239.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151211144355" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2-movie-screencaps.com-12239.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Diary Riddle showing Harry Potter one of his memories</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Voldemort, after an unsuccessful attempt to steal the Philosopher's Stone, was still hiding in Albania, Lucius Malfoy was still into possession of his diary. In the summer of 1992, <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a> began conducting raids on several wizarding households to confiscate Dark or illegally enchanted objects under his recently proposed Muggle Protection Act. Before Malfoy Manor could be raided, Lucius sold several of his more incriminating possessions at Borgin and Burkes and set in motion the old task that Voldemort assigned him which involved reopening the Chamber of Secrets. At <a href="/wiki/Flourish_and_Blotts" title="Flourish and Blotts">Flourish and Blotts</a> Malfoy planted the diary on eleven-year-old <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, who brought it to Hogwarts. By doing this, he hoped to kill two birds with one stone: he would rid himself of any ties connecting to the Dark Arts and he would discredit Arthur Weasley. Ginny began writing in it, and found that a sixteen-year-old Tom Riddle was answering. She found comfort in the diary, confiding it with her worries, not knowing she was being manipulated. Riddle would always have sympathy. The diary slowly drained the life and energy from Ginny, transferring it to itself. Under the diary's control, Ginny re-opened the Chamber of Secrets and released the basilisk, which <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrified</a> several students. While possessed, she also killed Hagrid's roosters and wrote threatening messages on the school corridors in rooster blood. Ginny became upset and confused, knowing that the diary was doing something to her, and tried to flush it down the toilet in Moaning Myrtle's bathroom. Harry and Ginny's brother <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> accidentally stumbled upon it, and Harry began communicating with the diary.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>  
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/52/Harry_destroying_Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140429000617" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry destroying Tom Riddle&#39;s Diary GIF.gif" data-image-key="Harry_destroying_Tom_Riddle&#39;s_Diary_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/52/Harry_destroying_Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140429000617" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/52/Harry_destroying_Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140429000617" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/52/Harry_destroying_Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140429000617" decoding="async" width="245" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry destroying Tom Riddle&#39;s Diary GIF.gif" data-image-key="Harry_destroying_Tom_Riddle&#39;s_Diary_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/52/Harry_destroying_Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140429000617" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_destroying_Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary_GIF.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry destroys Tom Riddle's diary with a <a href="/wiki/Basilisk" title="Basilisk">Basilisk</a> fang</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Ginny saw that Harry had the diary, she stole it back for she did not want Harry to find out all the things she had written in the diary, or what she had done while under its influence. When this piece of Voldemort's soul was ready to take his physical form from Ginny's life, the diary lured her into the Chamber while ignoring her pleas and cries for mercy. Harry found Ginny in time and destroyed the basilisk with <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Godric Gryffindor's Sword</a>. <a href="/wiki/Fawkes" title="Fawkes">Fawkes</a> also arrived, summoned by Harry's profound devotion and loyalty to Dumbledore.
</p><p>This encounter and Horcrux is what revealed Voldemort's past as "Tom Marvolo Riddle" to Harry. At first, Harry thought he was an ally, and asked him to help. Then, when revealing his future identity to Harry, Riddle implied that he wanted to kill Harry in revenge for destroying him over even continuing Salazar Slytherin's wish of purging the school of Muggle-borns. Instinctively, Harry used the basilisk's fang to stab the diary, thinking it would destroy its dark power.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_7-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Not only was the diary destroyed, but Harry also unknowingly destroyed one of Voldemort's Horcruxes.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> As Dumbledore surmised, the shard of Voldemort's soul that contained his core identity was still in hiding in Albania and remained unaware of these occurances for at least another year and a half.
</p>
<h3><span id="Return_to_full_strength_(1994-1995)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_full_strength_.281994-1995.29">Return to full strength <span class="template-c">(1994-1995)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=21" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Return to full strength (1994-1995)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Return to full strength (1994-1995)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>"I have my reasons for using the boy, as I have already explained to you, and I will use no other. I have waited thirteen years. A few more months will make no difference. As for the protection surrounding the boy, I believe my plan will be effective. All that is needed is a little courage from you, Wormtail -- courage you will find, unless you wish to feel the full extent of Lord Voldemort's wrath --</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort informing Wormtail of his plot to murder to Harry Potter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gathering_the_old_comrades">Gathering the old comrades</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=22" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Gathering the old comrades">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Gathering the old comrades"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/55/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14268.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150914145552" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="117" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14268.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14268.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/55/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14268.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150914145552" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/55/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14268.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150914145552" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/55/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14268.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150914145552" decoding="async" width="250" height="117" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14268.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14268.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/55/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14268.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150914145552" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14268.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Peter Pettigrew holding a weakened and immobile Voldemort</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the summer of 1994, when Voldemort had all but given up hope of obtaining any help from his former servants, Peter Pettigrew, also known as "Wormtail," who had faked his own death years earlier and hid from authorities in his <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> form of a rat, travelled to Albania. Wormtail, tired of travelling and hungry, decided to eat something in an inn near the forest in which Voldemort was hiding. He was found there by <a href="/wiki/Bertha_Jorkins" title="Bertha Jorkins">Bertha Jorkins</a>, a <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> worker, who was on holiday in Albania. Although she recognised Peter, Pettigrew lured her into Voldemort's forest hideout and overpowered her, before handing her over to the Dark Lord. Upon torturing her, Voldemort was surprised to find that someone had put a powerful <a href="/wiki/Memory_Charm" title="Memory Charm">Memory Charm</a> on her. After breaking the charm, Voldemort learned from her that this year the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a> would be held at Hogwarts and that <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, an ex-Auror, will teach Defence Against the Dark Arts. She also revealed to him that <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Bartemius Crouch Jnr</a>, one of his loyal Death Eaters, who had been imprisoned in Azkaban after his fall and was thought to be dead, is alive. <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Senior" title="Bartemius Crouch Senior">Bartemius Crouch Snr</a> was concealing his son at his home after helping him escape prison. Jorkins had stumbled upon Crouch Jnr at his house, and Crouch Snr placed a Memory Charm on her so that she would not report it.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Voldemort, unable to possess her body and mind, which were damaged by the spells he cast, murdered her. Voldemort, knowing also that Wormtail had been deemed dead by the wizarding community, and would have attracted too much attention, didn't possess his body as well. Together, they built a rudimentary body that Voldemort used for travel and performing magic. While in this form, Voldemort was forced to drink a <a href="/wiki/Rudimentary_body_potion" title="Rudimentary body potion">Rudimentary body potion</a> made from <a href="/wiki/Unicorn_blood" title="Unicorn blood">unicorn blood</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nagini%27s_venom" title="Nagini&#39;s venom">venom</a> from <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Snake" title="Snake">snake</a> he befriended, to sustain his life. At some point, after Jorkin’s murder, he turned Nagini into his last Horcrux, believing his soul being in seven pieces.
</p><p>Knowing that Dumbledore was sure to have seen to it that the Philosopher's Stone was destroyed, Voldemort knew he would not be able to use the Elixir of Life to create a new body for himself.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF33_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF33-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> Voldemort decided to attempt an old piece of ritualistic Dark Magic to create a potion that would restore him to a body. He made plans to travel to England in order to obtain two of the three key ingredients: a bone from his father and the blood of his most hated enemy, Harry Potter. The third ingredient, the flesh of a servant willingly given, he would obtain from Wormtail himself.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5d/Voldemortbaby.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100806083453" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="181" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemortbaby.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemortbaby.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5d/Voldemortbaby.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100806083453" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5d/Voldemortbaby.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100806083453" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5d/Voldemortbaby.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100806083453" decoding="async" width="220" height="181" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemortbaby.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemortbaby.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5d/Voldemortbaby.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100806083453" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemortbaby.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort plotting to use Harry Potter to facilitate his return before killing him</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Returning to the <a href="/wiki/Riddle_House" title="Riddle House">Riddle House</a> in <a href="/wiki/Little_Hangleton" title="Little Hangleton">Little Hangleton</a>, Voldemort set his sights on finally killing Harry Potter. He considered kidnapping Harry during the <a href="/wiki/1994_Quidditch_World_Cup" title="1994 Quidditch World Cup">422nd</a> <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_World_Cup" title="Quidditch World Cup">Quidditch World Cup</a>, where protection from his <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">relatives</a> and Dumbledore would not be so effective, but he was not strong enough to do it with the whole horde of Ministry employees running about, and instead began to concoct a plan to have the boy delivered to him instead, which lead to <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Bartemius Crouch</a>'s infiltration of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> under the guise of the far-famed <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, whom he eventually learned that Albus Dumbledore had persuaded to come out of retirement to fill the role of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher for the <a href="/wiki/1994-1995_school_year" class="mw-redirect" title="1994-1995 school year">1994-1995 school year</a>. 
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>But I am not a man, Muggle. I am much, much more than a man. However...why not? I will face you...Wormtail, come turn my chair around.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort revealing himself to Frank Bryce, before murdering him<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0f/Frank_Bryce_murder.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007233603" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="80" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Frank Bryce murder.gif" data-image-key="Frank_Bryce_murder.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0f/Frank_Bryce_murder.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161007233603" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0f/Frank_Bryce_murder.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007233603" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0f/Frank_Bryce_murder.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161007233603" decoding="async" width="180" height="80" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Frank Bryce murder.gif" data-image-key="Frank_Bryce_murder.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0f/Frank_Bryce_murder.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161007233603" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Frank_Bryce_murder.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort murdering Frank Bryce with the <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As they were discussing their plans, Voldemort and Wormtail were unaware that a Muggle caretaker of the Riddle House, <a href="/wiki/Frank_Bryce" title="Frank Bryce">Frank Bryce</a>, who has been suspected by the villagers for the murder of the Riddle family for a half of a century, had been standing behind the door eavesdropping on their plans. When Nagini arrived in the corridor and spotted him, she informed Voldemort in Parseltongue about his presence. Voldemort invited him into the room and after a short conversation he killed him for overhearing their plan.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Eve_of_war">Eve of war</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=23" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Eve of war">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Eve of war"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>During the Quidditch World Cup, Barty Crouch Jnr escaped from his father's enchantments and cast the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a>, but was quickly recaptured again. Voldemort and Wormtail went to the Crouch estate, where Voldemort placed Crouch Snr under the Imperius Curse and freed Crouch Jnr for good.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Voldemort ordered Crouch Jnr and Pettigrew to capture Moody at <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody%27s_house" title="Alastor Moody&#39;s house">his home</a>. When they did it, Crouch placed Moody under Imperius Curse and created <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> which he used to impersonate Moody for the entire school year. He influenced the Tournament for months, ensuring that Harry would be the one to get to the Triwizard Cup first which, unbeknownst to anyone, was a <a href="/wiki/Portkey" title="Portkey">Portkey</a>. Meanwhile Voldemort returned to the Crouch estate with Wormtail, where they ordered Crouch Snr to continue about his business as usual.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Crouch Snr started to show signs of resisting the Imperius Curse, Voldemort decided it was no longer safe to allow him to leave the house, and instead made him stay home under the presumption of being sick. In late <a href="/wiki/May" title="May">May</a> of <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> Crouch Snr continued to fight through Voldemort's control and eventually escaped due to Wormtail's negligence.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Voldemort quickly alerted Crouch Jnr to stop his father at all costs as he surmised that Crouch was intending to tell Dumbledore all about his past actions and Voldemort's plans. Upon Jnr's success, Voldemort spared Pettigrew from being given to  Nagini as meat instead opting to punish him with the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Duel_in_Little_Hangleton">Duel in Little Hangleton</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=24" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Duel in Little Hangleton">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Duel in Little Hangleton"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>And then I ask myself, but how could they have believed I would not rise again? They, who knew the steps I took, long ago, to guard myself against mortal death? They, who had seen proofs of the immensity of my power in the times when I was mightier than any wizard living?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort expressing his resentment towards his Death Eaters<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Pettigrew_voldemort.png/revision/latest?cb=20170814150547" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pettigrew voldemort.png" data-image-key="Pettigrew_voldemort.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Pettigrew_voldemort.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170814150547" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Pettigrew_voldemort.png/revision/latest?cb=20170814150547" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Pettigrew_voldemort.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170814150547" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pettigrew voldemort.png" data-image-key="Pettigrew_voldemort.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Pettigrew_voldemort.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170814150547" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pettigrew_voldemort.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pettigrew prepares to place Voldemort inside the cauldron</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/24_June" title="24 June">24 June</a> 1995, Harry, in the spirit of sportsmanship, requested <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric Diggory</a> to tie with him for the win. When they both touched the Portkey, they were transported to a <a href="/wiki/Little_Hangleton_graveyard" title="Little Hangleton graveyard">Little Hangleton graveyard</a> where Wormtail and Voldemort were waiting. Under Voldemort's orders, Pettigrew murdered Cedric with the Killing Curse and went on to have Harry tightly bound and gagged to the <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_Gravestone" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s Gravestone">Riddle family tombstone</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Rebirth_of_Voldemort_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110820035948" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rebirth of Voldemort GIF.gif" data-image-key="Rebirth_of_Voldemort_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Rebirth_of_Voldemort_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20110820035948" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Rebirth_of_Voldemort_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110820035948" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Rebirth_of_Voldemort_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20110820035948" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rebirth of Voldemort GIF.gif" data-image-key="Rebirth_of_Voldemort_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Rebirth_of_Voldemort_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20110820035948" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rebirth_of_Voldemort_GIF.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort's rebirth</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Wormtail had placed Voldemort's rudimentary body into a cauldron containing the near finished potion, he added the first two ingredients, one of which was his hand, causing it to turn from a poisonous-looking blue to burning red before he proceeded to obtain Harry's blood and added it to the <a href="/wiki/Regeneration_potion" title="Regeneration potion">potion</a> for his master's <a href="/wiki/Return_of_Lord_Voldemort" title="Return of Lord Voldemort">rebirth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Once the final ingredient was added, the potion turned blinding white, sending out bright sparks as it simmered before dying down and a thick white steam issued from the cauldron: the ritual was now complete, Voldemort regained his physical body, and emerged from the cauldron. Calling on Wormtail to robe him, the reborn Dark Lord took some time examining his body and getting reaccustomed to it. Then he called for his servant to show him his arm and used the now activated <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a> to summon his Death Eaters.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>I remember only forcing myself, sleeplessly, endlessly, second by second, to exist. ... I settled in a faraway place, in <a href="/wiki/Black_Forest" title="Black Forest">a forest</a>, and I waited. . . . Surely, one of my faithful Death Eaters would try and find me. . . one of them would come and perform the magic I could not, to restore me to a body . . , but I waited in vain. ...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort admonishing his Death Eaters for failing to resurrect him sooner<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14816.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190817204246" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14816.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14816.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14816.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190817204246" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14816.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190817204246" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14816.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190817204246" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14816.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14816.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14816.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190817204246" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-14816.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort confronting <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> over his lack of faith in his eventual return</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Those who were perhaps most loyal to him, save for those who willingly went to Azkaban in his name, appeared. Voldemort welcomed them before he scorned them for believing him to be dead and informed them that he would expect better of them now that he had returned. The Dark Lord told the Death Eaters of the events that had led to his first downfall, his years in hiding before he tried to steal the Philosopher's Stone by possessing Quirrell and eventual defeat before finally of how Pettigrew had located him, and they set out to orchestrate his resurrection. He rewarded Wormtail by constructing a silver hand.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>You have been taught how to duel. Harry Potter? We bow to each other. Harry, Come, the niceties must be observed. . . .Dumbledore would like you to show manners. . . . Bow to death, Harry. ... I said, bow, Very good, And now you face me, like a man . . . straight-backed and proud, the way your father died. . . .</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort preparing to duel Harry Potter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 230px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Duel_graveyard.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190324225041" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="228" height="129" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Duel graveyard.gif" data-image-key="Duel_graveyard.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Duel_graveyard.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/228?cb=20190324225041" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Duel_graveyard.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190324225041" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Duel_graveyard.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/228?cb=20190324225041" decoding="async" width="228" height="129" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Duel graveyard.gif" data-image-key="Duel_graveyard.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Duel_graveyard.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/228?cb=20190324225041" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Duel_graveyard.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort <a href="/wiki/Duel_in_Little_Hangleton" title="Duel in Little Hangleton">duels</a> Harry in a battle of wills, echoes appear as a result of <i><a href="/wiki/Reverse_Spell" title="Reverse Spell">Priori Incantatem</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>Voldemort then set his attention on Harry, and began to mock and humiliate the boy before the Death Eaters. He then had Harry untied so he could force the young wizard into a duel where the Dark Lord had a greater advantage over Harry. After inflicting the Cruciatus Curse several times and the Imperius Curse on Harry, Voldemort was ready to end the one sided duel and kill Harry once and for all. Yet as Voldemort cast <i>Avada Kedavra,</i> Harry simultaneously cast <i><a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Expelliarmus</a></i> and their twin-core wands became locked in <a href="/wiki/Reverse_Spell" title="Reverse Spell">Priori Incantatem</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>People who had been killed by Voldemort's wand came out as spectral visions: First, Diggory, next Bryce, then Jorkins, and followed by Lily and James Potter. They encouraged Harry, while distracting Voldemort. Harry pulled away and had enough time to grab Cedric's body and the Triwizard Cup to return to Hogwarts infuriating Voldemort who had lost his chance at killing Harry right then and there which resulted in Harry alerting Dumbledore to Voldemort's return which then created obvious obstacles in his plans to regain his power over the Wizarding World.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Back at Hogwarts, Crouch Jnr was  discovered by Dumbledore and Harry but was subjected to the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a> before he could be put on trial before the Wizengamot.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Thus, the only knowledge of Voldemort's return was Harry's word, which was vigorously disputed by the Ministry of Magic. Voldemort was able to grow in power in secret,<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> concentrating on recruiting many wizards as well as the giants to his side in addition to stealing the full record of the prophecy regarding himself and Harry.
</p>
<h3><span id="Second_Wizarding_War_(1995-1998)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_Wizarding_War_.281995-1998.29">Second Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1995-1998)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=25" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Second Wizarding War (1995-1998)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Second Wizarding War (1995-1998)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
