<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bid_for_the_Prophecy">Bid for the Prophecy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=26" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Bid for the Prophecy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Bid for the Prophecy"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In 1995, Dumbledore reconvened the Order of the Phoenix once more, using Sirius Black's family home at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> as headquarters. Harry, Ron and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> set up a similar organisation at Hogwarts called <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, which was originally created to thwart the Ministry's meddling at the school under <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 172px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/eb/Daily_prophet_the_boy_who_lies.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140530153226" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="170" height="269" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Daily prophet the boy who lies.jpg" data-image-key="Daily_prophet_the_boy_who_lies.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/eb/Daily_prophet_the_boy_who_lies.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20140530153226" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/eb/Daily_prophet_the_boy_who_lies.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140530153226" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/eb/Daily_prophet_the_boy_who_lies.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20140530153226" decoding="async" width="170" height="269" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Daily prophet the boy who lies.jpg" data-image-key="Daily_prophet_the_boy_who_lies.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/eb/Daily_prophet_the_boy_who_lies.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20140530153226" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Daily_prophet_the_boy_who_lies.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> article showing the Ministry trying to libel Harry Potter and anyone who believed him</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Thanks to the Ministry's denial of Voldemort's return and the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a>'s</i> smear campaign against Dumbledore and Harry, the general public was left unaware and ignorant of his presence, making it easy for his operations to run smoothly and without interference. Eventually,  Voldemort travelled to Azkaban and freed several of his most loyal Death Eaters, such as <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>. Voldemort had little trouble with this, as many of the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> were happy to obey him. The Dark wizards returned to his side thereafter.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f1/Azkaban_escape.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190416165532" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Azkaban escape.gif" data-image-key="Azkaban_escape.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f1/Azkaban_escape.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190416165532" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f1/Azkaban_escape.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190416165532" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f1/Azkaban_escape.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190416165532" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Azkaban escape.gif" data-image-key="Azkaban_escape.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f1/Azkaban_escape.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190416165532" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Azkaban_escape.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort breaks Azkaban's gates</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort's first attempt at securing the prophecy was to have Malfoy put Order member <a href="/wiki/Sturgis_Podmore" title="Sturgis Podmore">Sturgis Podmore</a> under the Imperius Curse and send him to take the prophecy. However, Sturgis was unable to get into the Department of Mysteries. 
</p><p>His next attempt was to use the Imperius Curse on an <a href="/wiki/Unspeakable" title="Unspeakable">Unspeakable</a> named <a href="/wiki/Broderick_Bode" title="Broderick Bode">Broderick Bode</a>. He was ordered to retrieve the prophecy, but was seriously injured in the process and was put into a permanent ward at <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a>. From this, Voldemort learned that the only people who could retrieve a prophecy are the people who are included in the prophecy. Voldemort could not risk going into the Ministry himself, so he used a <a href="/wiki/Mind-reading" title="Mind-reading">telepathic</a> link through Harry's scar to cause him to go there instead.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=27" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Department of Mysteries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Battle of the Department of Mysteries"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>You do not seek to kill me, Dumbledore? Above such brutality, are you?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort duelling with Albus Dumbledore<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/False_vision_-_Voldemort_tortures_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190817234257" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="False vision - Voldemort tortures Sirius Black.jpg" data-image-key="False_vision_-_Voldemort_tortures_Sirius_Black.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/False_vision_-_Voldemort_tortures_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190817234257" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/False_vision_-_Voldemort_tortures_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190817234257" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/False_vision_-_Voldemort_tortures_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190817234257" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="False vision - Voldemort tortures Sirius Black.jpg" data-image-key="False_vision_-_Voldemort_tortures_Sirius_Black.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/False_vision_-_Voldemort_tortures_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190817234257" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:False_vision_-_Voldemort_tortures_Sirius_Black.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort's false vision of torturing Sirius Black</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Members of Dumbledore's Army, including Harry, Hermione, Ron, Ginny, Neville, and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> went to the Department of Mysteries seeking to rescue Sirius Black, whom they believed to be trapped there. Harry wound up retrieving the prophecy from its shelf. At once, Death Eaters appeared, demanding Harry hand over the prophecy. Dumbledore's Army fought back, and during the battle that ensued, the prophecy was destroyed. Voldemort was forced to come to the Ministry, but upon learning of its destruction he tried to murder Harry.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190324225454" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore and Voldemort duel.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190324225454" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190324225454" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190324225454" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore and Voldemort duel.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190324225454" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_and_Voldemort_duel.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort duels Dumbledore in 1996 after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort's attempt was foiled by Dumbledore, and a <a href="/wiki/Duel_in_the_Ministry_Atrium" title="Duel in the Ministry Atrium">fantastic duel</a> ensued. Despite Voldemort's overwhelming magical abilities, much to his great frustration, Dumbledore managed to hold his own against the Dark Lord, calmly avoiding and deflecting Voldemort‘s barrage of attacks while also maintaining the offensive. Though he deflected all of Dumbledore attempts to contain him, and even managed to nearly kill his former teacher, Voldemort was eventually trapped in an orb of water that he was forced to Disapparate out of. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 196px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Voldemort_posseses_Harry_Potter.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190209120222" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="194" height="123" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort posseses Harry Potter.gif" data-image-key="Voldemort_posseses_Harry_Potter.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Voldemort_posseses_Harry_Potter.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/194?cb=20190209120222" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Voldemort_posseses_Harry_Potter.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190209120222" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Voldemort_posseses_Harry_Potter.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/194?cb=20190209120222" decoding="async" width="194" height="123" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort posseses Harry Potter.gif" data-image-key="Voldemort_posseses_Harry_Potter.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/44/Voldemort_posseses_Harry_Potter.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/194?cb=20190209120222" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_posseses_Harry_Potter.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry possessed by Voldemort</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort then attempted to possess Harry instead, hoping Dumbledore would kill the boy in an attempt to destroy Voldemort himself, but Harry's heart, full of grief over the loss of his godfather Sirius, was able to force Voldemort out of his mind. With both the loss of the prophecy and his failure to kill Harry and defeat Dumbledore, Voldemort aborted his mission, dragging Bellatrix along as he fled, but not before <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> and the other Ministry officials arrived, witnessing for themselves that the Dark Lord had, in fact, returned. After a year of operating secretly, Lord Voldemort's cover was now blown and the remaining Death Eaters incapacitated by the Order, including Lucius, were taken into custody and sent to Azkaban.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime following this, Voldemort would secretly engage in a sexual relationship with Bellatrix Lestrange. Out of this union would be born their daughter <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a>, who would be given over to be raised by the Rowle family, a family sworn to Voldemort.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> At another point, Voldemort discovered that Malfoy had been careless with the diary Horcrux and it had been destroyed, leaving Voldemort highly furious.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_start_of_open_war">The start of open war</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=28" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The start of open war">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: The start of open war"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>I have been careless, and so have been thwarted by luck and chance, those wreckers of all but the best-laid plans. But I know better now. I understand those things that I did not understand before. I must be the one to kill Harry Potter, and I shall be.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort discuses Harry Potter's triumphs and his own failures<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 170px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/He_who_must_be_not_be_named_returns.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140705195506" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="168" height="267" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="He who must be not be named returns.jpg" data-image-key="He_who_must_be_not_be_named_returns.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/He_who_must_be_not_be_named_returns.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/168?cb=20140705195506" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/He_who_must_be_not_be_named_returns.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140705195506" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/He_who_must_be_not_be_named_returns.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/168?cb=20140705195506" decoding="async" width="168" height="267" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="He who must be not be named returns.jpg" data-image-key="He_who_must_be_not_be_named_returns.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/He_who_must_be_not_be_named_returns.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/168?cb=20140705195506" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:He_who_must_be_not_be_named_returns.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> confirms Voldemort's return</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With Voldemort no longer needing to keep his actions silent, the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> had begun. The Dementors left Azkaban to side with the Dark Lord, who could offer them more scope for their powers. As a result, there were many attacks by Voldemort's army. Mass Muggle killings were rampant; what was claimed to be a hurricane to the Muggle world was in fact a rampage by the <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giants</a>, whom Voldemort had drawn into allegiance. Voldemort himself duelled and killed <a href="/wiki/Amelia_Bones" title="Amelia Bones">Amelia Bones</a>, the Head of the Department of Magical Law Enforcement, who was described as having put up a good fight against him and as one of the greatest witches of the age.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Dementor attacks were daily, the effect on the Muggles manifested in severe depression and grim weather. Voldemort attempted to blackmail <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, and when he stood his ground, the Dark Lord initiated the destruction of the <a href="/wiki/Brockdale_Bridge" title="Brockdale Bridge">Brockdale Bridge</a>, sending at least twelve cars into the water.
</p><p>In July 1996, Voldemort required a spy within Hogwarts and inducted Lucius Malfoy's son <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco</a> as a Death Eater. He ordered Draco to kill Dumbledore, for he wished to punish Lucius for his failings by giving his son a task he could not do. If Draco failed, he would meet terrible consequences. However, Draco was able to sneak a group of Death Eaters into Hogwarts through a pair of Vanishing Cabinets that connected Borgin and Burkes with the Room of Requirement. The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> ensued.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Voldemort's plans were carried out when Snape used the Killing Curse on Dumbledore, as Draco himself was unable to bring himself to commit murder despite the threat he was under. Although the Death Eaters fled Hogwarts, the intrusion of the castle signified that there was no longer a single place safe from the Dark Lord.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor">Meeting at Malfoy Manor</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=29" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Meeting at Malfoy Manor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Meeting at Malfoy Manor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Meeting at Malfoy Manor">Meeting at Malfoy Manor</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>For those of you who do not know, we are joined here tonight by Charity Burbage who, until recently, taught at Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry. Yes . . . Professor Burbage taught the children of witches and wizards all about Muggles . . . how they are not so different from us . . . Not content with corrupting and polluting the minds of Wizarding children, last week Professor Burbage wrote an impassioned defence of Mudbloods in the Daily Prophet. Wizards, she says, must accept these thieves of their knowledge and magic. The dwindling of the purebloods is, says Professor Burbage, a most desirable circumstance. . . . She would have us all mate with Muggles . . . or, no doubt, werewolves. . . .</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort tormenting Charity Burbage before murdering her<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2f/Voldemort_kills_Burbage.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190819223348" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort kills Burbage.gif" data-image-key="Voldemort_kills_Burbage.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2f/Voldemort_kills_Burbage.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190819223348" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2f/Voldemort_kills_Burbage.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190819223348" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2f/Voldemort_kills_Burbage.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190819223348" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort kills Burbage.gif" data-image-key="Voldemort_kills_Burbage.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2f/Voldemort_kills_Burbage.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190819223348" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_kills_Burbage.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort killing Charity Burbage during the meeting held at Malfoy Manor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort took over <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a> as his headquarters. During the summer of <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, he captured the Hogwarts Professor of <a href="/wiki/Muggle_Studies" title="Muggle Studies">Muggle Studies</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charity_Burbage" title="Charity Burbage">Charity Burbage</a>, and killed her during a meeting with his Death Eaters before feeding her to <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>. Voldemort also imprisoned and interrogated the kidnapped wandmaker, Garrick Ollivander, about why his wand could not duel against Harry's. Ollivander revealed that their wands shared the same core, and would not work properly against each other. This came as a great relief to Voldemort, who worried that Harry had escaped from him in the graveyard by superior skill. Ollivander told Voldemort that he merely needed another's wand, and so he took Lucius Malfoy's. This served as a way to punish and demean the Malfoy family. At this point, he was nearly ready to conquer the Ministry, while insisting that <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a> must be surrounded entirely before he made his next move.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=30" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Seven Potters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Battle of the Seven Potters"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>He felt Voldemort before he saw him. Looking sideways, he stared into the red eyes and was sure they would be the last thing he ever saw: Voldemort preparing to curse him once more — </i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort attempting to murder Harry Potter during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/02/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140408223005" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Battle of the Seven Potters.gif" data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/02/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140408223005" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/02/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140408223005" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/02/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140408223005" decoding="async" width="245" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Battle of the Seven Potters.gif" data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/02/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140408223005" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry Potter's wand acting of its own accord against Voldemort during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">sky battle</a>, destroying the borrowed wand</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/27_July" title="27 July">27 July</a> 1997, when Harry left <a href="/wiki/4_Privet_Drive" title="4 Privet Drive">4 Privet Drive</a> for the final time, Voldemort flew to the scene with his Death Eaters to fight the Order of the Phoenix. In the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">ensuing battle</a>, Voldemort murdered Alastor Moody. When he attempted to attack Harry, Harry's wand acted of its own accord, releasing golden fire at him and destroying Malfoy's wand. Before Voldemort could react, Harry reached the protection of the home of <a href="/wiki/Edward_Tonks" title="Edward Tonks">Ted</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andromeda_Tonks" title="Andromeda Tonks">Andromeda Tonks</a>, and Voldemort was forced to retreat.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 191px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Voldemort_tortures_Garrick_Ollivander.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190817172458" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="189" height="77" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort tortures Garrick Ollivander.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort_tortures_Garrick_Ollivander.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Voldemort_tortures_Garrick_Ollivander.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/189?cb=20190817172458" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Voldemort_tortures_Garrick_Ollivander.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190817172458" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Voldemort_tortures_Garrick_Ollivander.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/189?cb=20190817172458" decoding="async" width="189" height="77" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort tortures Garrick Ollivander.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort_tortures_Garrick_Ollivander.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Voldemort_tortures_Garrick_Ollivander.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/189?cb=20190817172458" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_tortures_Garrick_Ollivander.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort torturing Ollivander</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort returned to his headquarters at Malfoy Manor and, accompanied by Peter Pettigrew, accused Ollivander of deliberately misleading him and tortured him with the Cruciatus Curse. Ollivander told him truthfully that never in wandlore has he ever heard of such a thing happening between two wands. Voldemort ordered Ollivander to tell him everything he knew about the legendary wand known as the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ministry_take-over">Ministry take-over</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=31" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ministry take-over">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Ministry take-over"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Fall_of_the_Ministry_of_Magic" title="Fall of the Ministry of Magic">Fall of the Ministry of Magic</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>The Ministry has fallen. Scrimgeour is dead. They are coming.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Kingsley Shacklebolt warning the Order of the Phoenix<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Thicknesse_regime.png/revision/latest?cb=20170103025010" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="188" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Thicknesse regime.png" data-image-key="Thicknesse_regime.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Thicknesse_regime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170103025010" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Thicknesse_regime.png/revision/latest?cb=20170103025010" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Thicknesse_regime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170103025010" decoding="async" width="250" height="188" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Thicknesse regime.png" data-image-key="Thicknesse_regime.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Thicknesse_regime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170103025010" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Thicknesse_regime.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The officials and the <a href="/wiki/Pius_Thicknesse" title="Pius Thicknesse">puppet minister</a> that Voldemort installed to run the Ministry and enforce the new regime</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Shortly after this, the Ministry of Magic was compromised and fell to the power of Voldemort when Minister <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a> was tortured for information and murdered, with the official version being that he retired. News of this came to the Order of the Phoenix during the wedding of <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a> at the Burrow due to <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a>.
</p><p>Voldemort established a totalitarian police state, with <a href="/wiki/Pius_Thicknesse" title="Pius Thicknesse">Pius Thicknesse</a>, under the Imperius Curse, serving as a puppet Minister for Magic and Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Corban Yaxley</a> as the Head of the Department of Magical Law Enforcement. The <a href="/wiki/Muggle-Born_Registration_Commission" title="Muggle-Born Registration Commission">Muggle-Born Registration Commission</a> was created to round up Muggle-borns and imprison them in Azkaban. Harry Potter was declared <a href="/wiki/Undesirable" title="Undesirable">Undesirable</a> No. 1 with a reward on his head, on the basis he was wanted for questioning over the death of Dumbledore. Seveurs Snape, meanwhile, took over as Headmaster of Hogwarts, while Death Eater siblings <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto Carrow</a> became teachers.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Voldemort placed a <a href="/wiki/Taboo" title="Taboo">Taboo</a> Curse on his name which enabled his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> to instantly locate anyone who spoke it out loud in the open. Voldemort chose not to publicly declare himself Minister of Magic in order to maintain an atmosphere of fear and uncertainty.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_search_for_the_Elder_Wand">The search for the Elder Wand</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=32" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The search for the Elder Wand">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: The search for the Elder Wand"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Mission_For_The_Elder_Wand" class="mw-redirect" title="Mission For The Elder Wand">Mission For The Elder Wand</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Kill me then, Voldemort!... That wand will never, ever be yours!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Grindelwald confronting Voldemort in Nurmengard<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Voldemort_killing_Gregorovitch.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20190817172720" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort killing Gregorovitch.JPG" data-image-key="Voldemort_killing_Gregorovitch.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Voldemort_killing_Gregorovitch.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190817172720" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Voldemort_killing_Gregorovitch.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20190817172720" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Voldemort_killing_Gregorovitch.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190817172720" decoding="async" width="220" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort killing Gregorovitch.JPG" data-image-key="Voldemort_killing_Gregorovitch.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Voldemort_killing_Gregorovitch.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190817172720" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_killing_Gregorovitch.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort interrogating Gregorovitch, seconds before killing him</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With his servants taking care of business in Britain, Voldemort travelled to <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> to seek out the acclaimed wandmaker <a href="/wiki/Mykew_Gregorovitch" title="Mykew Gregorovitch">Mykew Gregorovitch</a> and obtain the Elder Wand. Eventually, after murdering several people who got in his way, Voldemort found him, but was informed that the wand had been stolen. Voldemort performed Legilimency on Gregorovitch and saw the memory of a young blond boy who stole the wand. Voldemort demanded to know the identity of the thief, but when Gregorovitch didn't know it, Voldemort killed him.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20190817172422" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort and Grindelwald.JPG" data-image-key="Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190817172422" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20190817172422" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190817172422" decoding="async" width="220" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort and Grindelwald.JPG" data-image-key="Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190817172422" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort interrogating Grindelwald, seconds before killing him</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/24_December" title="24 December">Christmas Eve</a> of <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Nagini summoned Voldemort to <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a>, where Harry and Hermione Granger were visiting the graves of Harry's parents and investigating the possibility that <a href="/wiki/Bathilda_Bagshot" title="Bathilda Bagshot">Bathilda Bagshot</a> might have the Sword of Gryffindor. Harry and Hermione barely managed to escape. However, Voldemort found a picture of the aforementioned blond boy at Bagshot's home; this boy turned out to be none other than Dark wizard <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, whom Dumbledore had defeated in 1945.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 233px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/DH1_Voldemort_testing_the_Elder_Wand.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190207203409" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="231" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH1 Voldemort testing the Elder Wand.gif" data-image-key="DH1_Voldemort_testing_the_Elder_Wand.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/DH1_Voldemort_testing_the_Elder_Wand.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/231?cb=20190207203409" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/DH1_Voldemort_testing_the_Elder_Wand.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190207203409" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/DH1_Voldemort_testing_the_Elder_Wand.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/231?cb=20190207203409" decoding="async" width="231" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 Voldemort testing the Elder Wand.gif" data-image-key="DH1_Voldemort_testing_the_Elder_Wand.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/DH1_Voldemort_testing_the_Elder_Wand.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/231?cb=20190207203409" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_Voldemort_testing_the_Elder_Wand.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort <a href="/wiki/Lightning_spell" title="Lightning spell">testing</a> the Elder Wand's power after removing it from Dumbledore's tomb</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/March" title="March">March</a> of <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, Voldemort travelled to <a href="/wiki/Austria" title="Austria">Austria</a> and broke into <a href="/wiki/Nurmengard_Castle" title="Nurmengard Castle">Nurmengard</a> prison, where Grindelwald was being held, and demanded to know the location of the Elder Wand. Grindelwald baffled Voldemort by being completely unafraid of him and saying that he welcomed death. Voldemort then murdered him in a rage without gaining any information.
</p><p>At that moment, <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> summoned him by pressing the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a>. Harry Potter had accidentally broken the Taboo an hour prior, and he and his friends, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, were captured by a group of <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a> led by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>, and were brought to <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a>. He departed Germany to end Harry's life, but before he could arrive, they managed to escape with the assistance of <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elf</a> <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a>. The arriving Voldemort caused physical harm for Bellatrix and the Malfoys, and forbade them to leave the manor as punishment.
</p><p>Shortly after this, Voldemort deduced that Dumbledore, who had defeated Grindelwald, had won the Elder Wand. Voldemort then went to Hogwarts, where he met with Snape and proceeded to break into Dumbledore's tomb and thus stole the Elder Wand.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Learning_of_the_Horcrux_Hunt">Learning of the <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter%27s_Horcrux_Hunt" title="Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter&#39;s Horcrux Hunt">Horcrux Hunt</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=33" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Learning of the Horcrux Hunt">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Learning of the Horcrux Hunt"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Say it again! Say it again! Impostors? What impostors? I thought Gringotts had <a href="/wiki/Thief%27s_Downfall" title="Thief&#39;s Downfall">ways</a> of revealing impostors? Who were they? And they took? Tell me! </i>What did they take<i>?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort interrogating a Gringotts Goblin, becoming aware of Harry's Horcrux hunt<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/51/The_Killing_Curse.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120715135203" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Killing Curse.gif" data-image-key="The_Killing_Curse.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/51/The_Killing_Curse.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120715135203" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/51/The_Killing_Curse.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120715135203" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/51/The_Killing_Curse.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120715135203" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Killing Curse.gif" data-image-key="The_Killing_Curse.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/51/The_Killing_Curse.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120715135203" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Killing_Curse.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort learning that one of his <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Helga_Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Helga Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup">Hufflepuff's Cup</a>, was stolen, killing the bearers of bad news in a fit of rage</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/1_May" title="1 May">1 May</a> <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, Voldemort was informed by several goblins from Gringotts that Harry Potter and his friends, Ron Weasley and Hermione Granger, had robbed the <a href="/wiki/Lestrange_vault" class="mw-redirect" title="Lestrange vault">Lestrange vault</a>. This caused Voldemort to panic, and when he was informed that <a href="/wiki/Helga_Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Helga Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup">a small golden cup</a> had been stolen, he flew into a rage. Voldemort <a href="/wiki/Massacre_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Massacre at Malfoy Manor">massacred</a> all those who told him the news, having realised at that moment that Harry was hunting his Horcruxes. However, he could not figure out how he had discovered his secret when he never told anyone.
</p><p>In truth, Dumbledore and Harry had worked out, from studying Voldemort's past, that he had created Horcruxes, and also what they were and where they were hidden. Dumbledore first theorised about the Horcruxes and then passed the knowledge onto Harry; from there, Harry was able to complete the hunt. Voldemort listed all the locations of his Horcruxes in his mind, unaware that Harry was connected to his mind at the time. He unwittingly revealed that his last Horcrux was at Hogwarts, just as Harry previously suspected. This caused Harry, Ron, and Hermione to venture to Hogwarts.
</p><p>Following these revelations, Voldemort went to check out the Gaunt Shack and the Cave, only to discover to his fury that the Horcruxes stored there were missing and thus were likely destroyed.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=34" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>I know that you are preparing to fight. Your efforts are futile. You cannot fight me. I do not want to kill you. I have great respect for the teachers of Hogwarts. I do not want to spill magical blood. Give me Harry Potter, and none shall be harmed. Give me Harry Potter, and I shall leave the school untouched. Give me Harry Potter, and you will be rewarded. You have until midnight.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort's ultimatum before the final battle begins <sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Voldemort_and_his_Death_Eaters_waiting_before_the_battle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161124183816" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort and his Death Eaters waiting before the battle.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort_and_his_Death_Eaters_waiting_before_the_battle.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Voldemort_and_his_Death_Eaters_waiting_before_the_battle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161124183816" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Voldemort_and_his_Death_Eaters_waiting_before_the_battle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161124183816" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Voldemort_and_his_Death_Eaters_waiting_before_the_battle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161124183816" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort and his Death Eaters waiting before the battle.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort_and_his_Death_Eaters_waiting_before_the_battle.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Voldemort_and_his_Death_Eaters_waiting_before_the_battle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161124183816" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_and_his_Death_Eaters_waiting_before_the_battle.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort and his army beginning the siege of Hogwarts Castle</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort then returned to Hogwarts, where the residents had already ousted the Death Eaters teaching there and had begun preparing a defence against him. Voldemort rounded up his entire army of Death Eaters, Snatchers, Werewolves, Giants, and Dementors, and commanded his army to fight the Order of the Phoenix members, professors, and students who were in the castle: the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> ensued. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest?cb=20161218210623" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="86" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B7C32M1 Nagini&#39;s attack on Snape.png" data-image-key="B7C32M1_Nagini&#39;s_attack_on_Snape.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20161218210623" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest?cb=20161218210623" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20161218210623" decoding="async" width="220" height="86" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B7C32M1 Nagini&#39;s attack on Snape.png" data-image-key="B7C32M1_Nagini&#39;s_attack_on_Snape.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20161218210623" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort ordering Nagini to kill Snape in the Shrieking Shack</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort himself was not present at the opening stage of the battle, as he was staying within the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>, feeling there was no need for him to fight at the time. While in the shack, he investigated why the Elder Wand did not work any differently from his old wand. He came to the conclusion that it needed to accept him as a master and ordered Nagini to kill Snape. He believed this would solve the problem by transferring mastery of the wand to himself, assuming that since Snape killed Dumbledore then he was the current master of the wand.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/Harry%27s_sacrifice.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140616170544" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry&#39;s sacrifice.gif" data-image-key="Harry&#39;s_sacrifice.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/Harry%27s_sacrifice.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140616170544" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/Harry%27s_sacrifice.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140616170544" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/Harry%27s_sacrifice.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140616170544" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry&#39;s sacrifice.gif" data-image-key="Harry&#39;s_sacrifice.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/Harry%27s_sacrifice.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140616170544" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry%27s_sacrifice.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry willingly letting Voldemort hit him with the <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort then called a one-hour armistice, requesting Harry in exchange for peace and no further deaths. Unbeknownst to Voldemort, Harry carried within him the seventh Horcrux: the scar on his forehead, which was formed when Voldemort failed to kill him as an infant. When Harry met Voldemort in the Forbidden Forest, Voldemort used the Killing Curse on him almost immediately, but only destroyed the Horcrux, rendering his scar "normal." What was not revealed to Voldemort was that when he used Harry's blood three years prior in order to gain himself a new body, the blood passed Harry's mother's protection to Voldemort and anchored Harry to the living world through the Dark Lord. Harry was merely knocked to the ground and feigned death. Voldemort, as a result of destroying his soul shard in Harry, was also knocked out.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_duel_and_death">Final duel and death</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=35" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Final duel and death">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Final duel and death"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Something had happened when he had hit Harry with the Killing Curse. Had Voldemort too collapsed? It seemed like it. And both of them had fallen briefly unconscious and both of them had now returned. . . </i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort after having "killed" Harry Potter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Unsure of what had just happened, Voldemort ordered <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a> to check Harry's body. Narcissa did so and pronounced Harry dead, eliciting celebration from the Death Eaters. Voldemort then declared that no man could threaten him any more. He degraded Harry's body by performing the Cruciatus Curse, then forced the captured Hagrid to carry it back to Hogwarts for all to see. Voldemort did not realise, however, that Narcissa had lied to him in order to enter the castle so as to find her son.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>You see? Harry Potter is dead! Do you understand now, deluded ones? He was nothing, ever, but a boy who relied on others to sacrifice themselves for him!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort rejoicing over Harry Potter's "death"<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Voldemort-smiling.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180920185319" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="136" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort-smiling.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort-smiling.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Voldemort-smiling.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180920185319" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Voldemort-smiling.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180920185319" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Voldemort-smiling.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180920185319" decoding="async" width="180" height="136" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort-smiling.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort-smiling.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Voldemort-smiling.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180920185319" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort-smiling.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort gloating after Harry's "death"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Voldemort and his army marched to Hogwarts, Voldemort claimed Harry had been killed while trying to escape. Neville, instead of surrendering, charged at Voldemort. After Neville refused to join him, Voldemort placed a <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind Curse</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a> on him and set the hat on fire to make an example of him, claiming that Slytherin would be the only Hogwarts House from then on. But at that moment, reinforcements for the Hogwarts defenders arrived. Neville was able to throw off the curse and pulled Gryffindor's Sword from the Hat, and used it to decapitate Nagini, destroying the last remaining Horcrux. Enraged, Voldemort attempted to kill Neville, but Harry, now beneath his <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility cloak</a>, interfered and cast a Shield Charm between them.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>You won't be killing any of them. You won't be killing anyone ever again.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Harry Potter informing Voldemort of his impending doom<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/43/Deathly_Hallows_-_Voldemort_Protego.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120112180806" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="74" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Deathly Hallows - Voldemort Protego.gif" data-image-key="Deathly_Hallows_-_Voldemort_Protego.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/43/Deathly_Hallows_-_Voldemort_Protego.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120112180806" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/43/Deathly_Hallows_-_Voldemort_Protego.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120112180806" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/43/Deathly_Hallows_-_Voldemort_Protego.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120112180806" decoding="async" width="180" height="74" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Deathly Hallows - Voldemort Protego.gif" data-image-key="Deathly_Hallows_-_Voldemort_Protego.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/43/Deathly_Hallows_-_Voldemort_Protego.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120112180806" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Deathly_Hallows_-_Voldemort_Protego.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort forcing himself into Hogwarts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the second round of the Battle of Hogwarts, Voldemort tried to strike down everyone within his reach and his weakened army forced its way into the castle. In the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>, his army was gradually cut down as Voldemort fought Slughorn, Shacklebolt, and <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> all at once and later blasted them away. When Bellatrix Lestrange was killed by <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a>, Voldemort turned his wand on her in rage. At that time, Harry cast a Shield Charm to protect her, and revealed himself to be very much alive. The two wizards then faced each other in the Great Hall.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>But what does it matter? Even if you are right, Potter, it makes no difference to you and me. You no longer have the phoenix wand: We duel on skill alone . . . and after I have killed you, I can attend to Draco Malfoy. . . .</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort threatening Harry in his final moments<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Here, Harry mentioned that by willingly sacrificing himself to Voldemort, he had protected everyone he cared about in Hogwarts with the same magic his mother created when she died for him. Harry tried to explain to Voldemort that he had magic Voldemort did not have, and a weapon more powerful than his, in addition to warning Voldemort of the fate that lay in store for him if he was unwilling to feel remorse for his actions. Goading him by using his birth name, Harry told him that Snape's loyalty was with Dumbledore all along, that Dumbledore's death was planned, and that Snape had not been the master of the Elder Wand; Draco had been.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest?cb=20150904231059" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished.png" data-image-key="B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest?cb=20150904231059" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished.png" data-image-key="B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The final duel between <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and Lord Voldemort</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Originally shocked, Voldemort remained unworried, because Harry did not have his original wand, and he told Harry he would kill him and then dispose of Draco to gain full mastery of the Elder Wand. But Harry revealed that he had <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">already disarmed Draco</a>, so the Elder Wand was now rightfully his. Refusing to believe this, Voldemort fired a Killing Curse at Harry, while Harry countered with his "trademark" spell of <i>Expelliarmus</i>. The Elder Wand refused to kill its true master, and Voldemort's spell rebounded off Harry's, killing the Dark Lord once and for all.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Legacy">Legacy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=36" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Legacy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Legacy"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-mortem">Post-mortem</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=37" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Post-mortem">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Post-mortem"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Professor, what is that?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Something beyond either of our help.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Description of Voldemort's ruined soul<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Voldemort%27s_mutilated_soul.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811144243" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort&#39;s mutilated soul.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort&#39;s_mutilated_soul.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Voldemort%27s_mutilated_soul.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180811144243" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Voldemort%27s_mutilated_soul.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811144243" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Voldemort%27s_mutilated_soul.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180811144243" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort&#39;s mutilated soul.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort&#39;s_mutilated_soul.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f9/Voldemort%27s_mutilated_soul.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180811144243" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort%27s_mutilated_soul.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort's mangled soul in <a href="/wiki/Limbo" title="Limbo">Limbo</a> for eternity</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After his death, Voldemort's body was moved to a <a href="/wiki/Resting_Chamber_of_Lord_Voldemort" title="Resting Chamber of Lord Voldemort">separate chamber away from the Great Hall</a>. It is unknown what happened to it afterwards, but it can be assumed that his body was disposed of. Meanwhile his mutilated soul was trapped in <a href="/wiki/Limbo" title="Limbo">Limbo</a> for eternity, as the soul is meant to stay whole and intact. Because of the destruction done to his soul, he was unable to move on or return to the land of the living as a ghost.<sup id="cite_ref-bloom_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bloom-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> After his confirmed death, the wizarding world at large seemed to be able to speak his name without any more fear. In the end, Lord Voldemort, who was extremely afraid of death, received a fate far worse than that.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_peace">Return to peace</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=38" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Return to peace">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Return to peace"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The death of Lord Voldemort changed the lives of hundreds of thousands of witches and wizards for the better, and Harry Potter was held in high esteem for removing complications of an enormous variety from many peoples' lives. However, his bloody campaign had left a great deal of damage that would not soon be repaired. Following the restoration of the original timeline, Delphini would attempt to go back in time to the night where Voldemort went after the Potters in Godric's Hollow and prevent him from doing so, hoping to ensure Voldemort was never defeated. Harry, Albus, Draco, Scorpius, Ginny, Ron, and Hermione would then go back to try to stop her. During this attempt, the group tried to catch her off guard by making Harry disguise himself as Voldemort. While he was eventually discovered, the group was nonetheless able to prevent Delphini's plan from succeeding and captured her. However, before they left back into their own time, both Harry and Delphini were forced to witness Voldemort's attack at Godric's Hollow, resulting in Harry witnessing his parents' deaths, and Delphini seeing her father's first defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Calamity" title="Calamity">Calamity</a> which occurred during the <a href="/wiki/2010s" title="2010s">2010s</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Portrait" title="Portrait">Portrait</a> of Riddle became one of many things that became <a href="/wiki/Foundable" title="Foundable">Foundables</a>, magical artefacts which appeared throughout the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">Wizarding world</a> without explanation. A memory of a young Riddle also manifested in the world as a Foundable.<sup id="cite_ref-WU_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WU-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternate_timeline">Alternate timeline</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=39" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Alternate timeline">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Alternate timeline"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>More than twenty years following his death, Voldemort's daughter Delphini would attempt to rewrite the timeline in order to bring back her father.
