He was capable of performing an incredibly flawless <a href="/wiki/False_memory_spell" title="False memory spell">False memory charm</a> to create fabricated memories in his victims, having used the charm twice in his lifetime: first on the <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">House-elf</a> <a href="/wiki/Hokey" title="Hokey">Hokey</a> after having murdered <a href="/wiki/Hepzibah_Smith" title="Hepzibah Smith">Hepzibah Smith</a>, to falsely implicate her for the crime, and again on his uncle <a href="/wiki/Morfin_Gaunt" title="Morfin Gaunt">Morfin Gaunt</a> to frame him for the <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_the_Riddle_family" title="Murder of the Riddle family">Murder of the Riddle family</a>, both crimes he himself committed. He was effortlessly capable of casting a powerful <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">Shield Charm</a>, allowing him to deflect spells and magical assaults instantly. Before the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, he amplified his own voice to a significant volume so all of Hogwarts could hear him deliver his ultimatum with the <a href="/wiki/Amplifying_Charm" title="Amplifying Charm">Amplifying Charm</a>, that his voice even sounded as if it was coming from the castle walls. He also performed an outstandingly powerful <a href="/wiki/Silencing_Charm" title="Silencing Charm">Silencing Charm</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwartian" title="Hogwartian">defenders</a> of Hogwarts during the final half of the Battle of Hogwarts to silence all of them, after he had supposedly killed Harry Potter, in a blinding flash of white light, showing his skills in charm-work to be exceptional.</li>
<li><b>Elemental magic mastery</b>: Voldemort was immensely accomplished in the manipulation of the elements, especially <a href="/wiki/Fire" title="Fire">fire</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTPF_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTPF-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> He set Neville and the Sorting Hat aflame with a flick of his wand when he defied him.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> In addition to fire, Voldemort was extremely proficient with the element of lightning, casting a <a href="/wiki/Lightning_spell" title="Lightning spell">colossal upsurge of lightning</a> into the sky after acquiring the Elder Wand that could be felt distances away and even blasting through Hogwarts's shields with a single, immensely powerful bolt of lightning.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Memory" title="Memory">Memory</a> modification</b>: Voldemort was also shown to be extremely adept at modifying the memories of others, as he was able to implant false memories into <a href="/wiki/Morfin_Gaunt" title="Morfin Gaunt">Morfin Gaunt</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hokey" title="Hokey">Hokey</a> and Dumbledore himself praised Voldemort for how effectively he modified the former two's memories, saying he had a very difficult time extracting the real memory, which he said required incredible Legillimency skill. Voldemort also was able to extract bits of information from the <a href="/wiki/Memory_Charm" title="Memory Charm">Memory Charmed</a> Bertha Jorkins, an accomplishment only Dumbledore has been shown capable of matching.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparition</a></b>: Voldemort was exceptionally proficient in Apparition, and could apparate with pinpoint accuracy even when locked in combat, using this ability to dodge and evade spells when duelling Dumbledore. Voldemort was also able to apparate silently, something that only he and Dumbledore were reputed to be able to do.</li>
<li><b>Control of <a href="/wiki/Underage_magic" title="Underage magic">Underage magic</a></b>: Even before being told that he was a wizard, or having any knowledge of <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a> or the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a> at all, the young Voldemort displayed an exceptional degree of control over his usage of underage magic, which he used to torment many of the other children at the orphanage. He was able to move objects with his mind, control animals to do his bidding, and even make bad things happen to those who annoyed him. Even Dumbledore commented that his powers were surprisingly well-developed for his young age, and that his level of control over them had made him uneasy.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Then you will find yourself easy prey for the Dark Lord! Fools who wear their hearts proudly on their sleeves, who cannot control their emotions, who wallow in sad memories and allow themselves to be provoked this easily — weak people, in other words — they stand no chance against his powers! He will penetrate your mind with absurd ease, Potter!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> explaining to Harry Potter's exceptional psychic abilities, during their Occulmency lessons<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tumblr_mv0xoiWzPj1qeijvdo1_250.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140705155925" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="130" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tumblr mv0xoiWzPj1qeijvdo1 250.gif" data-image-key="Tumblr_mv0xoiWzPj1qeijvdo1_250.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tumblr_mv0xoiWzPj1qeijvdo1_250.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140705155925" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tumblr_mv0xoiWzPj1qeijvdo1_250.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140705155925" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tumblr_mv0xoiWzPj1qeijvdo1_250.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140705155925" decoding="async" width="245" height="130" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tumblr mv0xoiWzPj1qeijvdo1 250.gif" data-image-key="Tumblr_mv0xoiWzPj1qeijvdo1_250.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tumblr_mv0xoiWzPj1qeijvdo1_250.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140705155925" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tumblr_mv0xoiWzPj1qeijvdo1_250.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> being possessed by Voldemort through Legilimency</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> and <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a></b>: Voldemort was exceptionally adept and gifted in the use of both Occlumency and Legilimency, being able to effectively shield his own mind and penetrate the minds of others. He was particularly talented and skilled in Legilimency, and as an adult, became the greatest Legilimens to ever have lived. His frighteningly exceptional prowess in Legilimency allowed Voldemort to delve and peer deep into the minds of others without needing to say the incantation or using his wand, seeing their deepest thoughts, and he can even use Legilimency to influence the minds that he invaded. <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> has stated that Voldemort could not only read, but also control and unhinge the minds of others, often enjoying telepathically invading the minds of others, creating incredibly realistic visions designed to torture them into madness (such as the one he sent to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>), and only killing them "after extracting the last exquisite ounce of agony", when he had them literally begging for death. He was also able to use Legilimency to briefly possess Harry, even though he had already regained a physical body, which caused Harry so much pain that he even begged for death. Hence, Voldemort could almost always tell when someone was lying. However, when <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a> lied that Harry Potter was dead, Voldemort notably believed her.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> The most remarkable part about this skill was that he seemed to have already been able to consciously use it while he was still a child in the orphanage. Extremely few people were skilled enough in <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> to shield themselves from him. <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, and also possibly <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a> were notably the only known ones able to block out Voldemort's Legilimency using Occulumency. Additionally, Harry Potter, despite his link to Voldemort's mind, discovered that he could block Voldemort's intrusions into his mind by feeling love, as direct contact with Harry's mind while he was feeling love was excruciatingly painful for Voldemort with his maimed and diminished soul.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Using his mastery of Occlumency, Voldemort was able to block his connection to Harry, preventing him from seeing what he is doing, although it could be broken through when Voldemort was angered enough, which became increasingly so due to Voldemort's volatile temper rising from the exhaustive search for the Elder Wand and the destruction of his Horcruxes. While it's unknown if Severus Snape or Albus Dumbledore ever attempted Legilimency on him, it's likely that neither would be able to penetrate his mind despite being skilled Legilimens themselves.</li>
<li><b>Power of possession</b>: Voldemort had the power to possess living creatures and gain complete control over their actions by doing so. While in his spectral form, this was the only remaining power he had access to until his body was restored. Since he told his Death Eaters that this was his only <i>remaining</i> power, he must have been able to use this power during at least the First Wizarding War. Once the possession is done, the victims will have no knowledge of what happened. This form of possession shortens the lifespan of the small animals he inhabits, and in the terms of wizards, his face would appear on the back of their head. In this case, it would seem that his possession is partial, as <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirrell</a> had some (albeit little) control over his actions. It also shortened the host wizard's life, but he was able to extend it via <a href="/wiki/Unicorn_blood" title="Unicorn blood">unicorn blood</a>, and enhanced their magical abilities by combining their own innate powers with his weakened powers.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_27-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> He was also able to possess Harry and presumably others in his physical form.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> It is unknown if this ability is unique to him, as he is the only one known to use it.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Flight" title="Flight">Flying</a></b>: Voldemort was able, and invented the ability, <a href="/wiki/Unsupported_flight" title="Unsupported flight">to fly without support</a>, defying the law of magic that states objects can only fly through use of a flying charm. He first exhibited this flying ability when in pursuit of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> over <a href="/wiki/Little_Whinging" title="Little Whinging">Little Whinging</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> He frequently used his ability to fly throughout the Second Wizarding War, and was known to have taught Severus Snape how to duplicate the feat.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parseltongue</a></b>: Voldemort was a Parselmouth, a trait he inherited from his ancestor, <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a>, the magical ability to communicate with <a href="/wiki/Snake" title="Snake">snakes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_7-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> It seems that most of his <a href="/wiki/House_of_Gaunt" title="House of Gaunt">Gaunt</a> ancestors (even his <a href="/wiki/Merope_Riddle" title="Merope Riddle">mother</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt" title="Marvolo Gaunt">grandfather</a> and <a href="/wiki/Morfin_Gaunt" title="Morfin Gaunt">uncle</a>) inherited this highly unusual trait; such traits are commonly passed down through families through inbreeding, a practice employed by the Gaunt family.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> This ability was one that he favoured immensely, as he was extremely capable of communicating with the <a href="/wiki/Serpent_of_Slytherin" title="Serpent of Slytherin">Serpent of Slytherin</a><sup id="cite_ref-COS_7-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> and his loyal pet snake and Horcrux <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>, commanding them to commit horrific actions in his various diabolical plots.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Immortality" title="Immortality">Immortality</a></b>: Voldemort is the only Dark wizard who was known to have created more than one Horcrux. These Horcruxes were his school diary, the <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring" title="Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s Ring">Marvolo Gaunt's Ring</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw%27s_Diadem" title="Ravenclaw&#39;s Diadem">Ravenclaw's Diadem</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" title="Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup">Hufflepuff's Cup</a>, <a href="/wiki/Slytherin%27s_Locket" title="Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Slytherin's Locket</a>, Nagini, and Harry Potter himself. As long as these Horcruxes remained active, Voldemort was immortal and undying, even by a magic as powerful as the Killing Curse.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_19-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a></b>: Voldemort displayed tremendous and near unrivalled skills in Transfiguration. He easily transfigured Dumbledore's fire-rope into a <a href="/wiki/Fire_to_snake_spell" title="Fire to snake spell">black snake</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_25-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> He was also skilful in <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">conjuration</a>, as he could craft silver objects of incredible durability, as seen when he produced a <a href="/wiki/Silver_shield_spell" title="Silver shield spell">silver shield</a> strong enough to repel Dumbledore's curse, which was extremely powerful. He could even conjure artificial limbs that possessed far greater strength and immunity to some spells, as he created an <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew%27s_silver_hand" title="Peter Pettigrew&#39;s silver hand">artificial silver forearm and hand</a> for <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a> <a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">non-verbally</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a></b>: As Defence Against the Dark Arts was the subject Voldemort offered to teach when he tried to become a teacher, it can be assumed that despite being far more interested in using dark magic than learning to defend from it, Voldemort had achieved a high score on his O.W.L and N.E.W.T exam and therefore that this was his favourite subject as a student. He was excellently skilled in defending from dark magic in addition to being the most powerful practitioner of the Dark Arts. It can also be assumed that his knowledge of the Dark Arts also made him aware of many advanced defensive spells that few knew of, as he claimed that he could teach students magic they cannot learn from any other should he be the Professor of Defence Against the Dark Arts.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Spell_creation" title="Spell creation">Spell creation</a></b>: Voldemort was also extremely capable of inventing his own magical <a href="/wiki/Spell" title="Spell">spells</a>, as evidenced with the spell <a href="/wiki/Morsmordre" title="Morsmordre">Morsmordre</a>, which summoned the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a> in the sky, being one of Voldemort's own dark inventions. He and his followers used it to summon a floating, green Dark Mark, usually over the houses of their victims.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_28-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> He also is the first wizard to be able to fly unsupported (something longtime thought to be impossible) meaning he must have devised a way to do so himself. He once mentioned to his followers that a few spells of his own invention were used to assist in his rudimentary body. It is also likely that some of the dark spells used to hide and protect his Horcruxes were constructed by him as even Dumbledore had difficulty in overcoming them.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/HarryPotterVolFr.gif/revision/latest?cb=20170501081529" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="HarryPotterVolFr.gif" data-image-key="HarryPotterVolFr.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/HarryPotterVolFr.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170501081529" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/HarryPotterVolFr.gif/revision/latest?cb=20170501081529" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/HarryPotterVolFr.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170501081529" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="HarryPotterVolFr.gif" data-image-key="HarryPotterVolFr.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/04/HarryPotterVolFr.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170501081529" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:HarryPotterVolFr.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort's wandless possible casting of <a href="/wiki/Fiendfyre" title="Fiendfyre">Fiendfyre</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Wandless_magic" title="Wandless magic">Wandless</a> and <a href="/wiki/Non-verbal_spell" class="mw-redirect" title="Non-verbal spell">nonverbal magic</a></b>: Voldemort was also immensely accomplished at both wandless and nonverbal magic, enough so to be capable of using both effortlessly. He could move objects magically without the incantations to do so normally, using his hand to remove the masks from the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> who returned to him after his rebirth while he scolded them and easily lifting the grounded <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> up by harshly motioning him and later instantly disarming him with a simple wave of his arm during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>. He was also capable of pushing a dead giant out of his way with a lazy wave of his hand during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> and also magically moving his cloak to restrain Harry Potter with a mere hand gesture. He was capable of casting spells ranging from simple charms to Dark spells and even the most advanced of magic such as the Unforgivable Curses to their full potency without speaking the incantation.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">Alchemy</a></b>: Voldemort was learned in the ancient art and science of Alchemy, to the point where he was confident that if he was able to steal the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a>, he would be able to not only use it to produce the <a href="/wiki/Elixir_of_Life" title="Elixir of Life">Elixir of Life</a>, but also manipulate the process of doing so in a manner that would allow him to "<i>create a body of</i> [his] <i>own</i>" for his mangled soul to inhabit, thus restoring himself.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_27-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Wand" title="Wand">Wand</a> versatility</b>: Voldemort has shown the ability to use wands other than his own with no handicap. He used his uncle Morfin's wand to kill his father and paternal grandparents as a teenager and in 1997, he used <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy%27s_wand" title="Lucius Malfoy&#39;s wand">Lucius Malfoy's wand</a> for a period of time, and could  effectively cast a <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a> on <a href="/wiki/Charity_Burbage" title="Charity Burbage">Charity Burbage</a> with it. Later, during the same year, he intended on using <a href="/wiki/Selwyn" title="Selwyn">Selwyn</a>'s wand, though this did not come to be. In the following year, he took ownership of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>; despite not unlocking the wand's full power, he was still able to use his usual level of magic (which was described by himself and Snape to be extraordinary), being able to pressure and ultimately defeat three extremely skilled opponents all at once (<a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>).</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e3/Voldemort_reborn.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20110425021938" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="72" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort reborn.JPG" data-image-key="Voldemort_reborn.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e3/Voldemort_reborn.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110425021938" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e3/Voldemort_reborn.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20110425021938" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e3/Voldemort_reborn.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110425021938" decoding="async" width="180" height="72" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort reborn.JPG" data-image-key="Voldemort_reborn.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e3/Voldemort_reborn.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110425021938" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_reborn.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lord Voldemort's fearsome visage</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b>Intimidation</b>: Lord Voldemort, due to his virtually unequalled capacity for heinous torture and murder, commanded an extremely intimidating presence, enough to frighten low-level thugs and make them work for him out of sheer fear of how he would react to their refusal. He was able to swiftly intimidate famed wandmakers <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mykew_Gregorovitch" title="Mykew Gregorovitch">Mykew Gregorovitch</a>, both of whom instantly submitted to his malevolent demands, with even the mere sight of him effortlessly terrifying <a href="/wiki/Frank_Bryce" title="Frank Bryce">Frank Bryce</a> and likes of the extremely courageous <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, the latter of whom would become haunted by the crimson eyes and cruel gaze of the Dark Lord for three years.  Among the extremely few individuals who did not fear Voldemort included the tremendously fearless <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> (who remained staunch in consistently opposing the Dark Lord) and the exceptionally brave <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> (who was among the extremely few wizards unafraid to call him by name), along with those who defiantly stood up to Voldemort during his reign of terror and died fighting valiantly against him. His inner circle of Death Eaters overwhelmingly feared him and consequentially maintained their fierce loyalty to him at least partly out of fear of what he would do to them otherwise. Indeed, Voldemort's profound experience in intimidation tactics allowed him to instil great fear into the hearts of <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizardkind</a>, to the point that almost all feared uttering his name aloud to one another, with <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggarts</a> even commonly appearing as Voldemort since he represented the worst fear of many members of wizardkind.</li>
<li><b>Physical aptitude</b>: Voldemort was in excellent physical condition despite his skeletal physique, with his strength and agility easily overwhelming Harry Potter when he attacked him violently.</li>
<li><b>Intellectual genius</b>: Voldemort was not only a great wizard, but also possessed an incredible, genius intellect, as he was considered to be the most brilliant student ever to attend Hogwarts by Dumbledore. His intellect is evidenced by his strategic cunning in being able to mastermind and orchestrate two of the most destructive wars in British wizarding history, with him overwhelming all of the Britain wizarding community and nearly triumphing in both the first war and second wizarding wars.</li>
<li><b>Charisma</b>: Even at a young age, Voldemort displayed remarkable talent for the manipulation of others, being able to manipulate <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> into telling him about Horcruxes and gain the trust of every teacher in Hogwarts, with only <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> managing to not be swayed by Voldemort's charisma. He also surrounded himself with a group of friends who would become Death Eaters, though Voldemort felt no affection for any of them. He was considered charming by most people who met him, and was able to inspire others to follow him. As an adult, his skills in manipulation grew even further, successfully convincing many wizards and witches to join his cause, although <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> noted that Voldemort also used tricks, jinxes, and blackmail to get people to join him. Even when his physical body and magical powers were severely weakened, Voldemort was able to use his charisma to manipulate <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a> into serving him, when Quirrell originally intended to be the other way around. He also earned the trust of <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> when she discovered <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s diary">his diary</a>.</li>
<li><b>Acting skills</b>: Besides his formidable magical skills and extensive knowledge of magic, as a teenager, Tom proved to be a consummate actor, being able to hide his true nature from almost everyone in Hogwarts except Dumbledore. He was able to convince virtually all of the Hogwarts staff and instructors that his facade of being a model student was his true personality and was able to avoid detection of having opened the Chamber of Secrets.</li>
<li><b>Leadership skills</b>: Even when he was still only a young student, Riddle was already a very effective leader, as he was able to lead the <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_gang" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s gang">forerunners of the Death Eaters</a> to effectively sneak past surveillance, being responsible for several nasty incidences that were never connected to them, showing that even at a young age, Riddle was a very competent leader. As he grew older and gained more experience in leading and thus honed leadership skills further, Tom's style of leadership presumably changed from the original charismatic rule of the Hogwarts gang to the tyrannical and completely ruthless - though no less highly effective - command of his Death Eaters demonstrated throughout both the First and Second Wizarding War. The best example of his efficiency as a leader would be the fact that he, with the help of less than forty united Death Eaters, completely overwhelmed and came very close to dominating the entire population of magical Britain during the First Wizarding War and eventually conquered the whole magical Britain during the Second Wizarding War.</li>
<li><b>Salesmanship skills:</b> A largely overlooked talent of Voldemort's was his skills at brokering sales as an assistant at Borgin and Burke's when he was in his late teens. Even Dumbledore was impressed by his skills as a salesman during his time as an employee of Borgin and Burkes. His charisma and knowledge of various magical artefacts helped him in this job and allowed him to acquire a wide variety of magical relics for his employers at the time. This talent and job allowed him to discover the Locket of Slytherin and Helga Hufflepuff's Cup in the possession of Hepizbah Smith. He was often reserved for rather delicate matters that took subtlety and persuasion, but which he also masterfully completed.</li>
<li><b>Teaching skills</b>: When Voldemort attempted to apply for a position as a teacher at Hogwarts, he expressed full confidence in being able to teach the students things they can gain from no other wizards. Despite his ulterior motives that concludes his lack of desire to genuinely pass down knowledge to the next generation, his years of extensive studies and charisma would have certainly made him a successful instructor; something he intended to take advantage of to influence the students and recruit his future army. It can be assumed that had he been allowed to become the Defence Against the Dark Arts Professor, he would have been able to convince many of his students to join his cause and, given that he claimed to be able to teach them magic they cannot learn from others, he would have most likely successfully created a powerful army of wizards and witches. He had proven himself to be a powerful mentor; among his known feats are personally training Bellatrix Lestrange in the Dark Arts, instructing Peter Pettigrew how to brew advanced dark potions, and teaching Severus Snape unsupported flight. In general, the Death Eaters knew how to perform some spells of his own making, mainly the <i>Morsmordre</i> spell. Even Quirinus Quirrell believed that if he sought out Voldemort's remains, he would be able to learn some powerful magic from the Dark Lord.</li>
<li><b>Indomitable willpower</b>: Voldemort possessed an unbreakable determination to achieve his goals, spending months seeking out the prophecy and later the Elder Wand. He patiently waited for fourteen years in the Albanian forests as well as for several months on the back of Quirrell's head as well as in the old <a href="/wiki/Riddle_House" title="Riddle House">Riddle House</a> for an equally lengthy time period, showing that aside from his determination, he had an unusual endurance and tolerance for boredom. Additionally, the Dark Lord possessed an obliviousness to danger that made him invulnerable to fear and intimidation, with only <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> being able to intimidate him, which in turn became a well-known fact. Ironically, he feared death and would never put his life on the line for anything, despite his willingness to take risks to further his goals, such as when he entered the Ministry to kill Harry Potter in person. His indomitable willpower had been commended by both of his archenemies, albeit in a sardonic way.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Name">Name</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=43" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Name">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Name"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Voldemort</b>: "<i>They do not call me 'Tom' any more. These days, I am known as—</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>I know what you are known as. But to me, I'm afraid, you will always be Tom Riddle. It is one of the irritating things about old teachers. I am afraid that they never quite forget their charges' youthful beginnings.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> talking to Voldemort when Voldemort returned to ask for a job at Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/I_am_Lord_Voldemort.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190227225113" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="I am Lord Voldemort.gif" data-image-key="I_am_Lord_Voldemort.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/I_am_Lord_Voldemort.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190227225113" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/I_am_Lord_Voldemort.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190227225113" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/I_am_Lord_Voldemort.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190227225113" decoding="async" width="250" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="I am Lord Voldemort.gif" data-image-key="I_am_Lord_Voldemort.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/I_am_Lord_Voldemort.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190227225113" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:I_am_Lord_Voldemort.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Tom Riddle rearranging the letters of his name</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort was born Tom Marvolo Riddle, a name he hated due to it being a common name. When he later learned that his father and namesake was a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a>, he decided to forge his own name, "Voldemort", from an anagram of his full name ("Tom Marvolo Riddle" becomes "I am Lord Voldemort"). He used his middle name, Marvolo, to track down his magical heritage, due to it being a wizarding name. During this time, Voldemort had adopted the name "The Heir of Slytherin" after learning about the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> and his descent from <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a>. Using this name, he hoped to create a terrifying legacy of his own. Few people ever knew that Voldemort's true name was "Tom Marvolo Riddle" to begin with.
</p><p>At first, this name was used to refer to him or to address him. Later, he became so feared in the wizarding community that nearly everyone referred to him only as "<i>You-Know-Who</i>", "<i>He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named</i>", or "<i>The Dark Lord</i>", the last one used primarily by his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> and other supporters. <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Fudge</a> even wrote it to the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister" title="Prime Minister">Muggle Prime Minister</a> rather than saying it. According to <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, not pronouncing his name is a mark of respect. Saying his name to Death Eaters was akin to blasphemy. On <i><a href="/wiki/Potterwatch" title="Potterwatch">Potterwatch</a></i>, he was called "<i>Chief Death Eater</i>". Most people either flinched, screamed or shuddered when they heard the name spoken.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> was one of the few who dared refer to him as "Voldemort," although he preferred to use the name "Tom", using the former in conversation, and the latter when addressing Voldemort himself, showing his fearlessness. In ignoring the name <i>Voldemort,</i> Dumbledore disallowed him the intimidation he sought while appealing to what little remained of his former student deep within Voldemort. Dumbledore also insists on others to use the name "Voldemort", rather than "You-Know-Who", or such varieties, believing that fear in the name would only increase fear of the thing itself. Much later, Harry, despite never fearing <i>Voldemort</i> in name, would use the name "Riddle" in their final confrontation, for the same reasons Dumbledore did. Voldemort would hate it when people dared call him by his forsaken name.
</p><p>After the coup at the Ministry in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Taboo" title="Taboo">Taboo curse</a> was placed on the name "Voldemort"; speaking the name would summon Death Eaters, <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a> officials, or <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a> via <a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparition</a>. This was used to find those who opposed Voldemort's rule, as only they would dare speak the name. This was how Harry, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> were found at <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Court_Road" title="Tottenham Court Road">Tottenham Court Road</a> and before being brought to <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a>. Also, <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a> barely escaped Death Eaters when he spoke it.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_22-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Voldemort's demise at the Battle of Hogwarts, it would appear that the wizarding world at large would no longer fear in speaking his name aloud, as <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> was one of such people. This could be due to the growth of literature and research about his life and heritage, with one book titled <i><a href="/wiki/Marvolo:_The_Truth" title="Marvolo: The Truth">Marvolo: The Truth</a></i>. One reason why the author gave the book that title was to reveal to the Wizarding public the connection between "Lord Voldemort" and his undignified grandfather <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt" title="Marvolo Gaunt">Marvolo Gaunt</a>, thereby depriving Voldemort of the climate of fear and mystery that he had spent much of his life creating around himself. It could also be that his death was confirmed by thousands of witnesses, unlike his first downfall that only an infant Harry ever witnessed.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=44" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Relationships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=45" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="Parents,_grandparents,_and_uncle"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Parents.2C_grandparents.2C_and_uncle">Parents, grandparents, and uncle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=46" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Parents, grandparents, and uncle">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Parents, grandparents, and uncle"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>You think I was going to use my filthy <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle_Senior" title="Tom Riddle Senior">father</a>'s name forever? I, in whose veins runs the blood of <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a> himself, through my <a href="/wiki/Gaunt_family#Gaunt_Family_in_the_20th_Century" class="mw-redirect" title="Gaunt family">mother's side</a>? I, keep the name of a foul, common Muggle, who <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle_Snr.#Abandonment" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle Snr.">abandoned</a> me even before I was born, just because he found out his wife was a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a>? No, Harry. I fashioned myself a new name, a name I knew wizards everywhere would one day fear to speak, when I had become the greatest sorcerer in the world!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Tom Riddle to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> expressing his disdain for the Muggle side of his family<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/MorfinPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20180102031633" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="284" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="MorfinPM.png" data-image-key="MorfinPM.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/MorfinPM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180102031633" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/MorfinPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20180102031633" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/MorfinPM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180102031633" decoding="async" width="180" height="284" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="MorfinPM.png" data-image-key="MorfinPM.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/MorfinPM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180102031633" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:MorfinPM.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Tom Riddle's uncle, <a href="/wiki/Morfin_Gaunt" title="Morfin Gaunt">Morfin Gaunt</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Tom Riddle grew up in a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> orphanage, not knowing any members of his family. His mother, <a href="/wiki/Merope_Riddle" title="Merope Riddle">Merope Gaunt</a>, died shortly after giving birth, never attempting to save herself through magical or other means. His father's feelings toward him are unknown, as he fled then-pregnant Merope after she stopped drugging him with a <a href="/wiki/Love_potion" title="Love potion">love potion</a>, and didn't track down the whereabouts of their child thereafter. The two met face-to-face in <a href="/wiki/1943" title="1943">1943</a>, when Riddle killed his father and <a href="/wiki/Riddle_family" title="Riddle family">paternal grandparents</a>. Riddle was disgusted by his Muggle relatives, and took on the alias "Lord Voldemort" partly out of a desire to be rid of his "filthy Muggle father's name". Tom Riddle Jnr viewed his father as abandoning his mother for being a witch. Whether this was due to a lack of information or Riddle's prejudice against Muggles is unknown.
</p><p>Despite the maternal side of his family being direct descendants of the great <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a>, Tom was unimpressed when he found his deranged uncle <a href="/wiki/Morfin_Gaunt" title="Morfin Gaunt">Morfin</a> living in squalor at the <a href="/wiki/Gaunt_Shack" title="Gaunt Shack">Gaunt Shack</a>, and was not above framing Morfin for murder and stealing his <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt" title="Marvolo Gaunt">maternal grandfather's</a> prized <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring" title="Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s Ring">heirloom ring</a>. Even as a child, he showed contempt for <a href="/wiki/Merope_Riddle" title="Merope Riddle">his mother</a>, and for the weakness of mortality, when he assumed Merope must have been a Muggle if she had been unable to survive. Ironically, it is very possible that Voldemort's more sociopathic and violent tendencies throughout his life could be a result of the "vein of instability" caused by centuries of <a href="/wiki/Inbreeding" title="Inbreeding">inbreeding</a> due to the Gaunts' narcissistic attitudes towards their Slytherin lineage. 
</p><p>Considering Voldemort's loathing towards his heritage and true name, coupled with the rather dysfunctional dynamics of the Gaunt and Riddle families, it raises questions about why Merope chose to name him after his father and maternal grandfather. One possibility is that Merope, even after the abuse she had suffered at the ends of her father and husband, still enough held affection for them to name her only son after them. Alternatively, as Merope was on her deathbed while giving birth to the younger Riddle, she was likely reflecting on her life. Considering her Gaunt childhood of abuse, poverty, and isolation, she likely had very few, if any, friends to socialise with before her marriage to the elder Tom Riddle, leaving Marvolo and Morfin as the only men in her life, and "Tom" and "Marvolo" as the few male names that she could think of. 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Salazar_Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=47" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Salazar Slytherin">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Salazar Slytherin"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The only pride Voldemort ever took on his family was that he inherited the blood of the famous <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a> from his mother, which he consistently flaunted at every opportunity possible, proudly addressing himself as the "Heir of Salazar Slytherin", while regarding Slytherin as his "noble ancestor". 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=48" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>I shall attend to the boy in person. There have been too many mistakes where <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> is concerned, Some of them have been my own. That Potter lives is due more to my errors than to his triumphs. I have been careless, and so have been thwarted by luck and chance, those wreckers of all but the best-laid plans. But I know better now. I understand those things that I did not understand before. I must be the one to kill Harry Potter, and I shall be.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lord Voldemort announcing his intention to murder Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140603201724" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140603201724" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140603201724" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140603201724" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140603201724" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, his mortal enemy and unintentional Horcrux</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Harry Potter became Voldemort's mortal enemy after the Dark Lord heard part of a <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">prophecy</a> that foretold the birth of an individual destined to destroy him; two infants met the criteria, but for the simple reason that Harry was a half-blood like himself, Voldemort considered him more of a threat than <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>. In targeting Harry, Voldemort unwittingly <i>"marked him as his equal</i>", thus sowing the seeds of his own destruction. Because Harry's <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">mother</a> willingly sacrificed herself for her son, the <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">curse</a> backfired. Voldemort lost his physical body, and unintentionally transferred some of his powers and abilities to Harry, while a piece of his soul embedded itself in a <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_scars#The_lightning-bolt_scar" title="Harry Potter&#39;s scars">scar</a> on Harry's forehead, inadvertently making the boy a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH35_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH35-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Trelawney</a>'s prophecy stated that "The Chosen One" would have powers the Dark Lord lacked. That power is <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a>, and Dumbledore realised that it was Harry's abilities, combined with his capacity to love, that would empower him to defeat Voldemort. Unlike Harry, who was mentally, emotionally, and spiritually intact and whose friends supported him out of loyalty and love (platonic affection), Voldemort was psychologically, spiritually, and emotionally shredded, feeling only arrogance, hate, greed, and jealousy; and he controlled his followers through fear, intimidation and coercion. Harry was disturbed to notice many similarities between them — they were both orphans who thought of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> as their first real homes, and both physically resembled their fathers, and to some degree each other. However, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> insisted that they differed in one absolutely crucial way — Harry had the ability to love, while Voldemort did not.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>I have nothing more to say to you, Potter, You have irked me too often, for too long. AVADA KEDAVRA!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort attempting to kill Harry Potter during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>While Harry found it difficult to fathom that something so simple as love is the more powerful force, he understood that, once again, it was also about choices: Voldemort's actions regarding Harry were based on the prophecy, but Harry would choose to fight Voldemort whether or not the prophecy had been made. That choice, and the ability to make that choice, was largely what gave Harry powers that Voldemort lacked and prevented Harry from falling victim to the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark side</a>. Some years earlier, Dumbledore had stressed to Harry that it is one's choices that makes a person what they truly are, just as it had with Harry's father, James, when he chose to overcome his youthful bad behaviour.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Harrypossessed.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141127142301" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="117" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harrypossessed.gif" data-image-key="Harrypossessed.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Harrypossessed.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20141127142301" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Harrypossessed.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141127142301" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Harrypossessed.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20141127142301" decoding="async" width="245" height="117" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harrypossessed.gif" data-image-key="Harrypossessed.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Harrypossessed.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20141127142301" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harrypossessed.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort possessing Harry</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort became obsessed with Harry Potter after he failed to kill the one-year-old boy — livid that a helpless infant caused his downfall. He later sought revenge on Harry to prove that he, Voldemort, was the most feared and powerful wizard of all time. Voldemort's hatred and desire for revenge was strong enough that, when the Horcrux contained in his diary encountered him in the Chamber of Secrets in 1993, he indicated that even the desire to kill Muggle-borns in the name of Salazar Slytherin as his heir no longer mattered to him compared to trying to target Harry for several months since the start of the school year. Voldemort considered Harry weak in comparison to himself and he always discounted how love's power has aided Harry. But after possessing Harry's mind, Harry's overwhelming emotions for his friends and family were so overpowering and disturbing to Voldemort that they drove him out. As a result, he never attempted to possess Harry again.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Voldemort</b>: "<i>Potter doesn't mean that. Who else are you going to use as a shield today, Potter?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>No one. There are no more Horcruxes. It's just you and me. One of us is going to leave for good.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; The final confrontation between Voldemort and Harry at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Harry_and_VOldemort_BTLEOFHGWRTS.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20151129054544" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="108" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry and VOldemort BTLEOFHGWRTS.JPG" data-image-key="Harry_and_VOldemort_BTLEOFHGWRTS.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Harry_and_VOldemort_BTLEOFHGWRTS.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151129054544" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Harry_and_VOldemort_BTLEOFHGWRTS.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20151129054544" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Harry_and_VOldemort_BTLEOFHGWRTS.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151129054544" decoding="async" width="250" height="108" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry and VOldemort BTLEOFHGWRTS.JPG" data-image-key="Harry_and_VOldemort_BTLEOFHGWRTS.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Harry_and_VOldemort_BTLEOFHGWRTS.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151129054544" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_and_VOldemort_BTLEOFHGWRTS.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry and Voldemort before their final duel</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When the two faced off for the last time, Harry urged Voldemort to feel remorse — the only known means of repairing a fractured soul — but Voldemort reacted with disdain. Harry went on to inform Voldemort that despite wielding the Elder Wand, he was not its master; <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> won the wand's allegiance by disarming Dumbledore in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Astronomy Tower</a>, but Harry had disarmed Draco <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">months later</a>. Thus, Harry was the true master of the Elder Wand. In his fury, Voldemort made one last attempt at Harry's life, but the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a> was loyal to Harry, and the Killing Curse once again backfired on to Voldemort. Without his Horcruxes to sustain him, this time the curse finally and completely ended Voldemort's life. Voldemort and Harry were also related by blood, however distantly, through their shared descent from the Peverells (Voldemort through the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Gaunt" title="House of Gaunt">Gaunts</a> and Harry through the <a href="/wiki/Potter_family" title="Potter family">Potters</a>). This made them distant cousins.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Delphini">Delphini</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=49" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Delphini">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Delphini"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>It is unknown how Voldemort felt about his daughter since he died while she was still a baby. However, in the alternative timeline created via a mistake caused by Scorpius and Albus, Voldemort had apparently put Delphini (known as the Augurey) in charge of the Ministry: <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> (Headmistress of Hogwarts in this timeline) constantly informs the Augurey with dispatches about everything that is going on in Hogwarts; the Augurey gives instructions to <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> (Head of Magical Law Enforcement of the Ministry of Magic in this timeline), e.g. how to deal with incidents involving wizards killing Muggles and bribing the Muggle Prime Minister with gold in such cases. Some students in Hogwarts openly quote the Augurey's motto that "the future is ours to make", indicating that the Augurey was probably a famous and respected force as well as an inspiring example in the wizarding world of this timeline.  
</p><p>It is therefore likely that had Voldemort lived, he would have considered her an exceptionally faithful servant, something like his right-hand minion or deputy, and given her more power than he usually allowed his Death Eaters. It's notable that in this alternative timeline Delphi has her own official symbol - the bird emblazoned in a fascistic manner - that is widely used in this world, just like the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a>, the official symbol of Voldemort. In the office of Head of Magical Law Enforcement in the Ministry there are Augurey flags flying down with this symbol while there are flags with the Dark Mark in Hogwarts. None of the Death Eaters ever had their own individual symbols and none of them ever had individual titles or alias due to having just a collective name for their group, while Delphini was operating under her personal and unique alias "the Augurey" in this timeline, instead of being known just as another top Death Eater.  
</p><p>It is not known why he wanted a child, as he did not feel a need for love and disliked the idea of becoming emotionally attached to anyone, and in addition desired immortality. However, he likely realised that his daughter could become a talented and useful servant as Bellatrix was. It is also likely that he wished to preserve the Slytherin bloodline, on account of Voldemort being the last remaining heir of Slytherin. He kept her birth a secret, most likely because it may have placed her in danger, since Voldemort was considered the most powerful and dangerous Dark wizard of the time. 
</p><p>Delphini was curious about her parents, and wanted to have the chance to know them. She went to great lengths to meet and save her father, even to the point of meddling with time to create a future where he lived, which shows she had some love for him. After she was defeated by her cousin <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, she begged for death instead of having to face the fact that she failed her father. 
</p><p>It is rather ironic that Delphini held such strong affection and fascination for her father, a man who felt absolutely no love. The alternative timeline where Voldemort ruled shows that he would have considered Delphini (known as the Augurey in that universe) a faithful servant.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bellatrix_Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=50" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Bellatrix Lestrange">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Bellatrix Lestrange"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>The Dark Lord will rise again, <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Senior" title="Bartemius Crouch Senior">Crouch</a>! Throw us into Azkaban, we will wait!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Bellatrix Lestrange proclaiming her loyalty to Voldemort during her trial<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140622235902" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="250" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bellatrix Lestrange promo.jpg" data-image-key="Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140622235902" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140622235902" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140622235902" decoding="async" width="180" height="250" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bellatrix Lestrange promo.jpg" data-image-key="Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140622235902" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, his best and most loyal servant</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Bellatrix Lestrange was among Voldemort's most loyal and trusted <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. She was entrusted with <a href="/wiki/Helga_Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Helga Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup">one of his Horcruxes</a>, even though she was kept unaware of what it really was, and stored it in her <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts</a> <a href="/wiki/Lestrange_Vault" title="Lestrange Vault">vault</a>. She was fanatically loyal to her master as, after his first defeat in <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>, she did not join many of her fellow Death Eaters in denying their association with him. Instead, she proudly declared that she remained his most loyal servant and that he would surely return. She considered Azkaban a place where she could wait for him, rather than a prison.
</p><p>Her obsession extended to her being in love with and sexually attracted to him. On at least one occasion, during a meeting of his Death Eaters at Malfoy Manor, her face flushed and her eyes welled up with tears when he praised her.
</p><p>He did seem to consider her of greater importance than most of his other servants. He may have had at least a superficial affection for her, as he would call her "Bella" like other members of her family would. He seemed to be flattered by her unfaltering devotion as he praised her, along with her <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">husband</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rabastan_Lestrange" title="Rabastan Lestrange">brother-in-law</a> during his rebirth and promised that she would be rewarded; Snape later mentions that despite this he was more impressed by Snape's many years of useful information than Bellatrix's devotion however. At the conclusion of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, he grabbed her and Apparated away with her; she was the sole Death Eater who he bothered to help, though this may have been more due to her closer proximity rather than preferential treatment. When she was killed by <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, he was furious, and intended to avenge her death when Harry intervened.
</p><p>Although Bellatrix was married to one of Voldemort's other loyal Death Eaters, <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus Lestrange</a>, the union seemed to be nothing more than a business-like partnership. It was Voldemort to whom she spoke in a romantic manner. She was outraged by anyone showing him the slightest disrespect. When <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> called him by his name in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, she became enraged, due to feeling that he was unworthy of speaking the name.
</p><p>Unknown to nearly all, it would be revealed years later after their death that Bellatrix and Voldemort had in fact engaged in a sexual relationship, resulting in the birth of their daughter <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a> who, years later, threatened to upset the timeline to be with her father. As Voldemort believed that he could cheat death, through his Horcruxes, he probably did not feel a need to leave a child behind as an heir. It is highly likely that he used the relationship with Bellatrix as a way to reward her for her undying loyalty to him, and for her rather potent and notable successes as his most loyal lieutenant. However, a reward appears to be unlikely considering Bellatrix's failures at the Ministry.     
</p><p>Because of his egotistical and self-centred nature, he was likely to have been pleased by Bellatrix's obsessive love for him. Despite believing himself immortal, he may have considered the usefulness of Delphini via the idea of siring a lineage of lieutenants devoutly loyal to him through familial bonds while seeing them as extensions of his own power and authority, much like many kings and tyrants who procreated to expand and solidify their own power through blood ties. He may have also chosen Bellatrix as a mate due to her blood relations and thoroughly proven power as a witch, thus marking her as a potent genetic combination as well as an ideal fit for Voldemort who revelled in his own status and power. A mate of such fortitude and strength would certainly appeal to Voldemort's pathological need to expand his fame and reputation. Voldemort also may have seen Delphini as a way of extending the power of the Slytherin bloodline beyond himself so as to further showcase his as well as his family's might and to further terrorise his enemies with the idea of another Dark Lord ruling alongside him. Voldemort may also have been intellectually enthused or curious at the idea of a student with similar powers and potential as himself, highlighting his vanity and ego even further as he had had no living relatives whose powers he could compare his own to or to have learned from.     
</p><p>It is also possible that the conception of Delphini was unintentional as very little is known about her background.     
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nagini">Nagini</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=51" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Nagini">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Nagini"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I think he is perhaps as fond of her as he can be of anything. He certainly likes to keep her close and has an unusual amount of control over her, even for a Parselmouth.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore about Voldemort's affection for Nagini<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/Nagin.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081004075922" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="187" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nagin.jpg" data-image-key="Nagin.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/Nagin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081004075922" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/Nagin.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081004075922" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/Nagin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081004075922" decoding="async" width="180" height="187" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nagin.jpg" data-image-key="Nagin.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/Nagin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081004075922" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nagin.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>, his familiar and last Horcrux</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/Voldemort_nagini.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20181024041719" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="230" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort nagini.jpeg" data-image-key="Voldemort_nagini.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/Voldemort_nagini.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20181024041719" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/Voldemort_nagini.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20181024041719" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/Voldemort_nagini.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20181024041719" decoding="async" width="180" height="230" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort nagini.jpeg" data-image-key="Voldemort_nagini.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ef/Voldemort_nagini.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20181024041719" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_nagini.jpeg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nagini coiled around her master Voldemort</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort had a special relationship with Nagini, his pet snake who was also one of his <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>. Nagini was the only living being that Voldemort seemed to genuinely care about; however, due to the fact that Nagini was one of his Horcruxes, he might have cared about the part of his soul inside her rather than Nagini herself.
