However, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> speculated that Voldemort cared more about Nagini than any other living creature and that his affection for her had nothing to do with the part of his soul he'd placed inside her; in fact Dumbledore thought that it was <i>because </i>of his feelings for the snake (and that she underlines Voldemort's ancestry with <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a>) that he made Nagini into a Horcrux in the first place. Voldemort often stroked her head, wore her around his neck, and even used endearments and loving words when he spoke to her. During <a href="/wiki/Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Meeting at Malfoy Manor">one meeting</a> he demanded the Death Eaters silence immediately when he noticed that Nagini was becoming irritated by their jeers and yells. Nagini never drew the wrath of her master, even when she failed to keep <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> in <a href="/wiki/Bathilda_Bagshot%27s_Home" class="mw-redirect" title="Bathilda Bagshot&#39;s Home">Godric's Hollow</a>, though Voldemort generally did not react well to failure. Nagini obeyed her master's every order, and the two were able to communicate with each other <a href="/wiki/Mind-reading" title="Mind-reading">telepathically</a>. Albus Dumbledore noted that Voldemort had an unusual amount of control over her, even for a <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parselmouth</a>. He often used her to dispose of his enemies such as <a href="/wiki/Charity_Burbage" title="Charity Burbage">Charity Burbage</a>, and also threatened to feed <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a> to her when they failed him.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a> milked the <a href="/wiki/Nagini%27s_venom" title="Nagini&#39;s venom">venom</a> from Nagini's fangs, which he used in a <a href="/wiki/Rudimentary_body_potion" title="Rudimentary body potion">potion</a> that allowed Voldemort to regain a basic physical form. That same year, Voldemort made Nagini a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> with the murder of <a href="/wiki/Bertha_Jorkins" title="Bertha Jorkins">Bertha Jorkins</a>. Though he had often sent Nagini on personal missions, Voldemort kept her close to him after he discovered <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> was attempting to track down and destroy his Horcruxes. Nagini was beheaded by <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, and Voldemort felt rage and perhaps even grief at the loss of his snake. As Nagini was the last remaining Horcrux, her death allowed for Voldemort's ultimate defeat.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Albus_Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=52" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>There is nothing worse than death, Dumbledore!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort expressing his anger towards Dumbledore<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Albus_Dumbledore_%28HBP_promo%29_3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150822232849" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore (HBP promo) 3.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_(HBP_promo)_3.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Albus_Dumbledore_%28HBP_promo%29_3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150822232849" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Albus_Dumbledore_%28HBP_promo%29_3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150822232849" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Albus_Dumbledore_%28HBP_promo%29_3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150822232849" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore (HBP promo) 3.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_(HBP_promo)_3.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Albus_Dumbledore_%28HBP_promo%29_3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150822232849" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albus_Dumbledore_(HBP_promo)_3.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, the one wizard Voldemort always feared</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Tom Riddle met Albus Dumbledore at the age of eleven, when the Professor came to invite him to attend <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>. Although initially suspicious of Dumbledore, he was at least somewhat impressed by Dumbledore's demonstration of magic. Tom was pleased to discover that he was a wizard, as it confirmed the suspicions he long had about being "special." The boy disturbed Dumbledore, however, when he admitted to being able to hurt people who displeased him and being able to <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">talk to snakes</a>. Even as Tom became an extremely popular student among his peers and Professors at Hogwarts, Dumbledore remained wary of him, and kept a very close watch on him.
</p><p>Riddle (then known as Voldemort) returned to Hogwarts years after graduating to request the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> position from Dumbledore, who had become the school's Headmaster. Suspecting that Voldemort's true intentions were far more sinister than he let on, Dumbledore refused him the position; the result of Dumbledore's refusal was not only that the position of DADA professor became "cursed," but it affirmed Dumbledore's complete refusal to bend to Voldemort's will.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Voldemort</b>: "<i>But nothing I have seen in the world has supported your famous pronouncements that <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a> is more powerful than my kind of magic, Dumbledore.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Perhaps you have been looking in the wrong places...,</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Voldemort</b>: "<i>Well, then, what better place to start my fresh researches than here, at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>? Will you let me return? Will you let me share my knowledge with your students?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Voldemort to Albus Dumbledore requesting for the Defence Against the Dark Arts post<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Voldemort despised Dumbledore, not only due to the latter's continued opposition, but also because Dumbledore's belief in the triumphant power of <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a> was something that both confused and disgusted Voldemort. Dumbledore was thought to be the only person Voldemort ever feared and one of the few people Voldemort was unable to intimidate, due to Dumbledore being the only wizard whose powers and skill could rival that of Voldemort's. Dumbledore persisted on referring to him as "Voldemort" to others and addressing him as "Tom" in conversation, a subtle but steadfast refusal to allow Voldemort to dictate the terms of their relationship, and a trait that would later be inherited by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. Dumbledore led the efforts against Voldemort in the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>; over many years, Dumbledore gathered crucial information about Voldemort's past and passed it on to Harry Potter, who would essentially take Dumbledore's place as leader of the opposition in the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Dumbledore and Voldemort met face to face in the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, where Dumbledore addressed Voldemort as "Tom" and said it was foolish of him to come to the Ministry. Voldemort initiated a fierce <a href="/wiki/Duel_in_the_Ministry_Atrium" title="Duel in the Ministry Atrium">duel</a> with Dumbledore, during which he tried to murder both Dumbledore and Harry, but was unsuccessful; Dumbledore managed to maintain the offensive in the duel, forcing Voldemort to possess Harry so Dumbledore would kill Harry out of a desire to kill him as well. This too was unsuccessful as Harry was able to exorcise the Dark Lord from his body and mind by focusing on his intense feelings of grief over <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius</a>' death. <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> arrived at the Ministry just in time to see Voldemort escape with <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, and was finally forced to acknowledge the truth of Voldemort's return.
</p><p>Following his failure to kill either Dumbledore or Harry at the ministry, Voldemort assigned <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> to carry out Dumbledore's assassination. Dumbledore became aware of this plot, and addressed it by arranging his own death with <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>. At the time of his death in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Albus Dumbledore had fully equipped Harry Potter with the physical, mental and emotional tools he needed to defeat Voldemort once and for all in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>. Later on, during his search for the Elder Wand, Voldemort broke into Dumbledore's tomb.
</p><p>Both Voldemort and Dumbledore shared similar traits; they both wielded extraordinary power that made them among the most powerful wizards in history, although Dumbledore had proven to be, perhaps, his only superior, and understood love, which Voldemort was completely unable to do, both were half-blood, although Voldemort knew nothing about Hogwarts until he was 11. Both were recognised as two of the best wizards to go to Hogwarts and were both <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">Prefects</a> and <a href="/wiki/Head_Boy_or_Girl" title="Head Boy or Girl">Head Boy</a>. Both created and led their own causes (the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>). Both Dumbledore and Voldemort possessed the Elder Wand during their life and both also held trust in Severus Snape.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bartemius_Crouch_Jnr.">Bartemius Crouch Jnr.</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=53" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Bartemius Crouch Jnr.">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Bartemius Crouch Jnr."><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>He asked me whether I was ready to risk everything for him. I was ready.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Barty's servitude to Voldemort<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161221034115" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="282" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Barty Crouch Junior.jpg" data-image-key="Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161221034115" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161221034115" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161221034115" decoding="async" width="180" height="282" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Barty Crouch Junior.jpg" data-image-key="Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161221034115" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Barty_Crouch_Junior.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>., his loyal servant</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Another of Voldemort's most loyal and trusted servants was <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>. Barty Crouch was imprisoned in Azkaban with <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> and two other <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. He escaped with the help of his father and dying mother, and the former kept him confined to the Crouch home under the <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a>. When Voldemort learned, by way of torturing <a href="/wiki/Bertha_Jorkins" title="Bertha Jorkins">Bertha Jorkins</a>, that there was a Death Eater at large who remained loyal to him, Voldemort and <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a> overpowered the senior Barty Crouch and freed his son.
</p><p>In contrast with his real father, Crouch saw Lord Voldemort as a father figure of sorts and, after been disowned by his own father and after his Azkaban year, was fanatically devoted to the Dark Lord. In fact, at that point Crouch was willing to sacrifice and give absolutely everything to serve Voldemort. He also believed that if he finished off <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, he would be welcomed back, closer to Voldemort than a real son. In essence, Barty's loyalty is only matched by fellow Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>. However, Crouch's loyalty has led him to know many things about Lord Voldemort that even other loyal Death Eaters, such as Bellatrix, do not. Barty knows that Voldemort had a disappointing father, that he suffered the indignity of being named after that father, and that he had the great pleasure of killing said father to ensure the rise of the dark order. These three common threads helped to fuel Barty's loyalty. This also implies that Barty is aware of Voldemort's blood status as a half-blood, but doesn't care about it, in contradiction to the Death Eaters' belief of pure-blood supremacy. It could very well be that Voldemort told Barty these similarities between the two, and used them as a way to get Barty to join him. Voldemort seems to have acknowledged Barty's worth, something his own father failed to do, referring to Barty as "his most faithful servant." However, for all of Voldemort's public claims, he never truly cared for Barty any more than as a useful servant who is as easily disposable as any other, as Voldemort never wanted a friend.
</p><p>Barty Crouch Jnr helped Voldemort regain a physical body by capturing and imprisoning <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, a retired Auror, who was about to accept Dumbledore's offer to teach <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. Disguised as Moody, Barty Crouch entered Harry's name into the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a> and helped ensure that he would win the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>. By turning the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Cup" title="Triwizard Cup">Triwizard Cup</a> into a <a href="/wiki/Portkey" title="Portkey">Portkey</a>, Crouch made sure Harry was transported to the <a href="/wiki/Little_Hangleton_graveyard" title="Little Hangleton graveyard">Little Hangleton graveyard</a>, where Peter Pettigrew used Harry's blood to concoct a <a href="/wiki/Regeneration_potion" title="Regeneration potion">potion</a> that would allow Voldemort to be reborn. After Voldemort failed to kill Harry in the graveyard, Harry returned to Hogwarts, where Barty Crouch attempted to kill him personally, no longer pretending to be Alastor Moody. Harry was saved by <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> and <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, and Barty Crouch was given the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a>. It's unknown how Voldemort reacted when he learned Crouch's fate, though he possibly felt some disappointment due to the latter's loyalty and usefulness.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Severus_Snape">Severus Snape</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=54" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Severus Snape">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Severus Snape"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Perhaps you already know it? You are a clever man, after all, Severus. You have been a good and faithful servant, and I regret what must happen… The <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a> cannot serve me properly, Severus, because I am not its true master. The Elder Wand belongs to the wizard who killed its last owner. You killed <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>. While you live, Severus, the Elder Wand cannot truly be mine… It cannot be any other way.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort just before ordering <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a> to kill Snape<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, his formerly loyal servant turned enemy and victim</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Severus Snape became a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> in the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. He was extremely loyal to Voldemort until he realised that the Dark Lord planned to murder <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>. Snape appealed to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, becoming a spy in exchange for her protection. From that point on, Snape used <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> to prevent the Dark Lord from discovering his true allegiance.
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a> broke the <a href="/wiki/Fidelius_Charm" title="Fidelius Charm">Fidelius Charm</a> cast by the Potters, Lily died and Voldemort disappeared; however, while Snape was unable to save Lily herself, his love for her allowed her son, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, to survive. It was because Snape asked the Dark Lord to spare her life that Voldemort gave Lily the option to flee, thus making her death a <a href="/wiki/Sacrificial_protection" title="Sacrificial protection">willing sacrifice</a>. Following the death of the Potters, Snape's loyalty did not waver, and he swore to protect Harry from the Dark Lord, honouring Lily's sacrifice.
</p><p>When Voldemort was reborn and called his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> to him, Snape did not appear until two hours later. The Dark Lord was suspicious, and feared that Snape had abandoned his service. On Dumbledore's orders, Severus claimed that his delayed return had secured the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a>'s continued trust. The Dark Lord questioned Snape extensively, and found all his answers satisfactory; Snape was then welcomed back to the inner circle.
</p><p>Voldemort's trust in Snape was further cemented when the latter murdered <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>; the Dark Lord did not know that Dumbledore had previously arranged the assassination with Snape. Snape became the Dark Lord's most trusted advisor and was given the position of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> after the <a href="/wiki/Fall_of_the_Ministry_of_Magic" title="Fall of the Ministry of Magic">Fall of the Ministry of Magic</a>. Unbeknownst to Voldemort, Snape continued to undermine him as much as possible, following Dumbledore's instructions.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest?cb=20161218210623" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B7C32M1 Nagini&#39;s attack on Snape.png" data-image-key="B7C32M1_Nagini&#39;s_attack_on_Snape.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161218210623" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest?cb=20161218210623" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161218210623" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B7C32M1 Nagini&#39;s attack on Snape.png" data-image-key="B7C32M1_Nagini&#39;s_attack_on_Snape.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161218210623" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort coldly orders Nagini to kill Snape</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> began to coordinate the defences of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">Hogwarts Castle</a> for the impending battle against Voldemort, Snape fled, and was summoned to the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a> by his Master soon afterwards. Snape saw that the Dark Lord had cast special protection around <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>, and attempted to leave the Shack to give Harry a message from Dumbledore (as Dumbledore had instructed Snape that, once Voldemort seemed to fear for the serpent's life, he was to tell Harry that Harry himself was Voldemort's seventh <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>, and therefore had to die) on the pretence that he would find Harry and ensure that he was killed by no hand other than Voldemort's own. Dismissing Snape's concerns, Voldemort noted that, since <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>'s murder, Snape had become the true master of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>. Voldemort ordered Nagini to kill Snape, and although he claimed he regretted the necessity of this action, he showed neither sadness nor concern for the loss of Snape's life. Harry, who had witnessed the scene and entered the room upon Voldemort's departure, approached Snape, who gave him several <a href="/wiki/Pensieve" title="Pensieve">memories</a> that both revealed his true allegiance and passed on Dumbledore's message. Snape's last words reflected his truest motives: he instructed Harry to look at him, so that he would die looking into the eyes Harry inherited from Lily Evans.
</p><p>In his final duel against Voldemort, Harry revealed that Snape had been loyal to Dumbledore since Voldemort had targeted the Potters. Rather than express shock or betrayal, Voldemort reacted with indifference to these revelations, as he believed that he was now the master of the Elder Wand. Voldemort also spurned Harry's explanations that killing Snape did not make him (Voldemort) the master of the Elder Wand, and that Draco Malfoy held that position. This mistake soon ended up costing Voldemort his life, thus ensuring that Snape's sacrifice was not in vain.
</p><p>One of the possible reasons why Voldemort placed so much trust in Snape was due to their rather similar backgrounds. Both men were the only children of <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> fathers and <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> mothers. Both men's fathers had nothing but hatred for their sons and wives—<a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle_Snr" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle Snr">Voldemort's father</a> had abandoned his <a href="/wiki/Merope_Riddle" title="Merope Riddle">wife</a> when she was pregnant with their son, while <a href="/wiki/Tobias_Snape" title="Tobias Snape">Snape's father</a> was abusive towards <a href="/wiki/Eileen_Prince" title="Eileen Prince">his wife Eileen</a> and their young <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">son</a>. Both Riddle and Snape claimed greater identification with their maternal lineage than their paternal ancestry—the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Gaunt" title="House of Gaunt">Gaunts</a> and <a href="/wiki/Prince_family" title="Prince family">Prince family</a>, respectively. Both men grew up in poverty—Voldemort grew up in an <a href="/wiki/Wool%27s_Orphanage" title="Wool&#39;s Orphanage">orphanage</a>, while Snape lived in <a href="/wiki/Spinner%27s_End" title="Spinner&#39;s End">Spinner's End</a>. In addition, both Riddle and Snape were sorted into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a>, and were known for their intelligence. Both men had a passion for the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a> and <a href="/wiki/Blood_status" title="Blood status">blood purity</a> in their childhoods, and bestowed grandiose titles onto themselves (Riddle was known as Lord Voldemort, while Snape adopted the name the Half-Blood Prince). Both saw <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> as sort of a real home as opposed to their default home. Voldemort may have seen him as a trusted Death Eater who shared the same hatred for his father as he had for his own. The only thing that differs between Voldemort and Snape's relationships with their fathers is murder; Voldemort had murdered his own father while Snape did <i>not</i> murder his.
</p><p>However, there were differences between Snape and Voldemort. Snape had a secret love for <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> for all his life, which motivated him to defect from the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> and protect her son, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, after her death at Voldemort's hands. Voldemort, on the other hand, disregarded love as a weakness that was beyond his comprehension, and had an allegiance to only himself. This had coincidentally led to his own undoing. Another difference was that while Voldemort grew up completely unaware of the wizarding world until he was eleven, Snape had apparently already known by the time he was nine (likely due to the fact that his <a href="/wiki/Eileen_Prince" title="Eileen Prince">mother</a> was a witch and, unlike Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Merope_Riddle" title="Merope Riddle">mother</a>, was actually present in her son's childhood).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Peter_Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=55" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Peter Pettigrew">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Peter Pettigrew"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>Your devotion is nothing more than cowardice. You would not be here if you had anywhere else to go.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort's opinion of Pettigrew<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140602041920" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="267" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Wormtail DH1.jpg" data-image-key="Wormtail_DH1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140602041920" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140602041920" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140602041920" decoding="async" width="180" height="267" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Wormtail DH1.jpg" data-image-key="Wormtail_DH1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140602041920" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Wormtail_DH1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, his servant</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p> Peter Pettigrew, one of Lord Voldemort's most cowardly servants, became a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> during Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">first rise to domination</a>, and betrayed <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a> to Voldemort in order to save his own life. After Voldemort's first defeat, Pettigrew made no attempt to find his master; he transformed into a rat, and passed into the ownership of <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a>. Voldemort accepted Pettigrew as a helpful servant, though made it clear he thought little of his cowardice and was fully aware that Pettigrew came to him for lack of any other options.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> escaped from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>, where he had been detained after Pettigrew framed him for his own crimes, and Black followed Pettigrew to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. By chance, after <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> convinced Black not to murder Pettigrew on the spot, he managed to transform back into a rat, and escaped. With nowhere else to go, Pettigrew fled to <a href="/wiki/Albania" title="Albania">Albania</a> to seek protection from Black in the service of Lord Voldemort. Pettigrew proved his usefulness by sending Voldemort <a href="/wiki/Bertha_Jorkins" title="Bertha Jorkins">Bertha Jorkins</a>, who told them where to find <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Bartemius Crouch Jnr</a>. Pettigrew later played a key role in <a href="/wiki/Return_of_the_Dark_Lord" class="mw-redirect" title="Return of the Dark Lord">Voldemort's rebirth</a> by sacrificing his hand to the <a href="/wiki/Regeneration_potion" title="Regeneration potion">potion</a> that allowed Voldemort to acquire a new body. Despite all this, Voldemort still reviled Pettigrew for his obvious cowardice and past loyalty issues, and spoke in utter contempt for his servant. During meetings and missions, Wormtail was assigned to the most menial of tasks, such as jailer or dogsbody to Severus Snape, highlighting how unimportant he was in the organisation. Despite this, he forced <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a> to construct a new wand for Pettigrew, possibly as a further reward for his service.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, Pettigrew was killed by the <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew%27s_silver_hand" title="Peter Pettigrew&#39;s silver hand">silver hand</a> Voldemort had given him when he hesitated during an attempt to strangle Harry Potter, a fate likely similar to whatever punishment Pettigrew would've received from Voldemort himself for this. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Malfoy_family">The Malfoy family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=56" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Malfoy family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: The Malfoy family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>Lucius, my slippery friend, I am told that you have not renounced the old ways, though to the world you present a respectable face. You are still ready to take the lead in a spot of Muggle-torture, I believe? Yet you never tried to find me, Lucius. . . . Your exploits at the Quidditch World Cup were fun, I daresay. . . but might not your energies have been better directed toward finding and aiding your master?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort's disappointment in Lucius' cowardice and disloyalty<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH1_The_Malfoy_Family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200929193628" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH1 The Malfoy Family.png" data-image-key="DH1_The_Malfoy_Family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH1_The_Malfoy_Family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200929193628" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH1_The_Malfoy_Family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200929193628" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH1_The_Malfoy_Family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200929193628" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 The Malfoy Family.png" data-image-key="DH1_The_Malfoy_Family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH1_The_Malfoy_Family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200929193628" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_The_Malfoy_Family.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoy family</a>, his former servants</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Voldemort entrusted <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>: his diary, which made possible the reopening of the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>. The Dark Lord was enraged to hear, years later, that the diary had been carelessly handed to <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>. Lucius appeared not to have known that the object concealed a part of his master's soul, as in all likelihood, Voldemort had only told him that the object was enchanted to reopen the Chamber.
</p><p>Lucius pretended to have been under the <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a> after the Dark Lord's first downfall, and maintained a position of influence within the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> until the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> began. When Voldemort was reborn, he welcomed Lucius into his inner circle, though he reprimanded Malfoy for running from the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a> conjured at the <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_World_Cup" title="Quidditch World Cup">Quidditch World Cup</a>.
</p><p>Lucius quickly began to lose favour, however, after Voldemort heard about the diary's destruction. When the Death Eaters under his command lost the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> and failed to retrieve the <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">Prophecy</a>, the Dark Lord was extremely displeased; Lucius was sent to prison after the battle and, as punishment for the elder Malfoy's failure, Voldemort gave his son <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> the nearly impossible task of murdering <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, with the expectation that he, too, would fail, and then be punished accordingly by the Dark Lord. Though Draco more or less succeeded in fulfilling his mission, Voldemort continued to distrust the Malfoys' loyalty. He dwelt at <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a> for a while, and suspected that the family resented him for doing so. During his stay at the Manor, Voldemort used Draco as a pawn, forcing him to torture other Death Eaters, which effectively humiliated the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoy</a> pride.
</p><p>The following year, after <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> managed to escape from the Manor, Voldemort tortured Lucius and began to treat him with complete disdain. <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Malfoy</a> then focused on rescuing his son from <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, fearing only for Draco's life and seemed to abandon all loyalty to the Death Eaters' cause. In addition, Draco's <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">defeat</a> at the hands of Harry won the latter the allegiance of the Elder Wand. Voldemort snubbed Lucius' concerns for Draco and jeered that perhaps the teenager had chosen to ally himself with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> when he did not leave the school with the other <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherins</a>.
</p><p>After Voldemort succeeded in casting the <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a> on <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a> was ordered to confirm the death. Harry was alive, however, and Narcissa, concerned for her son, demanded news of Draco from Harry and, upon learning that Draco was alive and well, lied to the Dark Lord, stating that Harry was dead. She knew that she and Lucius would only be able to return to Hogwarts and reunite with their son if they were part of a victory party. These events allowed Harry to confront Voldemort for the last time. During their final duel, Harry informed Voldemort of Draco's gaining of the Elder Wand's allegiance, which Harry himself had earned after his (Harry's) defeat of Draco a few months earlier. In response, Voldemort stated that these turn of events "[made] no difference" between them and threatened that he would "attend to (i.e., kill)" Draco after killing Harry, likely as punishment not only for Draco's unintentional interference in Voldemort's plans, but also for Narcissa's deception and Lucius' failures. Fortunately for the Malfoys, this was not to be, as the Dark Lord was killed by a rebounding <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a>. Narcissa's instrumental intervention ensured that the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoys</a> were not convicted for their crimes.
</p><p>By <a href="/wiki/2020" title="2020">2020</a>, Draco had become so disillusioned from the Death Eater cause due to his experiences with Voldemort that he (Draco) helped the Trio defeat Voldemort's daughter <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a> in her plan to save Voldemort from <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_Godric%27s_Hollow_(1981)" title="Attack at Godric&#39;s Hollow (1981)">his first downfall</a> back in 1981. What was rather remarkable about Draco's involvement is this escapade was that Delphini was the illegitimate daughter of Draco's aunt Bellatrix, and therefore Draco's cousin. This defiance of Delphini and Voldemort demonstrated that Draco wanted so little to do with his erstwhile master that even having the Dark Lord's daughter being a blood relative was a repugnant notion to him. Draco also might have been motivated by a desire to redeem himself from his Death Eater past. During this period in his life, Draco also began referring to Voldemort by his name rather than the "Dark Lord" as he did in his youth, which might have been motivated by his self-redemption.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Death_Eaters">Death Eaters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=57" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Death Eaters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Death Eaters"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>Welcome, Death Eaters. Thirteen years. . . thirteen years since last we met. Yet you answer my call as though it were yesterday, we are still united under the Dark Mark, then! Or are we?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort viciously greeting his Death Eaters in <a href="/wiki/Little_Hangleton_graveyard" title="Little Hangleton graveyard">Little Hangleton graveyard</a> following his resurrection, expressing his disappointment.<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091129164509" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="247" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Unidentified Death Eater (II).jpg" data-image-key="Unidentified_Death_Eater_(II).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20091129164509" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091129164509" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20091129164509" decoding="async" width="180" height="247" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Unidentified Death Eater (II).jpg" data-image-key="Unidentified_Death_Eater_(II).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20091129164509" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Unidentified_Death_Eater_(II).jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, his devoted servants</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Those called Death Eaters were a group of <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizards</a> and Witches that followed Voldemort, fighting as the upper echelon of his army during both the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First</a> and <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding Wars</a>. However, Voldemort did not take kindly to failure or disloyalty from his servants, and he made sure those who had believed him dead and did not try to find him following his disappearance paid the price upon his return. When he summoned his Death Eaters to the <a href="/wiki/Little_Hangleton_graveyard" title="Little Hangleton graveyard">Little Hangleton graveyard</a>, after he regained his body, he tortured and questioned them before forgiving and allowing them back into his service.
</p><p>Despite many of the Death Eaters claiming to be close to Voldemort, and Voldemort often referring to them as his "friends" and his "true family", the Dark Lord saw them as little more than dispensable servants. The few Death Eaters in whom Voldemort appeared to place any amount of genuine trust were <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rabastan_Lestrange" title="Rabastan Lestrange">Rabastan Lestrange</a> though, as time passed, he lost trust in them due to constant failures or wavering trust.
</p><p>Some of Lord Voldemort's first Death Eaters were <a href="/wiki/Avery_(Riddle-era)" class="mw-redirect" title="Avery (Riddle-era)">Avery Snr</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lestrange" title="Lestrange">Lestrange</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mulciber_(Riddle-era)" class="mw-redirect" title="Mulciber (Riddle-era)">Mulciber Snr</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nott" title="Nott">Nott</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rosier" title="Rosier">Rosier</a> and <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>. Others were <a href="/wiki/Walden_Macnair" title="Walden Macnair">Walden Macnair</a>, <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Corban Yaxley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Augustus_Rookwood" title="Augustus Rookwood">Augustus Rookwood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Selwyn" title="Selwyn">Selwyn</a>, <a href="/wiki/Travers" title="Travers">Travers</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">Alecto and Amycus Carrow</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gibbon" title="Gibbon">Gibbon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Crabbe" title="Crabbe">Crabbe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Goyle" title="Goyle">Goyle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jugson" title="Jugson">Jugson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Avery_(Marauder-era)" class="mw-redirect" title="Avery (Marauder-era)">Avery Jnr</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mulciber_(Marauder-era)" class="mw-redirect" title="Mulciber (Marauder-era)">Mulciber Jnr</a>, <a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a>, <a href="/wiki/Evan_Rosier" title="Evan Rosier">Evan Rosier</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wilkes" title="Wilkes">Wilkes</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/DH2_Bellatrix_laughing.gif/revision/latest?cb=20180607215625" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH2 Bellatrix laughing.gif" data-image-key="DH2_Bellatrix_laughing.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/DH2_Bellatrix_laughing.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180607215625" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/DH2_Bellatrix_laughing.gif/revision/latest?cb=20180607215625" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/DH2_Bellatrix_laughing.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180607215625" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH2 Bellatrix laughing.gif" data-image-key="DH2_Bellatrix_laughing.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/DH2_Bellatrix_laughing.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180607215625" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH2_Bellatrix_laughing.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">"<i>His last best lieutenant</i>", <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Like Voldemort himself, many were not above denying any involvement in actions that could get them into trouble with the legal authorities of the magical community. Many were willing to switch their loyalties to avoid danger or punishment, rather than steadfastly supporting their presented views.
</p><p>After Voldemort's first downfall: <a href="/wiki/Avery_(Riddle-era)" class="mw-redirect" title="Avery (Riddle-era)">Avery, Jnr</a> claimed to have been under the <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a> and avoided <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> but also didn't attempt to find his master. Voldemort never hesitated to punish Avery for his incompetence or simply for annoying him. The <a href="/wiki/Carrow_family" title="Carrow family">Carrow</a> siblings <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto</a> did not attempt to find him. Given Amycus (at the very least)' cowardly nature, it is likely that at the very least he would have done all he could to avoid Azkaban. Other Death Eaters who didn't try to find him were <a href="/wiki/Crabbe" title="Crabbe">Crabbe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Goyle" title="Goyle">Goyle</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Nott" title="Nott">Nott</a>, though Nott claimed to be Voldemort's most faithful servant only to be silenced by his master.
</p><p>Other individuals who showed disloyalty were <a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a> who betrayed many of his former comrades to the Ministry in return for his freedom from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>, and went on to become Headmaster of <a href="/wiki/Durmstrang_Institute" title="Durmstrang Institute">Durmstrang Institute</a>. Though he was still a <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> supremacist and did not accept <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a> into his school, Karkaroff fled following Voldemort's return and was consequently killed by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>. <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a> joined Voldemort out of cowardice, but did not attempt to search for him following his first downfall, so he hid from his fellow Death Eaters in the form of the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a> pet rat Scabbers and only rejoined him when he was flushed out by <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> who he framed for his own crimes. <a href="/wiki/Walden_Macnair" title="Walden Macnair">Walden Macnair</a> claimed to have been under the Imperius Curse to avoid Azkaban and did not attempt to find Voldemort after his first downfall. 
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Corban Yaxley</a> managed to avoid Azkaban and did not attempt to find Voldemort after his downfall, believing him finished. Despite this he was still given a lot of responsibility such as the task of recruiting <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, leading the Death Eater controlled Ministry of Magic, and escorting Harry Potter to his death.
</p><p>On the other hand, the <a href="/wiki/Lestrange_family" title="Lestrange family">Lestrange family</a> remained loyal to Voldemort, with <a href="/wiki/Rabastan_Lestrange" title="Rabastan Lestrange">Rabastan Lestrange</a>, his brother <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus Lestrange</a> and sister-in-law to the former/wife to the latter <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange (née Black)</a> going to Azkaban instead of publicly forsaking him. Voldemort greatly appreciated their loyalty and promised to honour them beyond the dreams of wizards. It's unknown how Rodolphus felt about his wife having feelings for Voldemort, though as he himself was highly devoted to his master, he may have supported it.
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Mulciber_family" title="Mulciber family">Mulciber family</a> served him faithfully with both the <a href="/wiki/Mulciber_(Riddle-era)" class="mw-redirect" title="Mulciber (Riddle-era)">Snr</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Mulciber_(Marauder-era)" class="mw-redirect" title="Mulciber (Marauder-era)">Jnr</a> Mulciber fighting for him and the younger even going to Azkaban for him. The <a href="/wiki/Rosier_family" title="Rosier family">Rosier family</a> served him faithfully, with <a href="/wiki/Rosier" title="Rosier">Rosier</a> being among his first Death Eaters and <a href="/wiki/Evan_Rosier" title="Evan Rosier">Evan Rosier</a> dying for him during the First War.
</p><p>Other individuals who served him faithfully were <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>, <a href="/wiki/Augustus_Rookwood" title="Augustus Rookwood">Augustus Rookwood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Travers" title="Travers">Travers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wilkes" title="Wilkes">Wilkes</a>. The first three went to Azkaban for him while the last was killed by Aurors during the First War. Rookwood was instrumental in Voldemort's plan to retrieve the prophecy, and was spared Voldemort's wrath when delivering him bad news (Avery was tortured instead). While Dolohov was one of the more devoted Death Eaters, this did not save him from being brutally tortured when he, along with Rowle, summoned Voldemort before capturing Harry.
</p><p>Both <a href="/wiki/Regulus_Black" title="Regulus Black">Regulus Black</a> II and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> defected after becoming disillusioned with the Death Eater lifestyle. The later also defected to protect <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> whose husband <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter I</a> and son <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> were targeted by Lord Voldemort for death, whereas the former defected for the wellfare of Kreacher.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Gibbon" title="Gibbon">Gibbon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jugson" title="Jugson">Jugson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Selwyn" title="Selwyn">Selwyn</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a> were also amongst those who served Lord Voldemort. Whether they had forsaken him or not is unknown.
</p><p>Although <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> is not a true Death Eater, Voldemort offered him the privilege to wear their robes in exchange for his services. While Voldemort saw Greyback as a valuable asset in threatening to set him loose onto people who refused to cooperate, he did not hold the werewolf in the same regard as genuine Death Eaters, and did not brand him with the Dark Mark. Fenrir joined up with Voldemort not for ideologies, but for greater access to victims of <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">werewolfry infection</a>, and did not attempt to find Voldemort after his first downfall. Regardless, the werewolf did resent the fact that he was not being treated with the same level of respect as Voldemort's inner circle (such as not having the Mark), many of whom regarded him with disgust and neglect. Indeed, while it is clear that Voldemort only treated all of his subordinates as tools for his bidding, his low respect for Fenrir made it even more apparent.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Armando_Dippet">Armando Dippet</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=58" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Armando Dippet">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Armando Dippet"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>While as a student at Hogwarts, Tom Riddle was a polite and intelligent young man who charmed almost all the staff members of Hogwarts. <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a>, in particular, was fond of Riddle. Dippet did not allow Riddle to remain in Hogwarts during the <a href="/wiki/Summer_holidays" title="Summer holidays">summer holidays</a> due to the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> opening at the time (unaware that Riddle was the one who opened it), but would have made special arrangements if the situation was safer. When Tom framed <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> for the crime, Armando accepted the model student's actions as honest heroism without questioning him, and merited him a <a href="/wiki/Special_Award_for_Services_to_the_School" title="Special Award for Services to the School">Special Award for Services to the School</a>. When Riddle was about to finish his education, he attempted to request Professor Dippet to remain at Hogwarts as the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher, to which Dippet refused on account that the newly graduated was too inexperienced, but invited him to reapply in a few years if he remain interested.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Horace_Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=59" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Horace Slughorn">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Horace Slughorn"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I am not proud… I am ashamed of what — of what that memory shows… I think I may have done great damage that day.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Horace Slughorn talking about Tom Riddle<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Horace_Slughorn_%28HBP_promo%29_1-1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100706114608" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="228" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Horace Slughorn (HBP promo) 1-1.jpg" data-image-key="Horace_Slughorn_(HBP_promo)_1-1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Horace_Slughorn_%28HBP_promo%29_1-1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100706114608" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Horace_Slughorn_%28HBP_promo%29_1-1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100706114608" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Horace_Slughorn_%28HBP_promo%29_1-1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100706114608" decoding="async" width="180" height="228" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Horace Slughorn (HBP promo) 1-1.jpg" data-image-key="Horace_Slughorn_(HBP_promo)_1-1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/Horace_Slughorn_%28HBP_promo%29_1-1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100706114608" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Horace_Slughorn_(HBP_promo)_1-1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, his former Head of House and one of those who admired him</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Professor Horace Slughorn was the <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">master</a> during Tom Riddle's years at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. Tom Riddle was a member of the <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club" title="Slug Club">Slug Club</a>, a "collection" of Slughorn's favourite students, including students who were well connected, and those who proved to be talented and appeared to have potential for great success. At some point during Tom Riddle's time at Hogwarts, he asked Slughorn about <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>. Slughorn initially baulked, but under the influence of Riddle's charm, convinced himself that Tom was asking for "purely academic" reasons and told him what tearing one's soul would basically entail. Most significantly, Tom asked if it was possible to make more than one Horcrux; while the question shocked and horrified Slughorn, he didn't deny that it was possible. With the information he received from Slughorn, Tom Riddle affirmed his decision to create six Horcruxes; ultimately, this would tear his soul into a total of seven separate pieces—seven being the "most powerfully magical number"—and allow him to effectively achieve some degree of immortality. Ashamed of having so badly misjudged Tom Riddle, and for the part he played in providing Riddle with such destructive information, Slughorn modified his own memory.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Slughorn left retirement and returned to Hogwarts to replace <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> as Potions master. <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> gave <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> the task being "collected" by Slughorn and retrieving the original version of the memory. Harry managed to get the memory from Slughorn in 1997, with the help of <a href="/wiki/Felix_Felicis" title="Felix Felicis">Felix Felicis</a>, copious amounts of <a href="/wiki/Mead" title="Mead">mead</a>, and Slughorn's fondness for Harry's mother, who had been another of Slughorn's favourites. The memory confirmed suspicions Dumbledore had about the steps Voldemort had taken to become immortal, which proved to be of vital importance in Voldemort's ultimate defeat.
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Slughorn, who initially appeared to flee the school, brought reinforcements from <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> to join the fight against the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, and later duelled directly against Voldemort with <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ginny_Weasley">Ginny Weasley</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=60" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ginny Weasley">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Ginny Weasley"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>...I was patient. I wrote back. I was sympathetic, I was kind. Ginny simply loved me... No one's ever understood me like you, Tom... I'm so glad I've got this diary to confide in... It's like a friend I can carry around in my pocket... If I say it myself, Harry, I've always been able to charm the people I needed.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Tom Riddle to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> on his manipulation of Ginny<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190125210110" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="224" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="COS promo Ginny Weasley T. M. Riddle&#39;s Diary.jpg" data-image-key="COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle&#39;s_Diary.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190125210110" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190125210110" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190125210110" decoding="async" width="180" height="224" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="COS promo Ginny Weasley T. M. Riddle&#39;s Diary.jpg" data-image-key="COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle&#39;s_Diary.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190125210110" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:COS_promo_Ginny_Weasley_T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny in her first year with Tom  Riddle's diary</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Although Voldemort had lost his physical body, he managed to approach <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, a first year <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> girl and younger sister of <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> who had a huge crush on <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, through one of his <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>: <a href="/wiki/T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary" title="T. M. Riddle&#39;s Diary">his diary</a>. Tom Riddle's <a href="/wiki/Soul" title="Soul">soul</a> communicated with Ginny through his diary, sympathising with her problems and giving her advice, which made her emotionally vulnerable to Riddle's influence. As this fragment of his soul was preserved as his 16-year old self, prior to the later disfigurements, Tom Riddle was able to use his earlier good looks to make girls swoon as he had done decades earlier, in this case making an insecure girl feel valued that a tall, dark and handsome man took an interest in her problems. Eventually, Riddle was able to possess Ginny, use her to open the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> and free <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">Salazar Slytherin's Basilisk</a> to petrify several <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> students (including <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>). When Ginny figured out what she had been doing, despite having no memory of what happened during the times she was possessed, she attempted to flush the diary down a toilet; however, as the diary was a Horcrux, it remained undamaged and later ended up in the hands of Harry Potter himself.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140407011351" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="100" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginevra Weasley Writing on the Wall.gif" data-image-key="Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140407011351" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140407011351" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140407011351" decoding="async" width="245" height="100" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginevra Weasley Writing on the Wall.gif" data-image-key="Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140407011351" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginevra_Weasley_Writing_on_the_Wall.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A possessed Ginny writing a message on the wall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny, worried the Diary would reveal to Harry things she'd written about <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">her feelings for him</a>, stole the diary back. Riddle possessed Ginny one last time and had her enter the Chamber of Secrets, with every intention of killing her and using her life to restore his own. Harry, however, as a <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parselmouth</a>, was able to enter the Chamber, rescue Ginny, and slay the Basilisk with the <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Godric Gryffindor's Sword</a>. He then used one of the Basilisk's <a href="/wiki/Basilisk_venom" title="Basilisk venom">fangs</a> to stab the Diary, effectively making it the first of Voldemort's Horcruxes to be destroyed.
</p><p>Despite being outwardly sympathetic and understanding, Riddle actually felt great contempt for Ginny, viewing her as "silly" and describing her as "stupid little Ginny". He considered her "boring" at first, but thought that her diary entries became "far more interesting" after he started possessing her as he apparently found her confusion amusing. Ginny's retrieval of the diary angered Riddle as he had hoped to learn more about Harry Potter. When Voldemort's lieutenant, <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix</a>, was <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley%27s_curse" title="Molly Weasley&#39;s curse">killed</a> by Ginny's mother <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a> in retaliation for nearly killing Ginny, Voldemort nearly turned his wand on both mother and daughter. However, this gave Harry the incentive to reveal his being still-alive. Ginny and her surviving relatives all saw Harry <a href="/wiki/Voldemort%27s_Last_Stand" title="Voldemort&#39;s Last Stand">defeat</a> Voldemort shortly thereafter. It was unknown to Voldemort that Ginny had won Harry's heart in her fifth year, but he might have suspected it.
