In addition, Ginny would marry Harry some point after Voldemort's death, making her the Dark Lord's distant cousin-in-law (albeit while Voldemort was dead).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rubeus_Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=61" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Rubeus Hagrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Rubeus Hagrid"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>Monsters don't make good pets, Hagrid.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Riddle before he turned Hagrid in<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a0/Rubeus_Hagrid_promo.png/revision/latest?cb=20161121052620" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="225" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rubeus Hagrid promo.png" data-image-key="Rubeus_Hagrid_promo.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a0/Rubeus_Hagrid_promo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161121052620" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a0/Rubeus_Hagrid_promo.png/revision/latest?cb=20161121052620" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a0/Rubeus_Hagrid_promo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161121052620" decoding="async" width="180" height="225" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rubeus Hagrid promo.png" data-image-key="Rubeus_Hagrid_promo.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a0/Rubeus_Hagrid_promo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161121052620" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rubeus_Hagrid_promo.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, his determined enemy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Rubeus Hagrid and Tom Riddle were both students at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> in the <a href="/wiki/1940s" title="1940s">1940s</a>, with Hagrid being three years his junior. In 1943, Riddle opened the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, unleashing a <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">Basilisk</a> on the school's <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> students. Most of the students who were attacked ended up <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrified</a>, but when the Basilisk finally succeeded in killing <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">one of them</a>, Hogwarts became in danger of closing—a consequence Riddle hadn't foreseen, which would mean him having to return indefinitely to <a href="/wiki/Wool%27s_Orphanage" title="Wool&#39;s Orphanage">Wool's Orphanage</a>. Upon realising the school might not have to close if the perpetrator were caught, Riddle stopped attacking students with the Basilisk, closed the Chamber of Secrets, and framed Hagrid, who was known for his love of dangerous <a href="/wiki/Creature" title="Creature">Creatures</a> and at the time was raising <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>, a young <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a>, for the crime. Hagrid managed to protect Aragog and even threw Riddle to the ground when he tried to curse him, making Hagrid the only person to challenge Riddle while he was a student. Despite this, Hagrid was expelled from Hogwarts, and the school was allowed to remain open. Believing in Hagrid's innocence, however, Professor <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> convinced Headmaster <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a> to allow Hagrid to stay on at Hogwarts as <a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">Gamekeeper</a>.
</p><p>Tom Riddle never felt remorse for framing Hagrid and ruining his life. As Riddle went on to become Voldemort, Hagrid joined the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and fought against Lord Voldemort and his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> in the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. In <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>, Hagrid was devastated when Voldemort murdered his friends <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a>, but shared in the relief of the rest of the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">Wizarding world</a> when Voldemort lost his powers and disappeared after failing to kill young <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. Although many believed that Voldemort was dead, Hagrid, agreeing with Dumbledore, believed that he would one day return to power. Along with the vast majority of the Wizarding community, Hagrid refused to say Voldemort's name, generally referring to him as "You-know-who" although he once reluctantly said Voldemort's name when explaining his background to Harry. When Voldemort was searching for the Philosopher's Stone, he took advantage of Hagrid's love and knowledge of magical creatures and through Quirinus Quirrell, gathered the secret of subduing <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a> through music from a drunken Hagrid, who was remorseful afterwards. Since Voldemort had a certain respect for Hogwart's professors, it is not known if that included Hagrid, who taught <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a>. This is unlikely considering Hagrid's half-giant status.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, after his resurrection, Voldemort dispatched his Death Eaters to convince the <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giants</a> to join their side, while Dumbledore had sent Hagrid and <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Olympe Maxime</a> to do the same. While Hagrid and Maxime were on good terms with the Gurg, <a href="/wiki/Karkus" title="Karkus">Karkus</a>, the Death Eaters supported the giant <a href="/wiki/Golgomath" title="Golgomath">Golgomath</a> in an uprising that resulted in Golgomath beheading Karkus and taking over the giant colony. The giants then attacked Hagrid and Maxime, who were forced to retreat.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, Hagrid fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> and was captured by the Death Eaters. After Harry sacrificed himself to be killed, Voldemort ordered a grieving Hagrid to carry his friend's "dead" body in his arms, where it would be clearly visible to Harry's supporters. When Harry finally defeated the Dark Lord, Hagrid was amongst the first few who were able to congratulate him on his triumph.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Quirinus_Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=62" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Quirinus Quirrell">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Quirinus Quirrell"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>Then . . . four years ago . . . the means for my return seemed assured. A wizard - young, foolish, and gullible - wandered across my path in the forest I had made my home. Oh, he seemed the very chance I had been dreaming of... for he was a teacher at Dumbledore's school... he was easy to bend to my will... he brought me back to this country, and after a while, I took possession of his body, to supervise him closely as he carried out my orders. But my plan failed. I did not manage to steal the Philosopher's Stone. I was not to be assured immortal life. I was thwarted . . . thwarted, once again, by Harry Potter. ...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort's control and possession of Quirrell<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e9/Quirinus_Quirrel.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110806132643" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Quirinus Quirrel.jpg" data-image-key="Quirinus_Quirrel.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e9/Quirinus_Quirrel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110806132643" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e9/Quirinus_Quirrel.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110806132643" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e9/Quirinus_Quirrel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110806132643" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Quirinus Quirrel.jpg" data-image-key="Quirinus_Quirrel.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e9/Quirinus_Quirrel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110806132643" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Quirinus_Quirrel.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a>, his loyal servant</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Quirinus Quirrell encountered Lord Voldemort's disembodied soul fragment in the <a href="/wiki/Albania" title="Albania">Black Forest of Albania</a>, during his world travels. Originally naively trying to capture the Dark Lord's remains, Quirrell overestimated himself thinking he could subjugate Voldemort and learn powerful magic from him. With promises of wealth, domination and possibly immortality, Voldemort convinced Quirrell to become his faithful servant, and even to share his body. Quirrell followed orders with a tint of fear, and at times tried, feebly and futilely, to resist the possession.
</p><p>On Voldemort's orders, Quirrell returned to <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a> and <a href="/wiki/1991_Break-In_of_Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" class="mw-redirect" title="1991 Break-In of Gringotts Wizarding Bank">broke into</a> <a href="/wiki/Vault_713" title="Vault 713">Vault 713</a> at <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts Wizarding Bank</a> to procure the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a>, only to find that it had been emptied earlier that day and the Stone transferred to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> by <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>.
</p><p>Quirrell took the position of <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a> of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> at Hogwarts, with the aim of tracking down the Stone. When he and Voldemort realised <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> was starting at Hogwarts that same year, Quirrell attempted to kill Harry, but was prevented from doing so first by <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, then, unwittingly, by <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone"><b>Voldemort</b>: "<i>Seize him! SEIZE HIM!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Quirrell</b>: "<i>Master, I cannot hold him -- my hands -- my hands!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Voldemort</b>: "<i>Then kill him, fool, and be done!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Voldemort furiously demanding Quirrell kill Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Quirrell once again turned his attention to finding the Philosopher's Stone, and overcame several enchanted obstacles to travel through the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone_Chambers" class="mw-redirect" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone Chambers">Philosopher's Stone Chambers</a>. Harry followed Quirrell through the Chambers, believing he was actually following Severus Snape, and eventually found Quirrell attempting to retrieve the Stone from the <a href="/wiki/Mirror_of_Erised" title="Mirror of Erised">Mirror of Erised</a> in the final chamber. Voldemort ordered Quirrell to use Harry to get the stone, and when the Stone appeared in Harry's pocket, Harry attempted to conceal the fact by lying about what he saw in the Mirror. Voldemort, seeing through Harry's lie, offered Harry power and glory, and even the possibility of seeing his parents again, in exchange for joining him and handing over the stone. Upon Harry's refusal, Voldemort ordered Quirrell to take the Stone by force, but found that Quirrell was unable to touch the boy without enduring excruciating pain as a result of the protection afforded to Harry by his mother's loving <a href="/wiki/Sacrificial_protection" title="Sacrificial protection">sacrifice</a>. To escape the pain, Voldemort separated his soul from Quirrell's body and fled, leaving Quirrell to die; Dumbledore noted that this was an act of Voldemort's mercilessness on his subordinates as much as towards his enemies.
</p><p>Three years after abandoning Quirrell to his demise, Voldemort expressed to his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> that he saw Quirrell as a foolish and gullible man whose only value was his position at Hogwarts.
</p>
<h3><span id="Wool's_Orphanage_residents"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Wool.27s_Orphanage_residents">Wool's Orphanage residents</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=63" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Wool&#039;s Orphanage residents">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Wool&#039;s Orphanage residents"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I can make things move without touching them. I can make animals do what I want them to do, without training them. I can make bad things happen to people who annoy me. I can make them hurt if I want to. I knew I was different. I knew I was special. Always, I knew there was something</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;A young Riddle explaining his difference and distance from, and disdain for the other Orphanage residents<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Tom Riddle grew up at the <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> <a href="/wiki/Wool%27s_Orphanage" title="Wool&#39;s Orphanage">orphanage</a> where his <a href="/wiki/Merope_Riddle" title="Merope Riddle">mother</a> brought him shortly before her death in <a href="/wiki/1926" title="1926">1926</a>.
</p><p>Tom's relationship with the other residents of the orphanage was strained, to say the least. Some of the orphanage's staff, such as Mrs Cole, believed that his mother had originated from a circus due to his middle name. Tom was never given sufficient attention from the staff due to his independent nature nurtured by a lack of parental love, as he rarely cried as an infant, and his peculiar nature distanced him from the others. When <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, then professor at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>, arrived at the orphanage to invite Tom to attend Hogwarts, Tom initially believed that <a href="/wiki/Cole" title="Cole">Mrs Cole</a>, the orphanage's matron, had called Dumbledore to take him to an asylum; Tom defensively insulted Cole for the one being insane and should be sent to an asylum instead. Dumbledore discovered that Tom had been bullying the other children, namely <a href="/wiki/Amy_Benson" title="Amy Benson">Amy Benson</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dennis_Bishop" title="Dennis Bishop">Dennis Bishop</a>, and that he had a habit of keeping trophies to signify the terror he was able to cause. He knew he was different from the other children; he was intelligent and far more powerful than his peers, and had no issue with punishing those who did not do as he told them. When Dumbledore assured him that he wasn't from an asylum, and that Tom was, in fact, a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>, Riddle was unusually quick to believe him, having always considered himself "special."
</p><p>Riddle hated the orphanage, which was a reminder of the poor and common start to his life; ultimately, he thought of Hogwarts as his first and real home. He would dread returning to the facility during the <a href="/wiki/Summer_holidays" title="Summer holidays">summer holidays</a>, even requesting then-<a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Dippet</a> to let him remain in school instead. Upon graduating, Riddle departed from the orphanage for good, distancing himself from it by immersing in the path of dark magic, and refused to use it as a hiding place for one of his <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hepzibah_Smith">Hepzibah Smith</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=64" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hepzibah Smith">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Hepzibah Smith"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>You naughty boy, you shouldn't have! You do spoil this old lady, Tom.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hepzibah Smith, in response to Riddle bringing her flowers on the day she showed him <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">The Locket of Slytherin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Helga_Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Helga Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup">The Cup of Hufflepuff</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Tom Riddle first met <a href="/wiki/Hepzibah_Smith" title="Hepzibah Smith">Hepzibah Smith</a> when he worked at <a href="/wiki/Borgin_and_Burkes" title="Borgin and Burkes">Borgin and Burkes</a>. As a polite, handsome, and clever young man with a great capacity to charm and a powerful gift of persuasion, he became friendly with Hepzibah, flattering her and making her feel pretty. He convinced her to show him two of her greatest treasures—<a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a> and <a href="/wiki/Helga_Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Helga Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup">Helga Hufflepuff's Cup</a>—which he planned to steal and turn into <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>. He killed Hepzibah two days later by mixing a lethal and little-known poison into her cocoa, and took the two artefacts. He was never suspected in her murder, as he framed Smith's house-elf, <a href="/wiki/Hokey" title="Hokey">Hokey</a>, by modifying the elf's memory. Prior to her death, Hepzibah realised too late of Tom's greed for the treasures, which led her affections to falter somewhat. Riddle was remorseless for his role in Smith's death, and even used it to turn the Cup into a Horcrux.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gellert_Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=65" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Gellert Grindelwald">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Gellert Grindelwald"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>It is unknown if Voldemort and Grindelwald had ever met each other prior to 1998. It is unknown what Voldemort's personal views on Grindelwald's atrocities towards Muggles were or his attempted revolution to subjugate them though it is likely he did not care and took no inspiration from Grindelwald for his own attempted conquests later on. Despite Grindelwald's status as one of the most powerful dark wizards to have ever existed, inferior only to Voldemort himself, he seemed to have no praise or respect for the elder dark wizard and treated him as merely another person to interogate in his search for the Elder Wand.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 208px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20190817172422" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="206" height="85" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort and Grindelwald.JPG" data-image-key="Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/206?cb=20190817172422" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20190817172422" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/206?cb=20190817172422" decoding="async" width="206" height="85" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort and Grindelwald.JPG" data-image-key="Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/206?cb=20190817172422" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_and_Grindelwald.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Grindelwald speaking to Voldemort in Nurmengard, seconds before his death</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>By the time Voldemort visited Grindelwald in his Nurmengard prison in 1998, Grindelwald seemed to know all about him, and claimed that he knew that Voldemort would one day visit him to seek out the Elder Wand. Despite being trapped and completely defenceless against one of the few wizards more powerful than himself,, Grindelwald showed no fear towards the Dark Lord, and 
laughed, scornfully challenging Voldemort to kill him, using the younger wizard’s chosen name in contempt of his great power, much to the latter's fury. Grindelwald refused to tell Voldemort the Elder Wand's location and taunted him by telling him that he would never be able to master the wand. Furious at his inability to gain information from the former master of the Elder Wand, Voldemort’s fury eventually broke, and he murdered Grindelwald with the Killing Curse. 
Ultimately, Grindelwald's prediction of Voldemort never fully mastering the Elder Wand would become reality, and would cause Voldemort's own demise during his final duel with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Order_of_the_Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=66" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150206155602" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix – first generation.jpg" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix_–_first_generation.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150206155602" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150206155602" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150206155602" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix – first generation.jpg" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix_–_first_generation.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150206155602" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, his enemies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Order of the Phoenix was a secret organisation founded and led by <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> to oppose Voldemort and his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>.
</p><p>Though it was unknown to Voldemort till shortly before his defeat, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> was a member of the Order who had defected from the Death Eaters and worked for Dumbledore as a spy shortly after Voldemort began hunting <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a>.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a> were members of the Order who became prime targets for Voldemort during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>, after Voldemort heard of a prophecy foretelling of a child destined to destroy him. This fit the description of their young son, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>. On <a href="/wiki/31_October" title="31 October">31 October</a>, <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>, Voldemort found the Potters after the <a href="/wiki/Fidelius_Charm" title="Fidelius Charm">Fidelius Charm</a> they had cast was broken by <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>. Voldemort killed James first and ordered Lily to stand aside, so he could kill Harry. When Lily refused to stand aside, Voldemort killed her as well, making her murder a <a href="/wiki/Sacrificial_protection" title="Sacrificial protection">sacrifice</a> that caused the Killing Curse Voldemort aimed at Harry to backfire; Voldemort lost his body and fled to <a href="/wiki/Albania" title="Albania">Albania</a>.
</p><p>Shortly after Voldemort lost his powers in 1981, the <a href="/wiki/Longbottom_family" title="Longbottom family">Longbottom family</a> suffered at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, her husband <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus</a>, her brother-in-law <a href="/wiki/Rabastan_Lestrange" title="Rabastan Lestrange">Rabastan</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>, who tortured <a href="/wiki/Alice_Longbottom" title="Alice Longbottom">Alice</a> and <a href="/wiki/Frank_Longbottom" title="Frank Longbottom">Frank Longbottom</a>, new parents to <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, to the point of insanity. They became permanent residents of <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a>, and Neville was left to be raised by his grandmother, <a href="/wiki/Augusta_Longbottom" title="Augusta Longbottom">Augusta Longbottom</a>. During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, Neville openly defied Voldemort and was tortured. However, he survived, and destroyed Voldemort's last remaining <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> when he beheaded <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a> using the <a href="/wiki/Sword_of_Gryffindor" title="Sword of Gryffindor">Sword of Gryffindor</a>.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor "Mad-Eye" Moody</a> was a highly skilled <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> and active member of the Order who fought against Voldemort during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. After Voldemort's first downfall in 1981, Moody was responsible for rounding up a number of Death Eaters, such as <a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a>, and killing several others, like <a href="/wiki/Evan_Rosier" title="Evan Rosier">Evan Rosier</a>. In <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, Voldemort ordered <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a> to kidnap Moody and imprison him in his own <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody%27s_trunk" class="mw-redirect" title="Alastor Moody&#39;s trunk">trunk</a>. For the next nine months, Crouch used Moody's hair to brew the <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> that would allow him to take Moody's place as temporary professor of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>. In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, Crouch used his position at Hogwarts to make sure <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> was transported to the <a href="/wiki/Little_Hangleton_graveyard" title="Little Hangleton graveyard">Little Hangleton graveyard</a>, where <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a> used Harry's blood in a <a href="/wiki/Regeneration_potion" title="Regeneration potion">potion</a> that allowed Voldemort to be restored to his body. When Voldemort failed to kill Harry in the graveyard and Harry returned to Hogwarts, Barty Crouch Jnr attempted to murder him personally. Dumbledore, <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> rescued Harry, after which Crouch was exposed, and Moody was freed. After Dumbledore's death in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Moody took charge of the Order of the Phoenix, until he was murdered by Voldemort during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>. Notably Voldemort seemed to acknowledge Moody's skills as a wizard as he targeted him personally as the most likely person to be guarding the real Harry.
</p><p>Nearly all of the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a> were active within the Order of the Phoenix. They fought against Voldemort during both the First and Second Wizarding wars. They lost family members such as <a href="/wiki/Fabian_Prewett" title="Fabian Prewett">Fabian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gideon_Prewett" title="Gideon Prewett">Gideon Prewett</a>, who were brothers of <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred Weasley</a>, who was killed in the Battle of Hogwarts. Voldemort had previously tried to manipulate <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, in an attempt to return to physical form, through one of his <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s Diary">Horcruxes</a>. Voldemort was furious when Molly defeated Bellatrix, and would have killed her, had Harry not intervened. Most of the Weasley family watched the final duel between Voldemort and Harry, and were witnesses to Voldemort's death.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Dorcas_Meadowes" title="Dorcas Meadowes">Dorcas Meadowes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Caradoc_Dearborn" title="Caradoc Dearborn">Caradoc Dearborn</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Bones_family" title="Bones family">Bones family</a>, the <a href="/wiki/McKinnon_family" title="McKinnon family">McKinnon family</a>, <a href="/wiki/Benjy_Fenwick" title="Benjy Fenwick">Benjy Fenwick</a> and <a href="/wiki/Emmeline_Vance" title="Emmeline Vance">Emmeline Vance</a> were all Order members killed either by Voldemort himself or by his <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First</a> and <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding Wars</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=68" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Etymology"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lord_Voldemort">Lord Voldemort</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=69" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Although <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> has never quite explained the origins of the name "Voldemort", there are some possible theories. "Mors", or "mortum" is the Latin word for death (which has evolved in many Romance languages as "<i>muerte</i>" or "<i>morte</i>", and the English word "murder" indeed has its origins in the same root word as "mors"). Therefore, while not necessarily true, the possible meaning of the word "Voldemort" may be either "representative of death" or "ambassador of death". Yet, the most accurate etymology of Voldemort would be the French sentence "Vol de mort" which literally means "flight of death" (accurate considering the murder sprees he committed and <a href="/wiki/Unsupported_flight" title="Unsupported flight">his invention of a spell to achieve unsupported flight</a>). It is quite plausible that is the real etymology of his name as J.K. Rowling herself speaks French and had taught it once. "Vol de mort" can also literally means "Theft of death" in French which can also be accurate since Lord Voldemort's search for immortality (which would mean he would have to steal his life from death). The Catalan expression "vol de mort", also means "flight of death" or, since "Vol" may also be from the Latin root "volo" ("I will, wish, want"), may mean "death wish".</li>
<li>J. K. Rowling has said in an interview that the T in Voldemort is silent.<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> This may be to the fact that the French word <b>mort,</b> meaning death, has a silent T. The silent T was maintained in the earlier editions of the audio book releases of the novels, but was discontinued in those releases following the release of the films, in which the T was used out loud. In 2015, Rowling again confirmed in an interview that her preferred pronunciation of the name was with a silent "T," though she noted "...but I'm pretty sure I'm the only person who pronounces it that way."<sup id="cite_ref-twittersilent_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-twittersilent-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tom_Marvolo_Riddle">Tom Marvolo Riddle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=70" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Tom Marvolo Riddle">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Tom Marvolo Riddle"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><b>Tom</b> is <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/diminutive" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:diminutive">diminutive</a> of Thomas Θωμᾶς, loaned from Aramaic תאומא taʔuma, meaning "twin"; cognate with Hebrew תאום  təʔōm.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> This choice can be explained by the fact that, to gain immortality, Tom Riddle divided, twinned in a way, his soul into different pieces so as to survive. Also, τόμος (tomos) is Ancient Greek for "slice" or "piece", which could link his name to the Horcruxes. A further evidence for that connection is Rowling's comparison of the making of a Horcrux to the splitting of the atom in terms of significance. The word "atom" derives from the same Ancient Greek word with an added negative prefix, ἄτομος ‎(átomos), meaning inseparable.</li>
<li>His maternal grandfather's name <b>Marvolo </b>suggests <i>marvelous</i>, from Latin <i>mirabilis</i>: consisting of from <i>mirari</i> "to wonder at", from root adjective <i>mirus</i> "wonderful" and suffix <i>-bilis</i>, denoting capacity. The name also contains the Latin root <i>volo</i> meaning "I wish, want, will, ordain, suppose, maintain that, be willing, to mean, signify, or denote." Another homophone, <i>volo</i> also means "I fly, speed, or move rapidly." Marvolo Gaunt &amp; his grandson Tom can be seen as characters who want to achieve greatness very quickly. It could also derive from Shakespeare's Twelfth Night character Malvolio (a punningly humorous name meaning roughly "I wish wickedly" or simply "ill-willing"). He is a Puritan who could not have fun and sought to stop the other servants from enjoying themselves. He is "sick with self love" and dreams of gaining domination. He thinks he is better than the others because he believes he is "pure." He is constantly the subject of practical jokes. The quote "Some are born great, some achieve greatness, and some have greatness thrust upon them" comes from here. At the end of the play, he swears revenge on the lot of them.</li>
<li>A <b>riddle</b> is "a form of word puzzle designed to test someone's ingenuity in arriving at its solution." Riddles were used as a way to both puzzle the audience and teach them to understand poetic language. Due to Voldemort's past being "a riddle" until the trio discover he was T. M. Riddle in the second book, it is only logical that he would be named that; moreover, <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> reportedly once saw the grave of one "Tom Riddell", which is probably the origin of the name. Voldemort created his name from arranging the letters of his full birth name, known as an anagram, another type of puzzle.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Behind_the_scenes">Behind the scenes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=71" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
