<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 202px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/RichardBremmerVoldemortMakeUp.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140129194957" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="200" height="189" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="RichardBremmerVoldemortMakeUp.jpg" data-image-key="RichardBremmerVoldemortMakeUp.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/RichardBremmerVoldemortMakeUp.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20140129194957" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/RichardBremmerVoldemortMakeUp.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140129194957" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/RichardBremmerVoldemortMakeUp.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20140129194957" decoding="async" width="200" height="189" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="RichardBremmerVoldemortMakeUp.jpg" data-image-key="RichardBremmerVoldemortMakeUp.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/RichardBremmerVoldemortMakeUp.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20140129194957" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:RichardBremmerVoldemortMakeUp.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Richard Bremmer (right) going through makeup for the scene where Voldemort's face is revealed</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In the films Voldemort is played by <a href="/wiki/Ralph_Fiennes" title="Ralph Fiennes">Ralph Fiennes</a>, who was born in 1962. Given Voldemort's real age, and the strenuous duties of the role, it is obvious why Voldemort is cast younger (he is said to be in his seventies at the time of his death). Fiennes' casting, however, makes the screen Voldemort look younger than three of the four Marauders (Sirius, James and Pettigrew), Snape, McGonagall, Molly and Arthur Weasley and Hagrid, characters who are younger than him in the books.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Richard_Bremmer" title="Richard Bremmer">Richard Bremmer</a> portrayed Voldemort in the flashback scene depicting the murder of Lily and James Potter in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>. His face (gone through prosthetic makeup and altered with visual effects) was also used for the scene in which Voldemort's face is finally revealed, though <a href="/wiki/Ian_Hart" title="Ian Hart">Ian Hart</a> (who also played <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Professor Quirrell</a>) voiced it instead of Bremmer. Bremmer himself is briefly heard in the fourth film, voicing Voldemort before his resurrection. Archive footage of Richard Bremmer appears in the final film during the <i>Prince's Tale</i> scene, although upon close-up on his face, he is played by Ralph Fiennes.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a4/FullRiddle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070812142742" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="FullRiddle.jpg" data-image-key="FullRiddle.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a4/FullRiddle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070812142742" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a4/FullRiddle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070812142742" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a4/FullRiddle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070812142742" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="FullRiddle.jpg" data-image-key="FullRiddle.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a4/FullRiddle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070812142742" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:FullRiddle.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Christian Coulson as Tom Riddle</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets</a></i> Voldemort is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Christian_Coulson" title="Christian Coulson">Christian Coulson</a>. In the <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)</a></i>, Tom is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Frank_Dillane" title="Frank Dillane">Frank Dillane</a> as a 16-year-old and also <a href="/wiki/Hero_Fiennes-Tiffin" title="Hero Fiennes-Tiffin">Hero Fiennes-Tiffin</a> as 11-year-old Tom Riddle. The latter is Ralph Fiennes' nephew.</li>
<li>He is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Akira_Ishida" title="Akira Ishida">Akira Ishida</a> in the Japanese dub of the second video game.</li>
<li>In the Flemish dub of the films, Voldemort is voiced by actor Dirk Denoyelle, who also voices Hagrid and Sirius Black. The actor claims he got the part because no other actor was willing to talk in a whispery voice during the dubbing of the first film. Though since film four, the actor has been using his normal speaking voice when doing Voldemort.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Although Harry Potter only realises he's one of Voldemort's Horcruxes in the final book, Dumbledore tells him that Voldemort put a bit of himself in Harry in the end of the second book.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/VoldemortPortraitWU.png/revision/latest?cb=20190704012314" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="250" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="VoldemortPortraitWU.png" data-image-key="VoldemortPortraitWU.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/VoldemortPortraitWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190704012314" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/VoldemortPortraitWU.png/revision/latest?cb=20190704012314" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/VoldemortPortraitWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190704012314" decoding="async" width="180" height="250" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="VoldemortPortraitWU.png" data-image-key="VoldemortPortraitWU.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/VoldemortPortraitWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190704012314" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:VoldemortPortraitWU.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A <a href="/wiki/Portrait" title="Portrait">Portrait</a> of Voldemort, as seen on <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Wizards_Unite" title="Harry Potter: Wizards Unite">Harry Potter: Wizards Unite</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/TomRiddleWU.png/revision/latest?cb=20190817191810" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="417" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="TomRiddleWU.png" data-image-key="TomRiddleWU.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/TomRiddleWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190817191810" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/TomRiddleWU.png/revision/latest?cb=20190817191810" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/TomRiddleWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190817191810" decoding="async" width="180" height="417" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="TomRiddleWU.png" data-image-key="TomRiddleWU.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/TomRiddleWU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190817191810" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:TomRiddleWU.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Tom Riddle as he appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Wizards_Unite" title="Harry Potter: Wizards Unite">Harry Potter: Wizards Unite</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>When Voldemort is seen drinking the <a href="/wiki/Unicorn_blood" title="Unicorn blood">Unicorn blood</a>, he is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Theo_Kypri" title="Theo Kypri">Theo Kypri</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_1-4" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4</a></i> Voldemort is the default <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a> form for most individuals in the game, whose Boggart is not described in canon, with a few exceptions. Upon the Voldemort boggart being repelled with the <a href="/wiki/Boggart-Banishing_Spell" title="Boggart-Banishing Spell">Boggart-Banishing Spell</a>, the Voldemort boggart will suck on an infant's dummy. Interestingly enough also in this game, despite Voldemort's Boggart being his own corpse canonically, in this game his Boggart will assume the form of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, as his greatest fear. Upon repelling his Harry boggart, Harry will fall down and die. This was likely due to his canonical boggart form being too disturbing for a children's video game, the same with both <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a>, who also have boggarts in the shapes of corpses (coincidentally, both are given Voldemort Boggart forms instead).<sup id="cite_ref-legohp14_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-legohp14-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In the <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(book_series)" title="Harry Potter (book series)">Harry Potter</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)">films</a>, the handle of Voldemort's wand resembles a bone.</li>
<li>In the city of Edinburgh, UK, near the Elephant Café where Rowling is said to have written some of <i>Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</i>, there is a famous cemetery named Greyfriar's Kirkyard. One of the headstones for those buried outside the walls of the graveyard (due to being suicides or enemies of the church) bears the name Tom Riddell. Rowling has stated that she often walked in the Kirkyard, so this may be a possible origin of the name.</li>
<li>In the film adaptation, Voldemort is shown to have very apparent veins on the top and back of his bald skull. Due to the veins' pattern, this was misinterpreted by some viewers who took it to be a scale-like motif and one of the features of Voldemort that had begun to resemble a snake after he began creating his Horcruxes.</li>
<li>In French, Vol de Mort can mean "flight from death", which reflects his obsession with immortality. It can also mean "Theft of Death", which is reminescent of the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>' name.</li>
<li>Although J.K. Rowling states that Voldemort is pronounced without the "t"<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> in the books, the first character to say the name in the series is Hagrid, whose dialogue is often spelled phonetically (e.g. <i>"go boil <b>yer</b> heads, both of <b>yeh</b>"</i>),<sup id="cite_ref-PS4_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS4-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> and the "t" is printed when he says it as well. The letter <i>is</i> also pronounced in the film versions. During a reading of one of her books, Rowling herself  pronounced Voldermort with a "t"<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> (but did not at another.)<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets</a></i>, Voldemort said that his father abandoned his mother when he found out that she was a witch, when he really left after Merope stopped giving him <a href="/wiki/Love_potion" title="Love potion">love potion</a>. Of course, this may have been how <i>he</i> saw the events, an attempt to twist them to justify his hatred of Muggles or simply his best guess as he might not have realised Merope used the potion. It could be possible that if not before, then possibly after Merope stopped giving her husband the potion, that her being a witch was stated and proven. Based on the words he speaks to Harry in the Little Hangleton graveyard, he indicates his father was anti-magic "he didn't like magic, my father", which could have been revealed during a possible conversation between father and son when the young Voldemort confronted his muggle father and grandparents.</li>
<li>In 2001, <a href="/wiki/Christian_Coulson" title="Christian Coulson">Christian Coulson</a> was cast as Tom Riddle in <i>Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets</i>, even though he exceeded the age group <a href="/wiki/Chris_Columbus" title="Chris Columbus">Chris Columbus</a> had set for auditions. When Coulson later expressed interest in returning for <i>Half-Blood Prince</i>, <a href="/wiki/David_Yates" title="David Yates">David Yates</a> felt Coulson was "too old" to play the role again. <a href="/wiki/Frank_Dillane" title="Frank Dillane">Frank Dillane</a> was eventually cast in Coulson's place. Archive footage of Coulson as Tom Riddle was used in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>, Tom Riddle was played by <a href="/wiki/Hero_Fiennes-Tiffin" title="Hero Fiennes-Tiffin">Hero Fiennes-Tiffin</a> at age eleven and <a href="/wiki/Frank_Dillane" title="Frank Dillane">Frank Dillane</a> at age sixteen. <a href="/wiki/Michael_Berendt" title="Michael Berendt">Michael Berendt</a> was also cast to portray Tom at age eighteen, but his scenes were cut from the final version of the film.<sup id="cite_ref-Michael_Berendt.27s_website_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Michael_Berendt.27s_website-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>When Warner Brothers was casting the role for the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire</a></i>, rumours circulated that both Rowan Atkinson and John Malkovich were considered. Both rumours were proven to be false.</li>
<li>In the Danish version of the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, voiced by <a href="/wiki/Nis_Bank-Mikkelsen" title="Nis Bank-Mikkelsen">Nis Bank-Mikkelsen</a>, calls Voldemort Tom instead of Romeo, which is his Danish name. The writers behind the Danish script made a mistake.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/Voldemort_destroys_the_Shield_from_Hogwarts_-_Deathly_Hallows_Part_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120812101221" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort destroys the Shield from Hogwarts - Deathly Hallows Part 2.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort_destroys_the_Shield_from_Hogwarts_-_Deathly_Hallows_Part_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/Voldemort_destroys_the_Shield_from_Hogwarts_-_Deathly_Hallows_Part_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120812101221" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/Voldemort_destroys_the_Shield_from_Hogwarts_-_Deathly_Hallows_Part_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120812101221" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/Voldemort_destroys_the_Shield_from_Hogwarts_-_Deathly_Hallows_Part_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120812101221" decoding="async" width="180" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort destroys the Shield from Hogwarts - Deathly Hallows Part 2.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort_destroys_the_Shield_from_Hogwarts_-_Deathly_Hallows_Part_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/Voldemort_destroys_the_Shield_from_Hogwarts_-_Deathly_Hallows_Part_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120812101221" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort_destroys_the_Shield_from_Hogwarts_-_Deathly_Hallows_Part_2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ralph Fiennes as Voldemort on set</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In the first film, Voldemort's eyes are shown to be red, as it is stated in the books. However, in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)</a></i> and subsequent film adaptations, Voldemort has light blue eyes, so that they would "show more emotion" than if they were red. Also, young Riddle has dark eyes (as described in the books) in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)</a></i> but light blue eyes in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)</a></i>. Interestingly, Harry's eyes were also changed from their much-emphasised colour in the books to Daniel Radcliffe's natural light blue.</li>
<li>Voldemort's character draws certain parallels to Adolf Hitler: Hitler claimed that the "Aryan" (blond haired, blue eyed Germans) race was the superior of all races and wanted to purify the human race of "non-Aryan" races even though he himself was neither a native German citizen nor representative of the "ideal Aryan" or "Nordic" as presented in the National Socialist world view. Voldemort preached a philosophy of pure-blood superiority despite the fact that he was a half-blood.</li>
<li>When BBC Newsbeat published an article titled "Why people are calling American businessman Donald Trump Voldemort" due to his suggestion that all Muslims should be banned from entering the United States of America, J.K. Rowling Tweeted that Voldemort was "nowhere near as bad."<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>J. K. Rowling explained that Voldemort went after Harry instead of Neville because he identified with the half-blood boy and therefore decided he must be the greater risk.<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceB_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceB-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Riddle was sixteen when he opened the Chamber of Secrets fifty years before the events of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets</a></i>, making him sixty-six in that book/film. Doing the maths, in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i>, during his final duel with Harry, he is seventy-one, which is the reverse of seventeen, Harry's age at the time (another possible representation of them being the antithesis of each other). Though his original body "died" at the age of fifty-four when he tried to murder Harry Potter as an infant. Presumably, his resurrection in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire</a></i> gave him a new fifty-four year old body. His soul, however, tortured and distorted it finally became, would be seventy-one. Otherwise, if he was totally newborn, he would have been three years old when he was finally defeated.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)</a></i>, he is shown with a forked, <a href="/wiki/Snake" title="Snake">snake</a>-like tongue, but in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)</a></i>, his tongue is normal.</li>
<li>Voldemort is described in the books as having cat-like slits for eyes, which is changed in the film. However, after he emerges from the cauldron in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire</a></i>, the slits can be briefly seen.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 177px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/01/Grandpre_Dueling_Wizards.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180914065858" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="175" height="135" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Grandpre Dueling Wizards.jpg" data-image-key="Grandpre_Dueling_Wizards.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/01/Grandpre_Dueling_Wizards.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20180914065858" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/01/Grandpre_Dueling_Wizards.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180914065858" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/01/Grandpre_Dueling_Wizards.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20180914065858" decoding="async" width="175" height="135" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Grandpre Dueling Wizards.jpg" data-image-key="Grandpre_Dueling_Wizards.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/01/Grandpre_Dueling_Wizards.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20180914065858" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Grandpre_Dueling_Wizards.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore vs. Voldemort in the Ministry's atrium</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 177px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/Battle_voldyreturn1.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20100119171110" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="175" height="133" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Battle voldyreturn1.PNG" data-image-key="Battle_voldyreturn1.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/Battle_voldyreturn1.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20100119171110" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/Battle_voldyreturn1.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20100119171110" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/Battle_voldyreturn1.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20100119171110" decoding="async" width="175" height="133" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Battle voldyreturn1.PNG" data-image-key="Battle_voldyreturn1.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/Battle_voldyreturn1.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20100119171110" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Battle_voldyreturn1.PNG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Duel in the Graveyard</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Mary GrandPré's illustrations for the American translation of Harry Potter describes him with a <b>green</b> skin, rather than the pale skin described in the books, and also with many alien/reptilian-like attributes.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> has said that it is of important symbolic significance that Voldemort, incapable of love himself, was conceived in an act of coercion, rather than genuine <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>When asked if Voldemort would affect the <a href="/wiki/United_States_of_America" title="United States of America">American</a> wizarding community, <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> said he affected everyone but his plan was <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">European</a> domination first.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In Fantastic Beasts interview Rowling says that even though fans had a sense that Voldemort was a threat to the whole wizarding world, fans never saw how he was affecting people in the rest of the world.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> revealed that after his death, Voldemort had to exist in the <a href="/wiki/Limbo" title="Limbo">Limbo</a> Harry talked to Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Soul" title="Soul">soul</a> in, as the crouched human childlike form, and was therefore unable to return as a <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">ghost</a>.</li>
<li>In the film adaptations, despite characters still calling him "He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named", "You-Know-Who", or (in the case of Death Eaters) "The Dark Lord", more characters call him by his name than in the book. Hermione first says the name in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, as opposed to <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Wormtail</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a> both say the name in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire</a> </i>(the first time that they conversed with him), and in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a> says the name, despite telling Harry not to say it in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>. It could be argued (in the film story) that Mr Weasley had become less afraid of Voldemort (while still regarding him as a major threat), enough to speak his name.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)</a></i>, when showing Harry the memory of when he first met Voldemort, the memory vials are labelled "<b>Thomas Marvolo Riddle</b>".</li>
<li>J.K. Rowling said that had <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> died and Tom Riddle escaped the diary, Voldemort would have become stronger.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 177px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Untitled147.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120221215508" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="175" height="194" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Untitled147.jpg" data-image-key="Untitled147.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Untitled147.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20120221215508" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Untitled147.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120221215508" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Untitled147.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20120221215508" decoding="async" width="175" height="194" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Untitled147.jpg" data-image-key="Untitled147.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ae/Untitled147.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20120221215508" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Untitled147.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort casts his final spell in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>J.K. Rowling has described Voldemort as the most evil dark wizard for hundreds and hundreds of years,<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> a self-hating bully,<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> a raging psychopath devoid of empathy,<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> a power-hungry racist,<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> someone who prefers for his henchmen to do his dirty work for him,<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceB_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceB-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> and that if psychologists were to get Voldemort in a room, pin him down, and take his wand away, he would be classified as a psychopath.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>A psychotherapist also speculated that Voldemort may have possessed Antisocial Personality Disorder and/or Narcissistic Personality Disorder, or perhaps even the childhood specific disorder called Reactive Attachment Disorder, of which the former two diagnoses originate from.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li>J.K. Rowling revealed that the inspiration for people referring to Voldemort as <em>He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named</em> came from the Kray twins who terrorised London and how she though it was an impressive demonstration of strength, that you can convince someone not to use your name. Impressive in the sense that demonstrates how deep the level of fear is that you can inspire. It's not something to be admired.<sup id="cite_ref-accio-quote.org_36-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-accio-quote.org-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Aside from his  <i><a href="/wiki/Pottermore" title="Pottermore">Pottermore</a></i> page, Voldemort is referred to as the "greatest dark wizard of all time" in Book 2,<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> and as the "most powerful dark wizard for a century" in Book 4, Chapter 2.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> While in Book 3,  he is described as the "most feared dark wizard for a hundred years."<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Voldemort is officially played by a total of seven actors: <a href="/wiki/Ralph_Fiennes" title="Ralph Fiennes">Ralph Fiennes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ian_Hart" title="Ian Hart">Ian Hart</a>, <a href="/wiki/Richard_Bremmer" title="Richard Bremmer">Richard Bremmer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Christian_Coulson" title="Christian Coulson">Christian Coulson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hero_Fiennes-Tiffin" title="Hero Fiennes-Tiffin">Hero Fiennes-Tiffin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Frank_Dillane" title="Frank Dillane">Frank Dillane</a> and <a href="/wiki/Michael_Berendt" title="Michael Berendt">Michael Berendt</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Michael_Berendt.27s_website_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Michael_Berendt.27s_website-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> although his scenes were cut. This makes him the character to be played by the most actors in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_films" class="mw-redirect" title="Harry Potter films"><i>Harry Potter</i> film series</a>. Whether intentional or not, this also rings true for Voldemort's fascination (and J.K Rowling's utilisation of it in the series) with the number seven.</li>
<li>A detailed replica of a Voldemort doll is sold at <a href="/wiki/The_Wizarding_World_of_Harry_Potter" title="The Wizarding World of Harry Potter">The Wizarding World of Harry Potter</a>.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_1-4" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4</a></i>, before Voldemort is revived, he is in a baby carriage sucking on a pacifier. Also, for the ritual, Harry's glasses are taken instead of his blood.</li></ul>

<ul><li>In the novel of <i>Deathly Hallows</i>, Harry and Voldemort duel in the Great Hall. In the film of <i>Deathly Hallows</i>, Voldemort and Harry battle in the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Staircase" title="Grand Staircase">Grand Staircase</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Catwalks_by_the_Quad_battlements" title="Catwalks by the Quad battlements">catwalks by the Quad battlements</a>, before Harry grabs Voldemort and they fall from a ledge. They Apparate together around the castle before landing at the <a href="/wiki/Viaduct_Courtyard" title="Viaduct Courtyard">Entrance Courtyard</a>, where they finish their duel.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Voldemorts_Death.gif/revision/latest?cb=20111116144244" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="188" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemorts Death.gif" data-image-key="Voldemorts_Death.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Voldemorts_Death.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111116144244" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Voldemorts_Death.gif/revision/latest?cb=20111116144244" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Voldemorts_Death.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111116144244" decoding="async" width="250" height="188" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemorts Death.gif" data-image-key="Voldemorts_Death.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Voldemorts_Death.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111116144244" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemorts_Death.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Voldemort disintegrating into ashes in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In the book, Voldemort's final words are "<i>Avada Kedavra!</i>" In the film, since his Killing Curses during the final battle are nonverbal, the last thing he says is "<i>I killed Snape!</i>", when Harry was confronting him about the Elder Wand. However, the game re-adds his last line from the book.</li>
<li>In the film adaptation, Voldemort disintegrates when he is defeated, while in the novel, he just falls to the ground.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Harry_duels_Voldemort_in_the_Hogwarts.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190324225142" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry duels Voldemort in the Hogwarts.gif" data-image-key="Harry_duels_Voldemort_in_the_Hogwarts.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Harry_duels_Voldemort_in_the_Hogwarts.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190324225142" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Harry_duels_Voldemort_in_the_Hogwarts.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190324225142" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Harry_duels_Voldemort_in_the_Hogwarts.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190324225142" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry duels Voldemort in the Hogwarts.gif" data-image-key="Harry_duels_Voldemort_in_the_Hogwarts.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Harry_duels_Voldemort_in_the_Hogwarts.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190324225142" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_duels_Voldemort_in_the_Hogwarts.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Final duel between Voldemort and Harry Potter in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In the book, it only says that Voldemort's curse rebounded on him and that the Elder Wand flew from his hand to Harry's. In the film, Voldemort dies when his Killing Curse begins filling in the fissures of the Elder Wand, and then his arms begins to turn black, causing him to disintegrate into ashes as he dies. It was, however, intended to be similar to the original book, and was also included in late stages of development, although it was changed to the depiction in the final version after the events of Osama bin Laden's death.
<ul><li>This also fits well the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters#Behind_the_scenes" title="Death Eaters">spectre-like attributes that Death Eaters were given in the films</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Tom Riddle is the only named Slytherin <a href="/wiki/Head_Boy_or_Girl" title="Head Boy or Girl">Head Boy</a>.</li>
<li>A 100-foot tall representation of Voldemort was included as part of the opening ceremonies of the 2012 Summer Olympics in London, during a presentation celebrating English children's literature. He was presented as leading fellow villains the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Child_Catcher" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Child Catcher">Child Catcher</a>, the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Queen_of_Hearts_(Alice%27s_Adventures_in_Wonderland)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Queen of Hearts (Alice&#39;s Adventures in Wonderland)">Queen of Hearts</a>, <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cruella_de_Vil" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Cruella de Vil">Cruella de Vil</a>, and <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Captain_Hook" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Captain Hook">Captain Hook</a>, before being defeated by an army of <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mary_Poppins_(character)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mary Poppins (character)">Mary Poppins</a>.</li>
<li>Oddly enough, despite his obsession with <a href="/wiki/Immortality" title="Immortality">immortality</a> and use of <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a> to achieve it, Voldemort died having lived an average <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> lifespan of 71 years old.</li>
<li>In the books, Voldemort's voice is frequently described as being cold and high, but Fiennes uses an occasionally deep voice, particularly when Voldemort is yelling or casting curses.</li>
<li>Voldemort had been rejected twice when applying for the job as teacher of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>. However, Voldemort shared the body of <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a>, who was from that time a teacher of Defence Against the Dark Arts for a year.
<ul><li>It is remarked in the story that the turban Quirrel wears smells foul, and most presume it is to protect him from a vampire he encountered in the Black Forrest. It is latter revealed that Voldemort was possessing Quirrell, and the smell was possibly owing to him.</li>
<li>Ironically Quirrell's story about a vampire is in some respect true, as Voldemort at the time was in a state between life and death, and himself admits that he is living parasitically off of the weaker man. This even includes making Quirrell drink the blood of <a href="/wiki/Unicorn" title="Unicorn">unicorns</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Ralph Fiennes' favourite line in the series is "I can touch you now" from <i>Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>His birth year, 1926, is a year of the Tiger on the Chinese Zodiac sign. He possesses qualities that are often associated with those born under this sign: independence, bravery, ambition, an aggressive attitude, a tendency to be over-confident at times, a short temper, and the ability to charm and seduce others.</li>
<li>In the practice of numerology, his date of birth gives him the number seven as his "life path number". He once mentioned to Horace Slughorn that seven is the most magical number. His personality includes traits that those with this life number are said to have: being aloof, preferring independence, lacking concern for others, and intimidating others.</li>
<li>Curiously, Riddle began studying at Hogwarts in 1938, one year before World War II struck, and graduated in 1945, the year the war ended and the same year Dumbledore gained mastery of the Elder Wand after defeating Grindelwald.</li>
<li>In an interview with the <i>Fantastic Beasts</i> cast, <a href="/wiki/Zo%C3%AB_Kravitz" title="Zoë Kravitz">Zoe Kravitz</a> says she believes, if Voldemort and Grindelwald got into a magical duel, that Voldemort would win. However, <a href="/wiki/Callum_Turner" title="Callum Turner">Callum Turner</a> was unsure and stated "But, Harry took him down".<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>When asked by a fan if Voldemort liked cake Rowling say she doesn't see him as a great cake lover and that she suspects he reached a point of inhumanity where he didn't actually need food.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In the German version, the only canon source that pronounces Voldemort's name canonically (with a silent t) is the first audiobook version read by Rufus Beck. The second audiobook version read by Felix von Manteuffel, as well as all films and video games, pronounce it with a hearable t.</li>
<li>Ironically, Voldemort's name would later be used for <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Voldemort_(distributed_data_store)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Voldemort (distributed data store)">a distributed data storage system</a> that was for key-values, similar to Voldemort and his Horcruxes.</li>
<li>Despite dying at the age of 71, it is likely that he was biologically younger, given that he was left without a body for 13 years, and received a new body in 1995, when he would have been 68. He was 54 two months from 55. So if this is true he would have been roughly 57.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/The_LEGO_Batman_Movie" title="The LEGO Batman Movie">The LEGO Batman Movie</a></i>, Voldemort appears as one of the many villains trapped in the Phantom Zone. Curiously, he is not voiced by <a href="/wiki/Ralph_Fiennes" title="Ralph Fiennes">Ralph Fiennes</a>, even though another major character in the film (Alfred Pennyworth) is; instead he is voiced by <a href="/wiki/Eddie_Izzard" title="Eddie Izzard">Eddie Izzard</a>.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Similarities_to_real-life">Similarities to real-life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?veaction=edit&amp;section=72" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Similarities to real-life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle?action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: Similarities to real-life"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Voldemort's character draws certain parallels to three real-life dictators; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a>, <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Stalin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joseph Stalin">Joseph Stalin</a>, and <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Benito_Mussolini" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Benito Mussolini">Benito Mussolini</a>. However, J.K. Rowling uses Hitler as the bigger influence for Voldemort.
</p>
<ul><li>Adolf Hitler:
<ul><li>Hitler promoted Aryan supremacy, claiming that blond haired and blue eyed Germans were superior to all races and wanted to purify the human race of "non-Aryan" races even though he himself was neither a native German citizen nor representative of the "ideal Aryan" or "Nordic" as presented in the National Socialist world view but an Austrian. Voldemort preached a similar philosophy of racial superiority, focusing on pureblood supremacy despite the fact that he was a half-blood.</li></ul></li></ul>
<ul><li><ul><li>Both men were power-hungry.</li>
<li>Hitler blamed the Jews for taking Germany's income. In a similar way, Voldemort blamed Muggle-borns for stealing magic.</li>
<li>Similarities of their death are evident; Hitler committed suicide to escape from the Allies while Voldemort’s killing curse rebounds because the Elder Wand’s allegiance didn’t lie with him. Both men killed themselves, though Voldemort's case was clearly unplanned.
<ul><li>That said, Hitler did have one noticeable difference from Voldemort: Voldemort was afraid of death, to the extent that his boggart would have been his own corpse, while Hitler, even before his demise, had suicidal tendencies, even deeply considering suicide after the failed Beer Hall Putsch while in hiding at Hanfstaengls,<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> and had threatened to commit suicide a few times whenever the Nazi Party lost during various elections, one time being when he and Strassler had a falling out and the latter resigned from the Nazi Party.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li>Prior to Voldemort and Hitler's reign, persecutions of both Muggle-born and Jews were evident. Salazar Slytherin (Voldemort's ancestor) upheld that Muggle-borns should not attend Hogwarts while early Christians had viewed Jews as people who must never live among them.</li>
<li>It is common sense to never say Hitler greetings. Similarly, it is inappropriate to say "Voldemort".</li></ul></li>
<li>Joseph Stalin:
<ul><li>Both men had feared names during their reign.
<ul><li>On a related note, both men also created their names largely because they hated their pasts.</li></ul></li>
<li>Both men also had unpleasant upbringings and started off in very modest circumstances (Voldemort was put into an orphanage by his dying mother with his father abandoning them largely thanks to the love potion wearing off, while Stalin, originally living in a Georgian village of what was then-known as the Russian Empire, was raised under an alcoholic and abusive father, and his mother shuffled him off to a monastery partly due to not wanting to deal with him.).</li></ul></li>
<li>Benito Mussolini:
<ul><li>Shared fascist ideology.</li>
<li>Both also formed gangs as young boys (Mussolini in particular went as far as to have his gang engage in violent raids throughout the countryside of Italy).</li></ul></li></ul>

<td>The <i>-volod</i> part of the name may be connected to the name "Volodimir", where "volod" equates to "ruler".
</td></tr></tbody></table>
